# Wiki Index

The catalog of all pages in this wiki. Each entry: a wikilink to the page and a one-line summary. The LLM reads this first when answering queries to identify candidate pages.

Keep summaries tight тАФ one line each. The index is engineered to be cheap to read; a fat index defeats its purpose.

When this file exceeds ~300 lines or the wiki passes ~150 pages, shard into `wiki/indexes/<type>.md` and replace this file with a directory of shards. See the `scaling-playbook.md` reference in the `llm-wiki` skill for the migration procedure.

---

- [[assembly-trim-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-TRIM-001 (quality trimming, BWA/cutadapt running-sum): cutadapt algorithm docs + BWA `bwa_trim_read`/`BWA_MIN_RDLEN` + Cock et al. 2010 sources; subtract-cutoff/argmin-partial-sum = BWA argmax, Phred+33 decode; `KI;<)(,%#$`@thr 10тЖТfirst 4 bases oracle; both-end-order + minLength-filter assumptions.
- [[assembly-trim-001-report]] тАФ validation report for ASSEMBLY-TRIM-001 (quality trimming, `SequenceAssembler.QualityTrimReads`/`TrimEnd`/`TrimStart`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[assembly-trim-001-evidence]]): Stage A тЬЕ PASS / Stage B тЭМ FAIL тЖТ ЁЯФз FIXED / State CLEAN, full suite 6535/0. **One real defect fully fixed** тАФ old `TrimEnd`/`TrimStart` took the *global-minimum* partial sum with **no `s < 0` early break** and chained the 5' pass onto the 3'-surviving window; ~19.5% of random reads diverged from cutadapt (`20,0,8,40`@10 kept only the last base vs all 4). Fix adds the `s<0` early break to both passes, runs each independently over the full read `[0,n)`, and adds the `startтЙеstop тЗТ (0,0)` drop rule; Python port vs cutadapt `quality_trim_index` = **0/900k mismatches**. Three new sourced tests (`5!)I`тЖТ`ACGT`, `##I##`тЖТ`G`, `5&&`тЖТdropped) each fail the old code. Pre-existing M1тАУM5/S1тАУS3 were all happy-path and shared the blind spot. Corrected the concept's stale "5'-pass-on-surviving-window" wording. Concept [[quality-trimming-running-sum]].

- [[chrom-aneu-001-report]] тАФ validation report for CHROM-ANEU-001 (aneuploidy detection, `ChromosomeAnalyzer.DetectAneuploidy` / `IdentifyWholeChromosomeAneuploidy`, `ChromosomeAnalyzer.cs:832тАУ917`, type `CopyNumberState`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[chrom-aneu-001-evidence]]): Stage A PASS / Stage B PASS / End state CLEAN, 31 passed 0 failed, build 0w/0e, zero code or test change. - [[compgen-rearr-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-REARR-001 (genome rearrangement detection by breakpoints, signed gene-order comparison; Comparative-genomics): Hunter Lecture 16 (HannenhalliтАУPevzner/BafnaтАУPevzner) + Tannier PMC3887456 + BafnaтАУPevzner 1998 sources; signed permutation `╬▒(i)=┬▒a`, extended `(0,тАж,n+1)`, breakpoint = pair where neither `(x,y)` nor `(тИТy,тИТx)` in ╬▓, `b(╬▒)` count + `d_BP=nтИТsim` + reversal lower bound `dтЙеb/2`; Inversion (sign-flip reversal) vs Transposition (orientation-preserving block move); Hunter `╬▒=(тИТ2,тИТ3,+1,+6,тИТ5,тИТ4)`тЖТb=6, identityтЖТ0, single-inversionтЖТ2 oracles; three scoping assumptions (orthologMap-supplied anchors, strand=sign, only Inversion/Transposition classified тАФ Translocation/indel/dup "Not implemented"); the signed-permutation alternative to block-signal [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]]; deviations None.
- [[compgen-reversal-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-REVERSAL-001 (Reversal/inversion distance as the breakpoint lower bound тМИb/2тМЙ; Comparative-genomics): NOT a new algorithm тАФ the UNSIGNED specialization of [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]'s reversal-distance bound (BafnaтАУPevzner 1998 + Hunter Lecture 16 + H├╝botter 2020 + BergeronтАУMixtackiтАУStoye 2009); `CalculateReversalDistance` counts unsigned breakpoints `|╬Ф|тЙа1` on the extended perm and returns `тМИb/2тМЙ=(b+1)/2`; [2,3,1,6,5,4]тЖТ2, [4,3,2,1]тЖТ1, identityтЖТ0 oracles; lower-bound-not-exact (no HP cycle/hurdle refinement); two assumptions (integer тМИb/2тМЙ rounding, unequal-lengthтЖТArgumentException); deviations None.

- [[protmotif-sp-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-SP-001 (signal-peptide cleavage-site prediction, `ProteinMotifFinder.PredictSignalPeptide`; ProteinMotif family): **redesign of the SAME method** тАФ **replaces** the fabricated tripartite n/h/c model of [[protmotif-domain-001-evidence|DOMAIN-001]] with the **von Heijne (1986) log-odds weight matrix** = EMBOSS 6.6.0 `sigcleave` (doc + `sigcleave.c` + `data/Esig.euk`/`Esig.pro`). Score = argmax over sites of `╬г ln(count/expect)` across positions тИТ13..+2 (natural log; zero counts тЖТ `1.0e-10` at conserved cols тИТ3/тИТ1, else `1.0`); cleavage between тИТ1/+1, `CleavagePosition` = 1-based mature start; `IsLikelySignalPeptide тЗФ Score тЙе 3.5` (`minWeight` default 3.5, ~95% sens/spec, cleavage 75тАУ80% correct); eukaryotic matrix (161 seqs) default, prokaryotic (36 seqs) via `prokaryote:true`. Worked oracle **ACH2_DROME (UniProt P17644)** тЖТ Score **13.739**, mature start **42**, window `LLVLLLLCETVQA` (re-derived exactly in Python). Corner cases: best site always reported (`minWeight` only flags likelihood); < 15-aa window тЖТ null; non-standard residues contribute 0; case-insensitive. One assumption (min length = 15-aa window); pitfalls log10-vs-ln and missing тИТ3/тИТ1 penalty. Enriches [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] (no new concept).

- [[protmotif-tm-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-TM-001 (Transmembrane helix prediction, Kyte-Doolittle hydropathy sliding window; ProteinMotif family, genuinely distinct hydrophobicity-based unit): slide a window of length **19** along the protein, score each window as the **arithmetic mean** of its per-residue Kyte-Doolittle (1982) hydropathy values, emit contiguous runs with window mean **> threshold 1.6** as membrane-spanning segments. One assumption = segment `End=lastPassingProfileIndex+windowSizeтИТ1` clamped (2026-06-16 off-by-one correction), no deviations; new concept [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]].

- [[pangen-heap-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit PANGEN-HEAP-001 (Pan-Genome Growth Model тАФ Heaps'-law fit of the new-gene curve; third PANGEN-* unit): micropan `heaps()` (rank 3, model `y=K┬╖x^(-alpha)`, count>0тЖТ1 binarization, first-appearance new-gene rule `(cm==1)[i]&(cm==0)[i-1]`, genome index starts at 2, n.perm=100, objective `J=sqrt(╬г(yтИТK┬╖x^(-alpha))┬▓)/|x|` over KтИИ[0,10000]/alphaтИИ[0,2], verbatim "alpha<1 open, alpha>1 closed") + Tettelin 2008 (power-law openness) + Tettelin 2005 (*S. agalactiae* anchor: 161/54 new genes, tg(╬╕)=33, тЙИ80% core, open) sources; exact oracles x=[2,3] y=[8,4]тЖТalpha ln2/ln(3/2)тЙИ1.7095 KтЙИ26.164 closed, constant y=[1,1]тЖТalpha 0 K 1 open; corner cases <2 genomes degenerate (no exception), binary presence only, alpha=1 boundary not-open; two assumptions (optimizer method non-correctness-affecting, fixed-seed permutation RNG); no contradictions. - [[quality-phred-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit QUALITY-PHRED-001 (Phred score handling тАФ parse/encode a FASTQ quality string + convert Phred+33 тЖФ Phred+64; QUALITY family): **Cock et al. 2010** *Nucleic Acids Research* 38(6):1767 (DOI 10.1093/nar/gkp1137, PMC2847217) тАФ the de-facto FASTQ spec: Phred `Q=тИТ10┬╖logтВБтВА(P)`, Sanger/**Phred+33** ASCII 33тАУ126тЖТQ0тАУ93 (`Q=ordтИТ33`), Illumina 1.3+/**Phred+64** ASCII 64тАУ126тЖТQ0тАУ62, Phred score **invariant** across variants so cross-variant conversion is a pure ┬▒31 re-offset (Solexa odds-ratio score out of scope, lossy); representability rules **Phred+64тЖТPhred+33 always safe** (Q0тАУ62 тКЖ 0тАУ93) vs **Phred+33тЖТPhred+64 overflows** for Q>62; oracles `!`/`5`/`?`/`I`/`~`тЖТ0/20/30/40/93, `@h~`тЖТ0/40/62, conversion `@h~`тЖТ`!I_` and `!I`тЖТ`@h`; must-test both-variant decode / round-trip identity / both-direction convert / out-of-range decode throws / Q>62 overflow throws / empty+null; two API-shape assumptions (malformed byte + overflow тЖТ `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`, range bounds source-backed); no contradictions. **No new concept** тАФ enriches shared [[phred-quality-encoding]] (adds the Cock et al. primary anchor + conversion representability rules) alongside sibling [[parse-fastq-001-evidence]].

Own concept [[fastq-quality-statistics]] (**depends on** [[phred-quality-encoding]]).
- [[rep-str-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit REP-STR-001 (Microsatellite / Short Tandem Repeat (STR) detection тАФ perfect default `FindMicrosatellites` **plus** the opt-in approximate/imperfect/interrupted `FindApproximateTandemRepeats` + `ComputeBernoulliStatistics`, Benson **Tandem Repeats Finder** 1999 model): Benson 1999 *Nucleic Acids Research* 27(2):573 (approximate-repeat definition, seven TRF statistics, wraparound-DP alignment, majority-rule consensus) + TRF definitions/desc pages (Bernoulli adjacent-copy model, PM matching / PI indel probability, defaults PM .80/PI .10) + TRF reference impl (recommended weights `(+2,тИТ7,тИТ7)`, Minscore 50) + Wikipedia Microsatellite (1тАУ6 bp unit, 5тАУ50 copies) sources; the opt-in approximate detector **closes the exact-copies-only gap** тАФ reports an interrupted tract as ONE repeat with percent-matches/percent-indels/score while the perfect detector fragments it; oracles `CAGCAGCAGTAGCAGCAG`тЖТperiod 3 `CAG`├Ч6 17match/1mismatch score 27 94.4%, single-base-deletion 29-bpтЖТscore 51 clears default gate, Bernoulli adjacent PM 13/15 distinct from consensus 17/18, `CACACATACACA`тЖТPM 0.80 on-threshold; three assumptions (deterministic exhaustive (start,period) scan vs TRF probabilistic k-tuple seeding тАФ the genome-scale residual; percentage denominator = total alignment columns; adjacent-copy segmentation for Bernoulli PM/PI, exact for substitution-only); no contradictions. **No new concept** тАФ enriches the repeats family anchor [[repetitive-element-detection]] (Approximate STR detection section).
- [[restr-filter-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RESTR-FILTER-001 (Restriction Enzyme Filtering тАФ the first RESTR-* / MolTools reagent-selection unit): filter the enzyme library by end type (`GetBluntCutters()` / `GetStickyCutters()`) and by recognition-site length (`GetEnzymesByCutLength(min, max)` + single-length overload). Sources: Wikipedia *Sticky and blunt ends* (blunt = both strands terminate in a base pair, sticky = 5'/3' overhang, **blunt & sticky are the only two categories тЖТ total, disjoint partition**, blunt-blunt always compatible) + Wikipedia *Restriction enzyme* (Type II undivided palindromes **4тАУ8 nt**; center cutтЖТblunt / staggeredтЖТsticky; EcoRI `G^AATTC` / SmaI `CCC^GGG` / KpnI `GGTAC^C` / PstI `CTGCA^G` examples) + Wikipedia *List of restriction enzyme cutting sites* (4/6/8-bp categories) + NEB/REBASE (KpnI 3' overhang, EcoRI 5' overhang) + PMC/REBASE (SfiI interrupted palindrome `GGCCNNNN^NGGCC`, 13 nt, outside 4тАУ8). Dataset oracle: SmaI/EcoRV/AluI/HaeIII blunt vs EcoRI(5')/KpnI(3')/PstI(3')/NotI/TaqI sticky + SfiI 13-nt interrupted. Contract: blunt тИк sticky = full library & disjoint; `[min,max]` **inclusive** (`6тЖТ6` all 6-cutters, `9тЖТ10` none, `[4,8]` whole undivided library **except** 13-nt SfiI); single-length overload agrees at `min==max`; `min>max`/negative/zero тЖТ empty. One API-shape assumption (inclusive range bounds; recognition-length values source-backed). No contradictions. New concept [[restriction-enzyme-filtering]].
- [[rna-dotbracket-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-DOTBRACKET-001 (Dot-Bracket / extended WUSS notation тАФ **parse & validate** a structure string; the notation/representation layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): `RnaSecondaryStructure.ParseDotBracket` (structure string тЖТ base pairs) + `ValidateDotBracket` (well-formedness). Sources: ViennaRNA *RNA Structure Notations* / *Dot-Bracket Notation* (rank 3 тАФ base pairs = matching `()`, unpaired = `.`; extended notation adds `<>`/`{}`/`[]` + uppercase/lowercase letter pairs; **families are not required to nest тЖТ pseudoknots**; uppercase = 5' opener / lowercase = 3' closer) + ViennaRNA WUSS / `vrna_db_from_WUSS()` + Infernal Nawrocki & Eddy 2013 (rank 3 тАФ **any matched pair = a base pair, symbol has no meaning if partners match**; flatten treats letter-pair pseudoknots as unpaired тЖТ each family an **independent pairing system**) + Rfam glossary (rank 5 тАФ `<>`/`()`/`[]`/`{}` all pair; non-bracket `-`/`,`/`:`/`.` all single-stranded). Algorithm: **one balanced-bracket stack per family** (shared stack would mis-pair `([)]`); a closer must match a same-family opener. Oracles тАФ parse `((((....))))`тЖТ(0,11),(1,10),(2,9),(3,8), `([)]`тЖТ`(`:(0,2)+`[`:(1,3), `<<<<[[[[....>>>>]]]]` / `((((AAAA....))))aaaa`тЖТtwo 4-bp crossing helices; validate `(((...)))`/`(([[]]))`/`([)]`тЖТ**true**, `(((...)` / `...)` / `)(` / `(]`тЖТ**false**. Two API-contract assumptions (malformed input тЖТ best-effort parse dropping unmatched closers, gate with `ValidateDotBracket`; empty/null тЖТ valid pair-free). No contradictions. New concept [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]].
- [[rna-energy-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-ENERGY-001 (**Free Energy Calculation**; the thermodynamic/energy layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateStackingEnergy`/`CalculateStemEnergy`/`CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy`/`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy`, the **Turner 2004 nearest-neighbor** free-energy terms summed into a fold's ╬ФG┬░ at 37 ┬░C. Sources: **NNDB (Nearest Neighbor Database) Turner04** (definitive parameter tables тАФ WC/GU stacking, hairpin `loop.txt`, terminal-mismatch, tri/tetra/hexaloop totals, hairpin bonuses/penalties) + Turner 2004 + Mathews 2004 (PNAS 101:7287) + Xia 1998 + SantaLucia 1998 + Heus & Pardi 1991; reference impls ViennaRNA / MFOLD / RNAstructure. Model `╬ФG┬░total = init + ╬гstacking + ╬гloops`. Key parameters тАФ WC stacking **all negative** (GC-rich most stable, `GC/CG` тИТ3.42, `GG/CC` тИТ3.26; `AA/UU` тИТ0.93); **G-U wobble variable, two positive** (`UG/GU` +0.30, `GU/UG` +1.29), note-a `GG/UU`=тИТ0.5, note-b `5'GGUC/3'CUGG` special 3-stack total тИТ4.12 (vs тИТ1.77); **hairpin-loop init positive & non-monotonic** (3тЖТ5.4, 4тЖТ5.6, 6тЖТ5.4, 9тЖТ6.4, Jacobson-Stockmayer beyond 9); special UNCG/GNRA tri/tetra/hexaloop total energies; all-C loop penalty (3-nt +1.5 / >3-nt 0.3n+1.6); terminal mismatch (96); +0.45 per AU/GU end. Oracles GC 3-bp stem тИТ5.78, NNDB hairpin example-1 `GGGAUAAAUCCC` тИТ3.42, GGUC/CUGG тИТ4.12; single base pair / empty / poly-A тЖТ **╬ФG┬░=0** (stacking needs тЙе2 adjacent pairs). No assumptions remain (all params = exact NNDB match); three **defined conditions** (37 ┬░C, 2-dp precision, unknown stacksтЖТ0.0). No contradictions. New concept [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]].
- [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-HAIRPIN-001 (**Hairpin Loop and Stem Free-Energy Calculation**, Turner 2004 NN model): a focused deep-dive on `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy` + `CalculateStemEnergy`, **not** a stem-loop enumerator and **not** miRNA-specific тАФ it enriches the energy-layer concept [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] (sibling of [[rna-energy-001-evidence]]) rather than defining a new one; distinct from the miRNA hairpin *finder* [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]. Source: **NNDB Turner 2004** hairpin pages (via Wayback) + **Mathews et al. 2004** PNAS 101:7287. Hairpin ╬ФG┬░ = init(n) + terminal mismatch + first-mismatch bonuses (UU/GA тИТ0.9, GG тИТ0.8) + special-GU-closure тИТ2.2 (**G-U only, not U-G** тАФ documented asymmetry) + all-C penalty (3-nt +1.5, >3-nt 0.3n+1.6); **3-nt loops get no first-mismatch term**; loops < 3 nt prohibited; special tri/tetra/hexaloop totals override the model (`CAACG` 6.8, `CCUCGG` 2.5). Stem = per-stack stacking + **+0.45/AU-end**, P pairs тЖТ **PтИТ1 stacks** (P тЙд 1 тЗТ 0). Oracles NNDB Example 1 (A-U closing, 6-nt loop AтАжA) loop +4.6 + helix тИТ6.01 = **тИТ1.4**; Example 2 (5-nt loop GтАжG, GG bonus) loop +4.1 + helix тИТ6.01 = **тИТ1.9**; all-C 3-nt loop 6.9, 4-nt 7.7. One display-precision item (2-dp intermediate rounding, tests assert `.Within(1e-9)`); no contradictions. **No new concept** тАФ enriches [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]].
- [[rna-invert-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-INVERT-001 (RNA inverted repeats / potential stem regions тАФ antiparallel **reverse-complement arms** that form a stem-loop; RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): IUPACpal (Alamro 2021, PMC7866733) `W G W╠Дс┤┐` gapped model + *k*-Hamming mismatch (perfect = k=0) + Watson-Crick RNA complement (AтЯ╖U, CтЯ╖G) + Wikipedia/Ussery 2008 (`5'---TTACGnnnnnnCGTAA---3'`, zero-gap тЗТ palindrome) + EMBOSS `einverted` (inverted repeat = stem-loop = local alignment of a sequence vs its reverse complement) sources; oracles `UUACGAAAAAACGUAA` (arm `UUACG` 0тАУ4 / loop 5тАУ10 / arm `CGUAA` 11тАУ15) and palindromic `GGCCAAAGGCC` (left 0тАУ3 / right 7тАУ10 / len 4); MUST antiparallel-not-parallel + no-IRтЖТempty; scope restriction = **perfect ungapped `k=0`** arms only (einverted scored mismatch/gap DP Not Implemented), loop bounds via minSpacing/maxSpacing, maximal-arm non-overlapping greedy reporting; no contradictions. **No new concept** тАФ reuses [[repetitive-element-detection]] (same IUPACpal IR model) + [[rna-base-pairing]] (antiparallel RNA complement) + [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]/[[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] (stem-loop framing).
- [[rna-mfe-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-MFE-001 (**Minimum Free Energy (MFE) RNA secondary-structure prediction** тАФ the ZukerтАУStiegler dynamic-programming folder; the folding/search layer of the RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy` / `PredictStructure`). Sources: **Zuker & Stiegler 1981** *NAR* 9(1):133 (rank 1 тАФ original MFE DP, loop decomposition hairpin/stacking/bulge-interior/multibranch, polynomial) + **Lorenz 2011** ViennaRNA 2.0 (rank 3 тАФ MFE fold "derived from the ZukerтАУStiegler decomposition", **O(n┬│)**) + **Ward 2017** *NAR* 45(14):8541 (rank 1 тАФ C(i,j)=min(hairpin, interior/bulge, multiloop) + multiloop M/M1 + exterior F matrices, **standard affine multiloop тЖТ O(n┬│) time / O(n┬▓) space**, "simplest model is best") + **NNDB Turner 2004** worked examples + **Mathews 2004** PNAS 101:7287. The unit that **consumes** the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] Turner terms and **produces** a [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] structure. Oracles `CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy("CACAAAAAAAUGUG")`=тИТ1.41 (NNDB Example 1, structure `((((......))))`), `CACAGAAAGUGUG`=тИТ1.91 (Example 2, GG first mismatch). Invariants INV-01 MFE тЙд 0, INV-02 suffix-monotone `MFE(s) тЙд MFE(prefix)`, INV-03 optimized DP == classic O(n┬│) baseline; empty/null / homopolymer `AAAAAAAA` / sequence `< minLoopSize+2` (`GCGC`) тЖТ 0 (min hairpin loop 3 nt); intramolecular тЗТ no helix-init constant. Two documented simplifications (multiloop per-unpaired `c=0` with `a=9.25`/helix `c=тИТ0.63`; 2-dp rounding, tests `.Within(1e-9)` + `Round(mfe,1)`==NNDB), no source contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]]; the folder the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] `AssessHairpinByMfe` path (prior pages' generic *RNA-STRUCT-001*) uses.
- [[rna-pair-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PAIR-001 (**RNA Base Pairing** тАФ the RNA-secondary-structure family's own base-pairing primitive): `RnaSecondaryStructure.CanPair` / `GetBasePairType` (typed `WatsonCrick`/`Wobble`/`null` classifier) / `GetComplement`. Sources: **Crick 1966** *J Mol Biol* 19:548 (wobble hypothesis тАФ G pairs C(WC)+U(wobble), U pairs A(WC)+G(wobble); G-U the only standard wobble, distinct from WC) + Wikipedia *Base pair* (canonical AтАвU 2 H-bonds / GтАвC 3 H-bonds, pairing reciprocal) + Wikipedia *Wobble base pair* + IUPAC-IUB 1970 *Biochemistry* 9(20):4022 (complement table) + Biopython `complement_rna("CGAUT")`тЖТ`"GCUAA"`. Rule {A-U, U-A, G-C, C-G}=WatsonCrick, {G-U, U-G}=Wobble, all else false/null; complement AтЖТU/UтЖТA/GтЖТC/CтЖТG/**TтЖТA**(DNA T=U)/NтЖТN/RтЖТY; symmetry `f(x,y)==f(y,x)`; non-alphabetтЖТfalse/null no exception. One non-correctness normalization (case-insensitive upper-casing). No contradictions. **No new concept** тАФ enriches the shared [[rna-base-pairing]] primitive (the MIRNA-PAIR-001 sibling), adding the typed `GetBasePairType` classifier surface.
- [[rna-partition-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PARTITION-001 (**RNA partition function (McCaskill) and Boltzmann structure probability** тАФ the probabilistic/ensemble layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): the Boltzmann-weighted counterpart of MFE folding that computes the equilibrium partition function `Z`, per-base-pair binding probabilities, and the Boltzmann probability of a given structure. Sources: **McCaskill 1990** *Biopolymers* 29(6-7):1105 (rank 1, PMID 1695107 тАФ full equilibrium partition function + substructure probabilities, **O(n┬│) recursion**) + **S. Will MIT 18.417 (2011)** slides (rank 1 тАФ inside `Q_ij = Q_{i,j-1} + ╬г_k Q_{i,k-1}┬╖Q^b_{kj}`, `Z = Q_{1n}`, base case `Q_ij=1` for iтЙеjтИТm; outside base-pair-probability recursion; `Pr[P|S]=ZтБ╗┬╣exp(тИТ╬▓E(P))`) + **Freiburg McCaskill tool** (rank 3 тАФ simplified fixed-per-pair `E_bp` model, WC+GU pairing) + **ViennaRNA pf_fold** (rank 3 тАФ `p(s)=e^(тИТ╬▓E(s))/Z`, default 37 ┬░C = 310.15 K, RT = 0.61626805). **Correction (2026-06-16):** base-pair probability requires the **outside** recursion `p_kl = Q^b_kl┬╖O_kl/Z`; the external-only term is **wrong for nestable pairs** (`GGGAAACCC` P(2,6)=6/20 not external 1/20; verified to 3.3e-16 vs Boltzmann brute force). Oracles (E_bp=0 тЗТ Z counts structures): `AAAA`тЖТ1, `GC`тЖТ1, `GGGGCCCC`тЖТ16, `GGGAAACCC`тЖТ20 (two independent derivations). Invariants Z тЙе 1 (empty structure weight 1), P(i,j) тИИ [0,1] + symmetric, per-base pairing sum тЙд 1 (300 random seqs, max 0.983), monotone in E_bp; min-loop m forbids jтИТk тЙд m pairs, WC+GU only. One simplification (fixed-per-pair `E_bp` energy model vs full Turner NN тАФ energy model only; recurrence + probabilities + invariants conformant with McCaskill 1990), no source contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]] тАФ the ensemble/`alternative_to` counterpart of [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]].
- [[rna-pkpredict-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PKPREDICT-001 (**Pseudoknot structure prediction тАФ canonical H-type, pknotsRG class**; the **crossing-helix layer** of the RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain a single simple recursive pseudoknot (two **crossing** helices, `i<k<j<l` Antczak 2018) тАФ the one feature the nested [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE]] / [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill|McCaskill]] predictors cannot represent. Sources: **Reeder & Giegerich 2004** *BMC Bioinformatics* 5:104 (rank 1, PMC514697 тАФ pknotsRG "two crossing helices with three intervening loops", grammar `a~~~u~~~b~~~v~~~a'~~~w~~~b'`, **O(nтБ┤)/O(n┬▓)**, canonization rules, penalties) + **pknotsRG `Energy.lhs`** source (rank 3 тАФ verbatim penalties + same-NN-model helices, no extra per-pair penalty) + **Wikipedia/Rivas & Eddy 1999** (H-type 5'тЖТ3' stem1-5'тЖТloop1тЖТstem2-5'тЖТloop2тЖТstem1-3'тЖТloop3тЖТstem2-3', two-layer `()`/`[]`) + **PDB 437D / Su 1999** (BWYV real H-type, tertiary-stabilized) + **Antczak 2018** (crossing `i<k<j<l`). Energy = Turner NN stacking both helices + penalties **pseudoknot initiation 9.0** (anti-spurious-knot gate) / **unpaired loop nt 0.3** / **base pair inside knot 0.0** (kcal/mol). Canonization: equal-length bulge-free helices / maximal extent / fixed overlap boundary. Oracles designed H-type `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`тЖТ`HasPseudoknot==true`, stems (0,15)тАж(3,12)+(6,21)тАж(9,18), two-layer `((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]`, ╬ФG<MFE; plain hairpin `GGGGAAAACCCC`тЖТ`HasPseudoknot==false` = MFE `((((....))))`; BWYV `GGCGCGGCACCGUCCGCGGAACAAACGG`тЖТNN optimum is the stem-1 hairpin **not** the knot (documented NN-only limit). Invariants `FreeEnergy тЙд CalculateMfeStructure().FreeEnergy` (MFE fallback), no spurious knot, each position paired тЙд1├Ч + тЙе1 genuine crossing; empty/null/too-shortтЖТempty pair-free ╬ФG 0. One documented scope note (PARTIAL pknotsRG coverage тАФ single canonical H-type only; recursively-nested / over-arching / multiple knots **not** implemented; loops fold with the existing MFE). No contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] тАФ the crossing-structure complement of the nested MFE folder + McCaskill ensemble.
- [[rna-pkrecursive-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PKRECURSIVE-001 (**Recursive pknotsRG pseudoknot prediction тАФ nested / multiple / over-arching H-type knots**; the **recursive-grammar extension** of the single-knot RNA-PKPREDICT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain **several** pseudoknots and knots **nested inside loops / over-arched by an enclosing helix**, filling exactly the PARTIAL-coverage gap the single-knot unit recorded. **Same pknotsRG class** (Reeder & Giegerich 2004/2007) тАФ same Turner-NN energy on both helices, same penalties **initiation 9.0 / unpaired loop nt 0.3 / pair inside knot 0.0** kcal/mol, same canonization rules тАФ but the three loops *u*/*v*/*w* now fold by the **same recursive folder** (a loop may contain a further knot), the top level **chains multiple knots**, and an enclosing helix may **over-arch** a knot. Sources: **Reeder & Giegerich 2004** *BMC Bioinformatics* 5:104 (loops "fold internally тАж **including simple recursive pseudoknots**", **O(nтБ┤)/O(n┬▓)**, canonization 8тЖТ4 boundaries vs Rivas & Eddy O(nтБ╢)/O(nтБ┤)) + **Reeder, Steffen & Giegerich 2007** *NAR* 35:W320 (per-interval **competition** with unknotted foldings тАФ the whole-sequence mechanism enabling multiple/nested knots) + **pknotsRG `Energy.lhs`** (verbatim 9.0/0.3/0.0) + **Antczak 2018** (crossing `i<k<j<l`). Constructed fully-derivable oracles: over-arching `AAAAAAAAGGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGGUUUUUUUU` (38 nt)тЖТ`((((((((((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]))))))))` **╬ФG тИТ14.37** (single-knot/MFE both тИТ13.05, no combined structure); two-knot 80-ntтЖТ**two** crossing knots (crossing-count 32) **╬ФG тИТ28.74** (single/MFE тИТ27.14, none); plain `GGGGAAAACCCC`тЖТ no knot = MFE; single-knot parity `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`тЖТidentical тИТ8.76. Invariants recursive ╬ФG тЙд MFE (0 violations, 150-seq random sweep), no spurious knots, each position paired тЙд1├Ч + тЙе1 crossing; empty/null/too-shortтЖТempty pair-free. **Excluded** (verbatim): triple-crossing helices, kissing hairpins, bulged/unequal-length helices. Two scope notes: PARTIAL recursion (realizes the recursive *class* via maximal-extent helix scan, not bit-identical to the reference 4-boundary ADP parser) + two-simultaneous-knot cases are **engineered** (isolated A┬╖U clamps тАФ two strong G┬╖C knots are the genuine MFE only when the cross-region nested alternative is suppressed). No contradictions. **Enriches** [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] (┬з6, the recursive extension of the single-knot concept тАФ no new concept).
- [[rna-pseudoknot-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PSEUDOKNOT-001 (**Pseudoknot detection** тАФ identify **crossing** base pairs in a **given** structure; the detection/analysis facet of the RNA crossing-helix family, `RnaSecondaryStructure.DetectPseudoknots`): given a base-pair **set** (not a sequence), a pure **O(n┬▓) combinatorial scan** reports every crossing pair-of-pairs `i<k<j<l`. Sources: **Antczak et al. 2018** *Bioinformatics* 34(8):1304 (rank 1 тАФ crossing/conflict `i<j<i'<j'`, pseudoknot **order** = min base-pair-set decompositions to nested, DBL notation order 0 `()`/1 `[]`/2 `{}`/3 `<>`/4тАУ8 letters, H-type `([)]`) + **Smit, Rother, Heringa & Knight 2008** *RNA* 14(3):410 (rank 1 тАФ pseudoknot presence *requires* crossing pairs; order-assignment / pseudoknot-removal family) + **biotite.structure.pseudoknots** (rank 3 тАФ crossing = not purely nestable; nested order 0 / knotted order 1+) + **Wikipedia Pseudoknot** (rank 4, cites Rivas & Eddy 1999). Crossing `i<k<j<l` = pseudoknot; two exhaustive negatives **nested** `i<k<l<j` + **disjoint** `j<k`. Oracles `([)]`=(0,2)+(1,3)тЖТ`0<1<2<3`тЖТone pseudoknot, nested (0,5)+(1,4)тЖТnone, disjoint (0,2)+(3,5)тЖТnone. Invariants тЙе2 pairs required / endpoints normalized min-max to open<close / deterministic / every reported knot satisfies `i<k<j<l`. **Distinct** from the energy-driven [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] predictor (pair set vs sequence, O(n┬▓) scan vs O(nтБ┤) energy DP) тАФ it *is* the crossing primitive that predictor's validity invariant leans on. One scope note: pseudoknot-**order** grouping (DBL layering) Not Implemented (reports the binary crossing relations); no contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] тАФ the analysis-side sibling of the crossing-helix predictor.
- [[rna-stemloop-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-STEMLOOP-001 (**Stem-Loop (Hairpin) Detection**, area `RnaStructure`): the **enumeration layer** of the RNA secondary-structure family тАФ `FindStemLoops(sequence, minStem, minLoop, maxLoop, allowWobble)` / `FindHairpins` **scan a sequence for every stem-loop** it can form (stem of antiparallel WC/wobble pairs + apical loop), an **O(n┬▓┬╖L)** scan distinct from the single-optimal [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]], the hairpin *energy* unit [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]], and the miRNA-specific [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]. Tetraloop families **GNRA** (GAAA/GCAA/GGAA/GUAA) / **UNCG** (UACG/UCCG/UGCG/UUCG) / **CUUG**, ~3.0 kcal/mol bonus; `FindPseudoknots` flags crossing pairs `i<k<j<l` (same primitive as [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]). Invariants non-overlap / тЙд1 pair per base / contiguous loop / antiparallel stem; defaults wobble-on, minLoop 3, minStem 3. Limitations: no PK prediction from sequence, simplified energy, no internal loops/bulges, single structure. No contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-stem-loop-enumeration]].
- [[rna-struct-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit RNA-STRUCT-001 (**Secondary Structure Prediction**, area `RnaStructure`): the **top-level structure-prediction umbrella** on `RnaSecondaryStructure` тАФ `Predict(sequence)` (a **Nussinov & Jacobson 1980** O(n┬│)/O(n┬▓) base-pair-**maximizing** DP), `PredictWithConstraints` (forced base pairs, Mathews 2004), `ToDotBracket`/`FromDotBracket` (notation round-trip). No source contradictions; one wiki reconciliation (RNA-STRUCT-001 тЙа RNA-MFE-001, superseding the earlier alias assumption). **New concept** [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]].

- [[pop-ancestry-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit POP-ANCESTRY-001 (Ancestry Estimation тАФ supervised/projection ADMIXTURE, estimate ancestry proportions Q by EM with **fixed** reference allele frequencies F; **first population-genetics POP-\* unit**): Alexander, Novembre & Lange 2009 *Genome Research* 19(9):1655 (rank 1 тАФ genotype gтИИ{0,1,2}=allele-1 count, Q I├ЧK / F K├ЧJ, **log-likelihood Eq. 2** `L=╬гс╡в╬гт▒╝{g┬╖ln(╬гq┬╖f)+(2тИТg)┬╖ln(╬гq┬╖(1тИТf))}` under `╬г_k q_ik=1`, **FRAPPE EM Eq. 4** `q^{n+1}=(1/2J)╬гт▒╝[g┬╖a+(2тИТg)┬╖b]`, convergence Eq. 5 ╬ФL<╬╡ default 10тБ╗тБ┤, cost O(IJK┬▓), K! label-permutation maxima) + Alexander & Lange 2011 *BMC Bioinformatics* 12:246 (supervised mode тАФ labelled reference individuals as training samples, less allele-freq uncertainty; full text Springer-gated) + ADMIXTURE 1.4 Manual ┬з2.10 supervised / ┬з2.14 projection (reference rows of Q pinned, refs 100% single-ancestry; learned F as fixed input `admixture -P`) sources; oracles symmetric K=2 J=2 panel f_A=[0.8,0.2]/f_B=[0.2,0.8] g=[2,0] from (0.5,0.5) тЖТ **one EM iter (0.8,0.2) exactly** тЖТ (0.9412,0.0588) тЖТ converges (1.0,0.0), single-SNP f=[0.9,0.1] g=2тЖТ(0.9,0.1)/g=1тЖТ(0.5,0.5) uninformative-het/g=0тЖТ(0.1,0.9), identical panels uniform fixed point; MUST ╬г_k q=1 / EM-ascent L non-decreasing / diagnosticтЖТsource; two assumptions (maxIterations budget augments ╬╡=10тБ╗тБ┤ convergence тАФ same fixed point; missing genotype тИЙ{0,1,2} skipped); label non-identifiability pinned by fixed labelled panels; no contradictions. Own concept [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]].
- [[pop-div-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit POP-DIV-001 (Diversity statistics тАФ nucleotide diversity ╧А, Watterson's ╬╕, Tajima's D, heterozygosity; **second population-genetics POP-\* unit**, sibling of POP-ANCESTRY-001): Nei & Li 1979 *PNAS* (╧А = ╬г_{i<j} d_ij / (C(n,2)┬╖L), mean per-site pairwise differences) + Watterson 1975 *TPB* (╬╕╠В_W = S/a_n, a_n = ╬г_{i=1}^{nтИТ1} 1/i harmonic number; per-site ╬╕_W = S/(a_n┬╖L)) + Tajima 1989 *Genetics* (D = (k╠В тИТ S/a_1)/тИЪ(e_1┬╖S + e_2┬╖S(SтИТ1)), **k╠В = average pairwise-difference COUNT not per-site ╧А**, variance terms a_1/a_2/b_1/b_2/c_1/c_2/e_1/e_2; DтЙИ0 neutral / D<0 excess rare alleles=sweep-or-expansion / D>0 deficit=balancing-or-contraction) + Nei 1978 *Genetics* (unbiased gene diversity H_obs = n/(nтИТ1)┬╖H_exp, H_exp = (1/L)╬г(1тИТ╬гp┬▓); haploid H_obs тЙб ╧А) sources; all "exact match" no deviations; Wikipedia oracle n=5/L=20/S=4/a_1=25/12 тЖТ k╠В=2.0/╧А=0.1/S/a_1тЙИ1.92/d=0.08/╬╕_WтЙИ0.096 тЖТ **DтЙИ0.273** (TD-C01/TD-C02); edge cases n=0тЖТ0, n=1тЖТ╧А0/╬╕ undef, n=2тЖТ╧А defined but **D undefinedтЖТ0** (needs nтЙе3), S=0/monomorphicтЖТall 0, VarтЙд0тЖТD=0; API note `CalculateTajimasD(k╠В, S, n)` takes k╠В NOT per-site ╧А; no contradictions. - [[pop-freq-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit POP-FREQ-001 (Allele & genotype frequencies тАФ major/minor frequencies, MAF, MAF filtering; foundational population-genetics POP-\* primitive): Wikipedia *Allele frequency* / *Genotype frequency* (biallelic `p = f(AA) + ┬╜f(AB)`, `q = f(BB) + ┬╜f(AB)`, **`p + q = 1`**; allele-counting `total = 2┬╖(n_AA+n_AB+n_BB)`, `major = 2┬╖n_AA+n_AB`, `minor = 2┬╖n_BB+n_AB`; four-o'clock oracle 49/42/9 тЖТ freq(a)=0.30/freq(A)=0.70) + Wikipedia *Minor allele frequency* (`MAF = min(alt_freq, 1тИТalt_freq)`, **`0 тЙд MAF тЙд 0.5`**; HapMap MAF тЙе 0.05, common>0.05 vs rare<0.05) + VCF/PLINK dosage encoding (0=hom-ref/1=het/2=hom-alt, `alt_freq = ╬гg/(2n)`) + Gillespie 2004 / NDSU PopGen sources; oracles AF-1тАжAF-6, MAF-1тАжMAF-6 (alt_freq 0.7 тЖТ MAF 0.3 symmetry; monomorphic тЖТ 0; 50/50 тЖТ 0.5), FLT-1тАжFLT-6 (MAF<0.01 / <0.05 / >0.4, empty/all/none); invariants p+q=1, major+minor=total, MAF symmetric 0тАж0.5; edge cases zero samplesтЖТ(0,0), empty vectorтЖТMAF 0, **negative count тЖТ `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`**; scope = biallelic counting/normalization only (no HWE test, no multiallelic, no phasing/imputation); all exact-match, no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[allele-genotype-frequencies]].
- [[pop-fst-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit POP-FST-001 (Fst fixation index + F-statistics Fis/Fit/Fst + pairwise Fst; population-genetics POP-\* differentiation unit, **consumes** per-population allele frequencies from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Fixation index* (**Wright 1965 variance-based** `Fst = ╧Г_S┬▓/(pBar(1тИТpBar))`; two-pop `pBar=(n1┬╖p1+n2┬╖p2)/(n1+n2)`, `╧Г_S┬▓=(n1(p1тИТpBar)┬▓+n2(p2тИТpBar)┬▓)/(n1+n2)`; multi-locus **ratio-of-sums** `╬г╧Г_S┬▓/╬гhet`; FstтИИ[0,1], 0=panmixia/1=fixed differences; **not a metric** тАФ fails triangle inequality) + Wikipedia *F-statistics* (heterozygosity partition `Fis=1тИТHi/Hs`, `Fit=1тИТHi/Ht`, `Fst=1тИТHs/Ht`; **exact identity** `(1тИТFit)=(1тИТFis)(1тИТFst)`) + Wright 1950/1965, Weir & Cockerham 1984 (╬╕ estimator тАФ cited as what is **deliberately NOT** implemented: no ANOVA/finite-sample bias correction), Holsinger & Weir 2009, Cavalli-Sforza 1994 sources; oracles identicalтЖТ0, fixed p1=1/p2=0тЖТ**1.0 exactly** (pBar=.5,var=.25,het=.25), pop1=(.9,.8)/pop2=(.1,.2)тЖТ1/2, unequal sizes 0.006274тАж, components Fis=1/19/Fit=1/13/Fst=1/39, scale 1/2499 & 61/198, pairwise cells 1/99,4/21,3/25, excess-het **negative** Fis=тИТ2/3/Fit=тИТ2/5/Fst=4/25; ref values Cavalli-Sforza (MbutiтАУPNG 0.4573, mean 0.1338) + Elhaik 2012 HapMap; edge cases denominator 0 (pBar=0/1, both-fixed-same, empty)тЖТ**return 0**, monomorphicтЖТ0; pairwise matrix symmetric, zero diagonal; 25 tests (тИТ1 dup +4 new); no deviations/contradictions. - [[pop-hw-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit POP-HW-001 (Hardy-Weinberg equilibrium chi-square test; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** genotype counts from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Hardy-Weinberg principle* (Hardy 1908 / Weinberg 1908 тАФ expected genotype freqs `f(AA)=p┬▓`/`f(Aa)=2pq`/`f(aa)=q┬▓`, Ford moth example, deviation causes, genotyping-error note) + Wikipedia *Chi-squared test* (Pearson goodness-of-fit `╧З┬▓=╬г(OтИТE)┬▓/E`) + Emigh 1980 (chi-square comparison) + Wigginton et al. 2005 AJHG (**exact test** тАФ cited as the out-of-scope alternative) sources; allele freq `p=(2┬╖n_AA+n_Aa)/(2n)`/`q=1тИТp`, expected counts `E={p┬▓n,2pqn,q┬▓n}`, **df=1** (`#genotypesтИТ#alleles=3тИТ2`), p-value via chi-square CDF (lower-incomplete-gamma approx), default **╬▒=0.05** critical 3.841; `TestHardyWeinberg` returns InEquilibrium/ChiSquare/PValue; oracles Ford moth (1469,138,5)тЖТ`pтЙИ0.954`/`╧З┬▓тЙИ0.83`тЖТin-eq (HW-E01), perfect (25,50,25)тЖТ`╧З┬▓=0` (HW-E02), excess-het (10,80,10)тЖТ`╧З┬▓=36 тЙл 3.84`тЖТout-of-eq (HW-E03), zero samplesтЖТInEquilibrium true/PValue 1 (HW-E04), fixed (100,0,0)тЖТin-eq (HW-E05), all-het (0,100,0)тЖТout-of-eq (HW-E06); edge cases **zero nтЖТPValue 1** (no evidence against HтВА), **expected-0 term skipped** (div-by-zero guard); scope = biallelic chi-square goodness-of-fit only (no exact test, no multiallelic); no deviations/contradictions. - [[pop-ld-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit POP-LD-001 (Linkage disequilibrium тАФ `CalculateLD` (D, D', r┬▓) + `FindHaplotypeBlocks`; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** allele/haplotype frequencies from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Linkage disequilibrium* (`D = p_AB тИТ p_A┬╖p_B`; Lewontin 1964 `D' = |D|/D_max` with sign-branched `D_max` clamped [0,1]; Hill & Robertson 1968 `r┬▓ = D┬▓/(p_A┬╖q_A┬╖p_B┬╖q_B)`; **diploid-frequency result** `R_AB = r_AB` (Wright 1933) тЗТ r┬▓ computable **without phase**) + Wikipedia *Haplotype block* (Gabriel 2002 / Patil 2001 threshold blocks) sources; implementation `r┬▓` = squared Pearson correlation of 0/1/2 genotype dosage vectors `Cov┬▓/(Var┬╖Var)`, `D` from diploid covariance `Cov=2D тЗТ D=Cov/2`; `FindHaplotypeBlocks` = simplified adjacent-pair Gabriel (consecutive `r┬▓ тЙе threshold`, default **0.7**, тЙе2 variants); oracles perfect LD (identical vectors)тЖТ`r┬▓тЙИ1`, no LD (balanced)тЖТ`r┬▓тЙИ0`, anti-correlationтЖТ`r┬▓=1`/`D'=1` (sign-blind), block oracles singleтЖТnone / two-highтЖТone / two-lowтЖТnone / all-strongтЖТone span / non-contiguousтЖТmultiple; INV `0тЙдr┬▓тЙд1`, `0тЙд|D'|тЙд1`, block StartтЙдEnd/тЙе2/non-overlapping/ordered, distance+IDs preserved; edge cases emptyтЖТ`r┬▓=0,D'=0`, monomorphic (zero variance/denominator)тЖТ`r┬▓=0` (guarded), all-identicalтЖТ`r┬▓=0`; scope = two-biallelic-loci r┬▓/D' + adjacent-pair blocks only (no full LD matrix, no phasing/EM, no decay-curve fit, no exact Gabriel CI); no deviations/contradictions. - [[probe-design-001-lna-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for the **LNA (locked nucleic acid) Tm-adjustment** variant of PROBE-DESIGN-001: an **LNA-adjusted nearest-neighbour Tm** that raises a probe's Tm/specificity (enabling shorter MGB-style 13тАУ20 nt probes) by locking internal bases. Sources: **McTigue, Peterson & Kahn 2004** (*Biochemistry*, rank 1 тАФ ╬Ф╬ФH┬░/╬Ф╬ФS┬░ increments for all **32** LNA+DNA:DNA nearest neighbours; internal LNA **raises Tm**), **MELTING 5** reference impl (`McTigue2004lockedmn.xml` verbatim table in **cal/mol** + `McTigue04LockedAcid.java` тАФ **additive-increment** application and **terminal-LNA rejection**), rmelting worked example. Model: compute plain DNA NN ╬ФH┬░/╬ФS┬░ then **add** the McTigue increment per LNA-containing step, onto the library's SantaLucia-1998-unified DNA NN engine (same as PRIMER-TM-001 [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]); terminal/non-ACGT/out-of-range тЖТ not-computable. Oracle CCATTGCTACC (LNA@4) тЖТ ╬ФH┬░ тИТ80.014 / ╬ФS┬░ тИТ216.6 тЖТ LNA Tm **63.528 ┬░C** vs all-DNA 59.692 (**╬ФTm +3.84 ┬░C**), agreeing with MELTING `mct04` 63.614 to 0.086 ┬░C (documented base-NN-set residual; increments applied exactly). Enriches [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] (LNA section).
- [[probe-valid-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit PROBE-VALID-001 (**hybridization-probe validation / off-target specificity scan** тАФ a **gapped SmithтАУWaterman local alignment** of the candidate probe against a pooled reference, replacing an earlier ungapped Hamming scan; the **specificity-checking sibling** of PROBE-DESIGN-001, a genuinely distinct algorithm): Smith & Waterman 1981 (local-alignment recurrence with the **zero floor** тЖТ local, indel-aware; traceback stops at 0 so a mismatched tail is trimmed), Altschul et al. 1990/1997 BLAST (the **gapped-vs-ungapped** improvement тАФ a single gapped alignment finds indel off-targets the ungapped HSPs miss; the unit realizes the *gapped local alignment* property, an **exact** full SW scan, not seed-and-extend or a genome-scale index), Karlin & Altschul 1990 / Altschul 1990 statistics (opt-in `ComputeLambdaNucleotide`/`ComputeKarlinAltschul`: `E=K┬╖m┬╖n┬╖e^(тИТ╬╗S)`, ╬╗ = root of `╬г p_i p_j e^(╬╗ s_ij)=1`, bit score `S'=(╬╗SтИТln K)/ln 2`, `E=m┬╖n┬╖2^(тИТS')`; preconditions expected-score<0 **and** a positive score; K caller-supplied), Kane et al. 2000 (empirical **>75% identity** cross-hybridization threshold, `minIdentity` default 0.75, caller-configurable; <14тАУ15 contiguous-complement caveat); oracles тАФ probe `ACGTACGTACGT` vs an indel copy `ACGTACTGTACGT` aligns `ACGTAC-GTACGT` 12/12 identity 1.0 `HasGaps=true` (**found by gapped, missed by ungapped Hamming maxMismatches=3**); indel+mismatch `ACGTACTGTACTT` тЖТ SW trims `TT` tail тЖТ 10/12 = 0.8333 (admitted @0.75, rejected @0.90); ╬╗ for +1/тИТ3 uniform-0.25 = **1.3740631** (тЙИ blastn 1.37, expected score тИТ2.0<0), K=0.711/S=30/m=20/n=1000 тЖТ bit **59.9627**, **E=1.7802eтИТ14**, EтЖУ in S and linear in m┬╖n; BLAST DNA scoring +2/тИТ3 gap тИТ2. ASSUMPTION: on-target = first perfect ungapped full-coverage exact match (API/labelling, not a sourced constant); no source contradictions. Own concept [[probe-offtarget-specificity-scan]].
- [[seq-atskew-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-ATSKEW-001 (**AT skew**, `(A тИТ T)/(A + T)` тАФ the A/T strand-asymmetry sibling of GC skew): Lobry 1996 *Mol Biol Evol* 13(5):660 (PMID 8676740, primary тАФ founding intra-strand base-asymmetry observation over *E. coli*/*B. subtilis*/*H. influenzae*) + Charneski et al. 2011 *PLoS Genet* 7(9):e1002283 (verbatim formula; Firmicute AT skew from **selection not mutation**) + Wikipedia "GC skew" (both formulas + range **тИТ1тАж+1**, AT skew `тИТ1тЗФA=0` / `+1тЗФT=0`) + Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils.GC_skew` (symbol conventions тАФ **case-insensitive** counting, **zero-denominator тЗТ 0.0**, ambiguous/non-canonical bases ignored); hand-derived oracles `AAAAтЖТ1.0`, `TTTTтЖТтИТ1.0`, `ATATтЖТ0.0`, `AAATтЖТ0.5`, `GGCCтЖТ0.0` (no A/T), `AAATGGGCCCтЖТ0.5` (G/C ignored), `aaatтЖТ0.5` (case-insensitive); corner cases empty/no-A-or-T тЗТ 0.0, non-A/T symbols ignored, bounds [тИТ1,+1]; one documented ASSUMPTION (lowercase + non-ACGT handling inferred by analogy from the shipped `GC_skew` тАФ formula itself fully sourced), no source contradictions. New family concept [[nucleotide-composition-skew]] (covers AT skew + its GC-skew sibling).

- [[seq-complex-dust-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-COMPLEX-DUST-001 (**DUST triplet-frequency low-complexity score**, `score = тИС_t c(cтИТ1)/2 / (LтИТ2)` over nucleotide triplet counts; the DNA-sequence low-complexity **masker**): Morgulis, Gertz, Sch├дffer & Agarwala 2006 *J Comput Biol* 13(5):1028 (PMID 16796549, primary тАФ "triplet frequencies in 64-base windows", SDUST rewrite = same score, symmetric/context-insensitive masking) + Li 2025 longdust arXiv:2509.07357 (verbatim score formula, `k=3` hardcoded, `LтИТ2` = number of triplets, default window 64 / threshold 2.0 = level 20, **HIGH score тЗТ LOW complexity**) + lh3/sdust `sdust.c` (incremental `rw += cw[t]++` = closed-form `c(cтИТ1)/2` sum, `if (rw*10 > L*T)` with `W=64`/`T=20` тЗТ score>2.0); hand-derived oracles `ATGC`тЖТ0.0 (all-distinct triplets) / `ACGTACGT`тЖТ0.333тАж / `AAAAAA`тЖТ1.5 / `ACACACAC`тЖТ1.0 / `AAAAAAAAAA`тЖТ3.5, homopolymer max `(LтИТ3)/2`, `L<3` undefined; two ASSUMPTIONs (general `wordSize` normalization `LтИТw+1` тАФ only k=3 source-backed; `L<wordSize`тЖТ0), no source contradictions. New concept [[dust-low-complexity-score]].
- [[seq-complex-kmer-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-COMPLEX-KMER-001 (**k-mer entropy** тАФ Shannon entropy `H = тИТ╬г pс╡в logтВВ pс╡в` of the overlapping k-mer frequency distribution, `pс╡в = nс╡в/(LтИТk+1)`, bits; the **entropy member of the `SEQ-COMPLEX-*` family**, `SequenceComplexity.CalculateKmerEntropy`): Li 2025 longdust arXiv:2509.07357 (overlapping `LтИТk+1` k-mers, `H=тИТ╬гpс╡вlogтВВpс╡в`, skewedтЗТlow / uniformтЗТhigh) + ├Зak─▒r 2025 EntropyтАУRank Ratio arXiv:2511.05300 (same formula, base-2тЗТbits, single-nt max logтВВ4=2) + Shannon 1948 (bounds `0тЙдHтЙдlog(k)`, deterministicтЗТ0 / uniformтЗТlog_b n); hand-derived oracles `ACGT` k=1тЖТ2.0 / `ACGT` k=2тЖТlogтВВ3тЙИ1.5849625 / `ATATAT` k=2тЖТ0.9709505945 / `AAAA` k=2тЖТ0.0 / `AAACGT` k=2тЖТ1.9219280949 (=logтВВ5тИТ0.4) / `AC` k=5тЖТ0.0 (L<k); homopolymerтЗТH0, all-distinctтЗТH logтВВN; two API-shape ASSUMPTIONs (L<kтЖТ0; k<1тЖТArgumentOutOfRangeException, null DnaSequenceтЖТArgumentNullException, null/empty stringтЖТ0), no source contradictions. **Same formula as [[k-mer-statistics]]'s `Entropy` field** (a second entry point, not a new measure) тАФ enriches that concept rather than adding a new one.

- [[seq-mw-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-MW-001 (**molecular weight calculation** тАФ the average-isotopic **molecular mass in Daltons** of a **protein, DNA or RNA** sequence via one shared polymerization formula). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* whole-sequence-scalar unit (mass, spanning all three molecule types) тЖТ NEW concept [[molecular-weight]], the mass-weighted sibling of the [[base-composition]] tally and of the [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] GRAVY scalar. Formula fully sourced: Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils.molecular_weight` (`weight = ╬г weight_table[x] тИТ (lenтИТ1)┬╖water`, one water removed per bond тАФ peptide for protein, phosphodiester for nucleic acid; `water = 18.0153` avg / `18.010565` monoisotopic; single monomer тЗТ free-monomer mass, circular тЗТ тИТone more water, double-strand adds the complement strand, **error for protein**; "only unambiguous letters", nucleotides assumed 5'-phosphate) + Biopython `IUPACData` average tables ("from PubChem": protein *free-amino-acid* A 89.0932тАжG 75.0666тАжW 204.2252; DNA *monophosphate* A 331.2218/C 307.1971/G 347.2212/T 322.2085; RNA A 347.2212/C 323.1965/G 363.2206/U 324.1813) + Expasy Compute pI/Mw (protein Mw = "addition of average isotopic masses of amino acids ... and ... one water molecule", Da тАФ algebraically = `╬г free-amino-acid тИТ (lenтИТ1)┬╖water`) + Expasy ProtParam (delegates to Compute pI/Mw) + Expasy FindMod (residue-mass table + HтВВO 18.01524). Re-derived oracles (avg tables, water 18.0153) `AGC`тЖТprotein **249.29** / DNA **949.61** / RNA **997.61** (Biopython docstring), single monomer (zero bonds тЗТ free-monomer mass) `G`тЖТ**75.0666** / `A` DNAтЖТ**331.2218** / `A` RNAтЖТ**347.2212**; empty/nullтЖТ0. One documented deviation (unknown/ambiguous symbols **skipped** тАФ contribute no mass and no bond, reflecting only recognized monomers, no invented average тАФ whereas Biopython *rejects* them; the SEQ-\* skip-unknown convention, an API-shape choice, in-alphabet values stay exactly source-conformant) + two API-shape assumptions (ToUpperInvariant case-fold; the skip resolution); no source contradictions (Expasy/Biopython agree on formula and average-mass tables to rounding). Note MW pairs with pI in the Expasy source but **pI/charge is a separate calculation not in this unit**.
- [[seq-pi-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-PI-001 (**isoelectric point (pI)** тАФ the **pH at which a protein's net charge is zero**, found by bisecting the HendersonтАУHasselbalch net-charge function over [0,14]). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* protein-property scalar (a charge/pH calculation, not mass or hydropathy) тЖТ NEW concept [[isoelectric-point]], the ExPASy Compute pI/Mw partner of [[molecular-weight]]. Charge model fully sourced: Osorio et al. 2015 Peptides `charge_pI.cpp` (net charge `╬г_basic +1/(1+10^(pHтИТpKa)) + ╬г_acidic тИТ1/(1+10^(pKaтИТpH))`, Moore 1985; basic {R,K,H,N-term} / acidic {D,E,C,Y,C-term}, both termini once) + EMBOSS `iep` (pI = net-charge-zero pH, `Epk.dat` scale N-term 8.6/C-term 3.6/C 8.5/D 3.9/E 4.1/H 6.5/K 10.8/R 12.5/Y 10.1, [0,14] bracket, "no electrostatic interactions" тЗТ composition-only/order-independent) + Peptides `charge()` (nine pKa scales; EMBOSS worked example `FLPVLAGLTPSIVPKLVCLLTKKC` net charge 3.037398/2.914112/0.7184524 @ pH 5/7/9) + seqinr `computePI` + ExPASy Compute pI/Mw (Bjellqvist 1993 scale; small/highly-basic-protein accuracy caveat; pairs pI with Mw). Derived-pI oracles (EMBOSS, bisection ┬▒0.01): `A`/`AG`тЖТ6.10 (termini-only midpoint), `D`тЖТ3.75, `K`тЖТ9.70, `DDDD`тЖТ3.23, `KKKK`тЖТ11.27, `FLPVLAGLTPSIVPKLVCLLTKKC`тЖТ9.67 (basic), `ACDEFGHIKLMNPQRSTVWY`тЖТ7.36 (EMBOSS тЙа seqinr Bjellqvist 6.78454 тАФ scale-dependent). Two assumptions (empty/nullтЖТ7.0 input-guard; pKa scale = EMBOSS, a parameter choice not a deviation), pIтИИ[0,14] invariant, no source contradictions.
- [[seq-secstruct-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-SECSTRUCT-001 (**protein secondary structure prediction** тАФ the **Chou-Fasman (1974/1978) P╬▒/P╬▓/Pt conformational propensities** evaluated as a generic **sliding-window mean-propensity profile**: for a window `W`, the arithmetic mean of each of the ╬▒-helix/╬▓-sheet/╬▓-turn propensities over each window). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* protein-property unit тЖТ NEW concept [[protein-secondary-structure-chou-fasman]] (the conformational-propensity analogue of the [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] hydropathy profile, sharing the exact `NтИТW+1` unweighted window-mean mechanism). Sources: Wikipedia ChouтАУFasman (rank 4; nucleation rules 4-of-6-helix threshold 1.03 / 3-of-5-sheet 1.00 / turn тИПp_t cutoff 7.5e-3; ~50тАУ60% Q3 / 29-protein caveat) + Kelley bioinfo lecture (rank 4; helix STEP 1тАУ4 state machine, worked A 142/83 E 151/37) + CSB|SJU Jakubowski (rank 4; **Lys P╬▒ 1.16**) + Przytycka NCBI lecture (rank 4; **Lys 1.14 0.74 1.01**) + ravihansa3000/ChouFasman reference impl (rank 3; full 20-residue Pa/Pb/Pt integer table, **Lys 114**) + BMC Bioinformatics PMC1780123 (rank 1, peer-reviewed; restates rules, helix тЯиP╬▒тЯй>1.03 & >тЯиP╬▓тЯй). Hand-derived oracles: single-residue window = that residue's tuple (A 1.42/0.83/0.66, E 1.51/0.37/0.74, V 1.06/1.70/0.50, N 0.67/0.89/1.56, K 1.14/0.74/1.01); `AE` W2 тЖТ helix 1.465 / sheet 0.60 / turn 0.70; `AEV` W3 тЖТ helix 1.330 / sheet 0.9666тАж / turn 0.6333тАж; `AXE` W3 averages only A+E; NтИТW+1 windows in N-terminus order, case-insensitive, W>N/non-positive/null/empty тЖТ empty. Three assumptions (the method under test is the generic **profile not** the nucleation/extension state machine, so default `W=7` is an API convenience not a CF constant; unknown residues **skip-and-excluded**; the **only contested value Lys P╬▒ resolved to 1.14** тАФ two independent sources incl. the reference impl vs a single 1.16), no contradictions on the 19 uncontested residues.
- [[seq-stats-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-STATS-001 (**the ORIGINAL sequence-composition umbrella** тАФ nucleotide composition A/T/G/C/U/N/Other + Length, **GC content** `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C+U)`, **GC skew** `(GтИТC)/(G+C)` and **AT skew** `(AтИТT)/(A+T)`; also `SummarizeNucleotideSequence` aggregator + `CalculateAminoAcidComposition`). Connective tissue for the piecemeal-ingested composition family: [[seq-composition-001-evidence]] is a later duplicate/consolidated registry entry over the two composition methods first delivered here, [[seq-atskew-001-evidence]] split out the AT-skew member, and [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance|SEQ-GC-ANALYSIS-001]] re-bundled both skews windowed. Sources: Biopython `gc_fraction`/`GC_skew` (rank 3; `gc/length`тИИ[0,1], emptyтЗТ0, case-insensitive, `ZeroDivisionError`тЗТskew 0.0) + Wikipedia "GC skew" (rank 4; both formulas, sign convention) + Lobry 1996 *MBE* 13(5):660 (rank 1, primary тАФ intra-strand base asymmetry). Worked oracles `ATGC`тЖТGC 0.5/skews 0, `GGGC`тЖТGC 1.0/GC skew 0.5/AT skew 0, `AAAT`тЖТGC 0.0/GC skew 0/AT skew 0.5, `GCCC`тЖТGC skew тИТ0.5, `AAUUGGCC`тЖТGC 0.5/AT skew 1.0; emptyтЗТall-zero, zero-denominator skewsтЗТ0.0, case-insensitive; one ASSUMPTION (degenerate IUPAC codes excluded from GC/AT totals тАФ agrees with Biopython over {A,T,G,C,U}), no contradictions. **No new concept** тАФ synthesized on existing [[base-composition]] (composition + GC content) and [[nucleotide-composition-skew]] (both skews).
- [[seq-summary-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-SUMMARY-001 (**`SummarizeNucleotideSequence` тАФ the per-sequence summary record**: bundles Length, nucleotide Composition (A/T/G/C/U/N), **GcContent** `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C+U)`, **Shannon Entropy** `тИТ╬гpс╡вlogтВВpс╡в` bits, **linguistic Complexity**, and **MeltingTemperature** (Wallace len<14 / GC-Marmur-Doty lenтЙе14) into one object). A **pure aggregation** тАФ each field MUST equal its canonical per-metric method on the identical input, so **no new concept**: composition/GC тЖТ [[base-composition]], entropy тЖТ [[seq-entropy-profile-001-evidence]]/[[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]], linguistic complexity тЖТ [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]], Tm тЖТ [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] (legacy Wallace/Marmur default, SEQ-TM-001). Sources: Biopython `gc_fraction` + `MeltingTemp` (Wallace `4(G+C)+2(A+T)` / Marmur-Doty `69.3+0.41┬╖%GCтИТ650/N`) + Wikipedia Shannon (base-2тЗТbits, max logтВВn) + Wikipedia linguistic complexity (Trifonov 1990, `C=тИПUс╡в`, 0<C<1). Oracles `ATGCATGC`тЖТGcContent 0.5/Entropy 2.0/Tm 24.0/Complexity 0.83968тАж, 16-mer `ATGCATGCATGCATGC`тЖТTm 43.375 (GC branch, lenтЙе14); empty/nullтЗТzero summary, case-insensitive. One ASSUMPTION (Tm threshold len<14 = SEQ-TM-001 `WallaceMaxLength`, non-correctness-affecting for the summary's equality contract), no contradictions. **Corrects** the earlier "thin GC wrapper" description of `SummarizeNucleotideSequence` on [[base-composition]]/[[seq-stats-001-evidence]] тАФ it is a full per-sequence statistics record.
- [[seq-thermo-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-THERMO-001 (**DNA duplex thermodynamics** тАФ the full nearest-neighbor **╬ФH┬░/╬ФS┬░/╬ФG┬░/Tm** 4-tuple of a Watson-Crick DNA duplex, a port of Biopython `Tm_NN` over the **DNA_NN3 / Allawi & SantaLucia 1997** table). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* full-tuple thermodynamics engine тЖТ NEW concept [[dna-duplex-nearest-neighbor-thermodynamics]] (neither the legacy Wallace/Marmur scalar Tm nor the 2004-unified PCR-primer engine [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]). Sources: Biopython `MeltingTemp.Tm_NN` (rank 3; DNA_NN3 table verbatim, two-terminus init counted off `seq[0]+seq[-1]`, `Tm=(1000┬╖╬ФH)/(╬ФS+R┬╖ln k)тИТ273.15` with `k=(dnac1тИТdnac2/2)┬╖1eтИТ9`, default 25 nM each тЗТ k=C_T/4, salt method 5 `0.368┬╖(lenтИТ1)┬╖ln[Na]`, docstring `CGTTCCAAAGATGTGGGCATGAGCTTAC`тЖТ60.32 ┬░C) + MELTING 5 User Guide (rank 3; Tm eq ┬з4.2, F-factor 1/4 ┬з4.3, default model "all97") + Wikipedia Nucleic acid thermodynamics (rank 4, cites SantaLucia 1998; per-terminus init corroboration). Oracles `GCGC`тЖТ╬ФH тИТ30.0/╬ФS тИТ84.91/╬ФG тИТ3.67/Tm тИТ18.6, `ATCG`тЖТ╬ФH тИТ23.6/╬ФS тИТ71.81, length<2 тЗТ `(0,0,0,0)`, case-insensitive; zero correctness-affecting assumptions (only the length<2 API convention), no source contradictions.
- [[seq-tm-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-TM-001 (**`CalculateMeltingTemperature` тАФ the standalone scalar melting temperature**, length-dispatched at `ThermoConstants.WallaceMaxLength = 14` between the **Wallace rule** `4(G+C)+2(A+T)` for short oligos and the **Marmur-Doty GC formula** `64.9+41┬╖(GCтИТ16.4)/N` for lenтЙе14). A **%GC rule of thumb carrying no ╬ФH┬░/╬ФS┬░/╬ФG┬░** тЖТ NEW concept [[melting-temperature]] (the **third distinct Tm surface** and the canonical home of the Wallace/Marmur formulas, previously only sketched as the legacy default on [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]). Sources: Biopython `MeltingTemp` `Tm_Wallace` (`4(G+C)+2(A+T)`, "rule of thumb 14тАУ20 nt", `ACGTTGCAATGCCGTA`тЖТ48.0) + `Tm_GC` (general form `A+B┬╖%GCтИТC/N+saltтИТD┬╖%mismatch`; valueset-1 `69.3+0.41┬╖%GCтИТ650/N` Marmur-Doty, valueset-2 QuikChange `81.5+тАжтИТ675/N`); the same evidence file's NN/`Tm_NN`/SantaLucia-1998 datasets belong to SEQ-THERMO-001. Oracles Wallace `ACGTTGCAATGCCGTA`тЖТ48.0 / `ATGCATGC`тЖТ24.0, Marmur-Doty `GCGCGCGCGCATATATATAT`тЖТ51.78 / 16-mer `ATGCATGCATGCATGC`тЖТ43.375; empty/nullтЖТ0, case-insensitive. **Consolidation note:** SEQ-TM-001 is a duplicate/consolidated Registry entry over the two methods already delivered under SEQ-THERMO-001 (`CalculateMeltingTemperature` here + `CalculateThermodynamics` тЖТ [[dna-duplex-nearest-neighbor-thermodynamics]]) тАФ consolidated not re-implemented (TestSpec ┬з7). One ASSUMPTION (14-nt dispatch boundary, non-correctness-affecting under explicit flag) + NN-facet default C_T assumption + repo-vs-Biopython Marmur-Doty constant variant (64.9/тИТ672.4 vs 69.3/тИТ650); no source contradictions. Resolves the "SEQ-TM-001 remains un-ingested / natural home for Wallace/Marmur" follow-up flagged by the SEQ-SUMMARY-001 and SEQ-THERMO-001 ingests.
- [[seq-replication-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-REPLICATION-001 (**replication origin prediction via the cumulative GC-skew minimum** тАФ the classic ori-finder: integrate an *integer* running skew (G:+1, C:тИТ1, A/T:0, `Skew_0=0`, prefix indices `[0,n]`) and read origin off the global **minimum**, terminus off the **maximum**): Rosalind BA1F Minimum Skew Problem (rank 3, canonical worked example тАФ 100-nt sample min тИТ4 @ positions **53, 97**, re-derived in-session exactly) + Grigoriev 1998 *Nucleic Acids Res* 26(10):2286 (rank 1 тАФ cumulative diagram min=origin/max=terminus, extrema тЙИ half chromosome apart, leading strand G-rich) + Lobry 1996 (PMID 8676740 тАФ skew sign flips at origin/terminus) + Wikipedia "GC skew" (max=terminal/min=origin); diagram oracles `CCGGGG`тЖТ`0,тИТ1,тИТ2,тИТ1,0,+1,+2` (min тИТ2 @2/max +2 @6), `GGGCCC`тЖТ`0,+1,+2,+3,+2,+1,0`, `AATT`тЖТflat; `PredictedOrigin=53` first-minimizer tie-break; one documented ASSUMPTION тАФ `IsSignificant` redefined threshold-free as `max>min` (invented `amplitude>count├Ч0.01` constant **removed**), flat diagram тЗТ origin=terminus=0/false; no source contradictions. New concept [[replication-origin-cumulative-skew]] (the distinct cumulative-integration + argmin/argmax *locator*, vs the scalar/windowed skew).
- [[seq-rnacomp-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-RNACOMP-001 (**RNA-specific per-base complement** тАФ `GetRnaComplementBase`, the IUPAC-complete RNA complement map; **RNACOMP тЙа composition**, this is complement chemistry, not the [[base-composition]] tally). **No new concept** тАФ enriched [[rna-base-pairing]] (which already owns the RNA base complement `GetComplement`, RNA-PAIR-001): added a *SEQ-family full-IUPAC RNA complement* subsection. Same chemistry as `RnaSecondaryStructure.GetComplement` but IUPAC-complete (AтЖТU/UтЖТA/GтЖТC/CтЖТG, **TтЖТA** treating DNA T as U; reciprocal RтЖФY/MтЖФK/DтЖФH/BтЖФV; self-complementary W/S/X/N; non-IUPAC pass-through). RNA sibling of DNA `GetComplementBase` (SEQ-COMP-001, not yet ingested); distinct from DNA path (`GetRnaComplementBase('A')='U'` vs `GetComplementBase('A')='T'`). Sources: Biopython `IUPACData.py`/`Seq.py`/API docs (`ambiguous_rna_complement` = `ambiguous_dna_complement` with TтЖТU; "any T is treated as a U") + bioinformatics.org SMS + NC-IUB 1984 (Cornish-Bowden 1985). One deviation: recognized bases returned **uppercase** (repo convention vs Biopython case-preserving) тАФ casing only, complement identity unchanged; no source contradictions.
- [[splice-acceptor-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SPLICE-ACCEPTOR-001 (**acceptor / 3' splice site detection** тАФ score candidate `AG` dinucleotides for the three cis-elements of a real 3'ss under the canonical **GU-AG rule**). First ingested member of the **splicing** family тЖТ NEW concept [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]]. Three scoring surfaces: default `FindAcceptorSites` (**AcceptorPwm** PWM + PPT-quality, `(score/(count+1)+2)/4` [0,1] heuristic; weights from Shapiro & Senapathy 1987), opt-in `FindAcceptorBranchPoint` (18тАУ40 nt window for the human **`yUnAy`** consensus, Gao 2008 conservation y@тИТ3 0.790/U@тИТ2 0.746/A@0 0.923/y@+1 0.751, found тЙе 0.8┬╖3.210; Mercer 2015 corroboration), opt-in **MaxEntScan score3ss** `ScoreAcceptorMaxEnt` (Yeo & Burge 2004 23-nt max-entropy model; MIT-licensed maxentpy 82,560-record tables `Data/maxent_score3.txt`; canonical `ttccaaacgaacttttgtAGgga`тЖТ**2.89** cross-check, +8.19/тИТ0.08); U12 **YCCAC** non-canonical scoring (Hall & Padgett 1994). Corner cases: < 20 nt тЖТ empty guard, no-AG тЖТ empty, cryptic intronic AG decoys, weak PPT skipped. All prior assumptions RESOLVED (PWM weights verified, normalization = design choice, branch-point constants source-traceable). Licence flag: bundled MaxEntScan table is the MIT port, not the academic-terms Burge-lab Perl. No source contradictions.
- [[splice-donor-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SPLICE-DONOR-001 (**donor / 5' splice site detection** тАФ score candidate `GT/GU` dinucleotides for the almost-invariant `GU` intron start under the canonical **GU-AG rule**). Donor member of the **splicing** family тЖТ NEW concept [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] (5' partner of [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]]). Single contiguous **`MAG|GURAGU`** consensus (тИТ3..+6; 0-G/+1-U ~100%, тИТ1-G ~80% for U1 snRNP; **no branch point / PPT** тАФ asymmetric with the acceptor). Two surfaces only: default **IUPAC consensus match-fraction** `FindDonorSites`/`ScoreDonorSite` (plainer than the acceptor PWM+PPT; GC donors self-penalize via the +1-U mismatch 8/9<9/9, old 0.7 penalty removed), opt-in **MaxEntScan score5ss** `ScoreDonorMaxEnt` (Yeo & Burge 2004 9-nt window, **single 16,384-entry table, no overlapping sub-windows** vs score3's 82,560 records; canonical `cagGTAAGT`тЖТ**10.86**, +11.08/тИТ0.12). GC-AG (~0.5тАУ1%) + U12 **AT-AC**/`ATATCC` non-canonical donors. Corner cases: < 9 nt тЖТ empty, no GT/GU тЖТ empty, cryptic donors. All prior assumptions RESOLVED (PWMтЖТIUPAC binary weights, normalizationтЖТmatch fraction, GC penalty removed). Licence flag: bundled MaxEntScan table is the MIT port, not the academic-terms Burge-lab Perl. No source contradictions.
- [[sv-breakpoint-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SV-BREAKPOINT-001 (**breakpoint detection from split / soft-clipped reads**). First ingested member of the **germline structural-variant (SV)** family тЖТ NEW concept [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]]. Localize an SV breakpoint to a single base at the aligned/clipped **junction** of a split read: the SAM/BAM CIGAR **soft clip `S` consumes the read (SEQ) but not the reference** and sits only at a read end тЖТ **leading `S` = left / trailing `S` = right breakpoint** (ClipCrop "marginal point between clipped and matched sequence"; L/R-breakpoints; a no-`S` read = no signal). **Cluster** per-read junctions under three source-backed constraints тАФ positional **tolerance** (ClipCrop "clustered within 5-base differences", 5 b), **minimum support** (SoftSearch тЙе x soft-clipped reads at a position, default 5 / configurable 2; support = # clipped reads in cluster), and **same clip-side + same chromosome** тАФ with a **min clip length** filter (тЙд 5 clipped bases dropped) and `RefineBreakpoint`. Repository `SplitRead` record: `PrimaryPosition` = anchored SAM POS / `SupplementaryPosition` = junction coordinate / `ClipLength`. Oracles: 3 reads @ 5000 ┬▒ тЙд 5 b, same chr, support тЙе 2 тЖТ one breakpoint ~5000; 1 isolated read тЖТ none; 5000 vs 5100 (gap > tolerance) тЖТ two below-support groups тЖТ none. Sources: SAM/BAM spec (samtools/hts-specs, rank 2 тАФ CIGAR consume table / POS / S-at-ends) + Tattini-Magi 2015 review (rank 1 тАФ anchored+imprecise split read, single-base resolution, clustering) + ClipCrop Suzuki 2011 (rank 1 тАФ junction=breakpoint, 5-b clustering, L/R) + SoftSearch Hart 2013 (rank 1 тАФ тЙе x clipped reads, orientation combining, min clip > 5). One ASSUMPTION (cluster reported coordinate = rounded **mean** of member junctions, sub-tolerance only, mirroring sibling `ClusterSplitReads`); operates on already-extracted `SplitRead` records, not raw BAM. Orthogonal to the oncology read-evidence [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] / [[chromothripsis-inference]]. No source contradictions.
- [[sv-cnv-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SV-CNV-001 (**read-depth copy-number variation detection**). The **read-depth-segmentation member of the germline structural-variant (SV) family** тЖТ NEW concept [[read-depth-cnv-segmentation]] (a distinct method from the split-read anchor [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]] тАФ aggregate **read depth of coverage**, not per-read junctions). Pipeline: **read depth тИЭ copy number** (Yoon 2009) тЖТ **windowed counting** (non-overlapping fixed-size windows, one read per start position, per-window mean RD) тЖТ optional **GC correction** `r_i' = r_i┬╖m/m_GC` тЖТ **log2 ratio** `log2(observed depth / reference depth)` (reference = overall median of window means when no baseline given) тЖТ **integer CN = round(2┬╖2^log2)** (CNVkit "round" method, diploid ploidy 2) тЖТ **del/dup call** + segment merge (`DetectCNV`/`SegmentCopyNumber`). Diploid anchors (verbatim CNVkit): 0.5├ЧтЖТlog2 тИТ1.0тЖТCN 1 (Deletion), 1.0├ЧтЖТ0тЖТCN 2 (Neutral), 1.5├ЧтЖТ+0.585тЖТCN 3 (Duplication/gain), 2.0├ЧтЖТ+1.0тЖТCN 4 (amp). Corner cases: **zero-depth window тЖТ no-call** (log2(0)=тИТтИЮ undefined, homozygous-deletion candidate, not тИТтИЮ); **NaN log2 тЖТ Neutral (CN 2)**; CN clamped **тЙе 0**. Sources: Yoon 2009 (Genome Res, rank 1 тАФ RDтИЭCN, windowed counting, GC formula) + CNVkit `call.py` + calling docs (rank 3 тАФ `n=ref_copies┬╖2^log2`, anchors log2(1/2)=тИТ1 / log2(3/2)=0.585, `max(0,ncopies)` clamp, `nan`тЖТneutral). Two ASSUMPTIONs (reference baseline = overall median of non-zero window means; diploid ploidy 2), both source-supported. The oncology [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) is the classification layer *on top of* this same log2 ratio (swaps `round` for hard-threshold binning into 5 CNA states). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[sv-detect-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SV-DETECT-001 (**structural-variant detection from paired-end mapping (PEM) signatures** тАФ discordant read pairs). The **discordant-read-pair member of the germline structural-variant (SV) family** тЖТ NEW concept [[discordant-pair-sv-detection]] (a third read-evidence channel, orthogonal to the split-read anchor [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]] and the depth-based [[read-depth-cnv-segmentation]]). Read how a mate pair's mapped **span + orientation** deviate from the concordant **FR** proper pair (SAM FLAG 0x02; **RF is everted/discordant**, not proper) and classify the SV type: span `> ╬╝+c┬╖╧Г` (FR, same chr) тЖТ **Deletion**, span `< ╬╝тИТc┬╖╧Г` тЖТ **Insertion**, **FF/RR** тЖТ **Inversion**, everted **RF** тЖТ **tandem Duplication**, mates on **different chromosomes** тЖТ **Translocation**. Span cutoff = `c` s.d. of the empirical insert-size distribution (BreakDancer `-c`, default 3 тЗТ mean=400/sd=50 тЗТ bounds [250,550]); **signature-then-cluster** with **min support** тЙе `-r` pairs (default 2). Corner cases: an insertion larger than the insert size is invisible to PEM span and its sequence is not recovered (split-read channel's job); below-support clusters dropped; cutoff bounds exact. One ASSUMPTION тАФ inter-chromosomal (translocation) precedence evaluated **before** orientation (inversion defined only for intra-chromosomal flipped pairs). Sources: Medvedev/Stanciu/Brudno 2009 (Nat Methods, rank 1 тАФ signature catalogue) + BreakDancer README + protocol (Chen 2009 / Fan 2014 тАФ s.d. cutoff, min support, DEL/INS/INV/ITX/CTX codes) + SAM/BWA proper-pair FR convention (cureffi/FLAG 0x02) + DELLY 2012 / SVXplorer 2020 (orientationтЖТtype: RF=dup, FF/RR=inv). Consumes already-mapped read-pair records, not raw BAM; research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[trans-diff-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-DIFF-001 (**two-group RNA-seq differential expression** тАФ log2 fold change + Welch's t-test + Benjamini-Hochberg FDR). **First ingested unit of the Transcriptome / RNA-seq family** тЖТ NEW concept [[differential-expression]]. `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculateFoldChange` / `FindDifferentiallyExpressed`: **log2FC** `log2((mean(treatment)+c)/(mean(control)+c))` (pseudocount c=1, positive = up in treatment, DESeq2 Love 2014 + Science Park lesson) + a **Welch unequal-variance t-test** raw p `t=(X╠ДтВВтИТX╠ДтВБ)/тИЪ(sтВБ┬▓/NтВБ+sтВВ┬▓/NтВВ)`, unbiased (NтИТ1) variances, Welch-Satterthwaite df, exact Student-t tail `p=I_{╬╜/(╬╜+t┬▓)}(╬╜/2,┬╜)` via regularized incomplete beta (Welch 1947) + **Benjamini-Hochberg FDR** reproducing R `p.adjust(method="BH")` `pmin(1,cummin(n/i┬╖p[o]))[ro]` (BH 1995). DE тЗФ **two-criterion gate** `|log2FC| тЙе threshold (default 1.0) AND adjusted p < alpha (default 0.05)`. Oracles: UP `log2(41/11)=+1.8981204тАж` / DOWN тИТ1.8981204тАж / FLAT 0; Welch {1,2,3} vs {7,8,9} тЖТ t=7.348469, ╬╜=4, p=0.0018262607 (SciPy cross-check); BH raw (0.001,0.4,0.5,0.9) тЖТ adj (0.004,0.6667,0.6667,0.9). Corner cases: <2 replicates тЖТ p=1; se=0 тЖТ p=1 (equal means)/p=0 (unequal); zero mean тЖТ pseudocount. Three source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (pseudocount 1, <2-replicate p=1, se=0 conventions). A **simple two-group** estimator, **not** the full DESeq2 negative-binomial GLM. `alternative_to` the rank-sum [[significant-taxa-detection]] (no built-in FDR); DE gene lists feed [[pathway-enrichment-ora]]. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[trans-expr-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-EXPR-001 (**RNA-seq expression quantification** тАФ TPM / FPKM / RPKM + quantile normalization). **Transcriptome / RNA-seq family** sibling of the anchor [[differential-expression]] тЖТ NEW concept [[expression-quantification]] (a distinct quantification/normalization method, upstream of the DE test). `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculateTPM` / `CalculateFPKM` / `QuantileNormalize`: **TPM** `(X_i/l_i)/╬г(X_j/l_j)┬╖10тБ╢` (length-normalize into RPK **then** rescale so each sample **sums to exactly 10тБ╢** тАФ the invariant RPKM lacks; Wagner 2012, Zhao/Ye/Stanton 2020); **FPKM/RPKM** `X_i┬╖10тБ╣/(l_i┬╖N)` (per-kb + per-million-reads; RPKMтЙбFPKM formula; `TPM=FPKM/╬г FPKM┬╖10тБ╢`); **quantile normalization** (Bolstad 2003 тАФ sort each column, set each rank to the cross-column rank mean, re-place; **tied values get the mean of the rank means they'd span**). Oracles: TPM A(10,2000)/B(20,4000)/C(30,1000) тЖТ **(125000,125000,750000)** sum 10тБ╢; FPKM X=1000,l=2000,N=10тБ╢ тЖТ **500**; quantile C1=(5,2,3,4)/C2=(4,1,4,2)/C3=(3,4,6,8) тЖТ C2's two tied `4`s тЖТ **5.166тАж** (mean of top-two rank means 4.666тАж/5.666тАж). Corner cases: all-zero counts тЖТ TPM 0/0 undefined тЖТ emit 0; non-positive length/N тЖТ FPKM 0; empty тЖТ empty. Two source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (all-zero TPM тЖТ 0; effective length = annotated length). Classic count-normalization, **not** an effective-length fragment model (kallisto/salmon) or TMM/median-of-ratios size factors (edgeR/DESeq2). TPM/RPKM are within-sample relative measures тАФ misused across samples (Zhao 2020). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[trans-splice-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-SPLICE-001 (**RNA-seq alternative / differential splicing** тАФ event classification + Percent-Spliced-In / PSI). **Transcriptome / RNA-seq family** sibling of the anchor [[differential-expression]] тЖТ NEW concept [[alternative-splicing-psi]] (read-quantification of splicing usage тАФ **distinct from** the genomic splice-site motif predictors [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] / [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]] / [[gene-structure-prediction-intron-exon]]). `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculatePSI` / `DetectAlternativeSplicing`: **PSI** `╬и = I/(I+S)` (inclusion / (inclusion+exclusion) reads; Wang 2008, PMC3330053, SUPPA2) with opt-in **rMATS length-normalized** `╧И╠В = (I/lс╡в)/(I/lс╡в + S/lтВЫ)` (Shen 2014, effective isoform lengths) тЖТ default unnormalized, switches to rMATS when both lengths > 0; **╬ФPSI** = splicing-level differential readout. **Five canonical AS classes** (Wang 2008 = rMATS codes): SkippedExon (SE), RetainedIntron (RI), AlternativeFivePrimeSS (A5SS, alternative **donor** = moving 3тА▓/END boundary of upstream exon), AlternativeThreePrimeSS (A3SS, alternative **acceptor** = moving 5тА▓/START boundary of downstream exon), MutuallyExclusiveExons (MXE); an event needs **тЙе2 isoforms** of one gene. Oracles: (I=80,S=20) тЖТ **0.80**; (80,20,lс╡в=200,lтВЫ=100) тЖТ **0.6666тАж**. Corner cases: **0/0 тЖТ NaN**, S=0 тЖТ PSI 1, I=0 тЖТ PSI 0, `0 тЙд PSI тЙд 1`, <2 isoforms тЖТ no event. Two source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (length normalization opt-in; forward strand / ascending coords). The splicing-level counterpart to the gene-level [[differential-expression]] тАФ a gene can be differentially spliced without changing total expression. Read-count ratio + coordinate comparison, **not** the full rMATS/SUPPA2 replicate statistics. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[splice-predict-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit SPLICE-PREDICT-001 (**gene structure prediction тАФ intron/exon**), the **composite / umbrella** of the **splicing** family тЖТ NEW concept [[gene-structure-prediction-intron-exon]]. Assembles the two boundary detectors into a whole split-gene model: find donors (`GT/GU`) + acceptors (`AG`) тЖТ **pair** into introns under the **GT-AG rule** (Breathnach & Chambon 1981 `MAG|GURAGU` / `(Y)nNCAG|G`; Burge 1999 "each donor pairs with exactly one acceptor") bounded by `minIntronLength` (default 60) / `maxIntronLength` тЖТ **greedy non-overlapping** selection тЖТ exons = the gaps тЖТ **type** each exon (Initial/Internal/Terminal/Single, Gilbert 1978) + **phase** = `(╬г preceding exon lengths) mod 3` (Alberts 2002) тЖТ emit **spliced sequence** + **overall score** = mean of per-intron `(donor+acceptor)/2`, [0,1]. Datasets: D1 two-exon 153 nt тЖТ 1 intron/2 exons/70-nt spliced, D2 single-exon 50 nt тЖТ Single, D3 empty тЖТ 0/0. Corner cases: 30-bp introns excluded by default min=60, no sites тЖТ single-exon, DNA TтЙбU. All 4 assumptions RESOLVED (greedy=design decision, phase=trivial, overall-score=definition, **default branch-point 0.3 constant removed**). No source contradictions.
- [[variant-annot-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-ANNOT-001 (**variant annotation** тАФ VEP-style functional consequence + Sequence-Ontology IMPACT). The **interpretation / annotation** member of the variant-analysis family тЖТ NEW concept [[variant-effect-annotation-vep]] (downstream of variant calling [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]], orthogonal to pathogenicity/tier classification). Ensembl **OverlapConsequence predicate system**: `Constants.pm` consequenceтЖТIMPACTтЖТrank table (**IMPACT stored on the term, not computed**; frameshift HIGH / missense MODERATE / synonymous LOW / intron MODIFIER) + `VariationEffect.pm` peptide predicates; **most-severe = lowest rank** (McLaren 2016 "most specific term under any parent"). The coding engine **translates ref/alt codons** through [[genetic-code-translation]] (NCBI Standard code table 1) and compares peptides: `synonymous` (ref_pep==alt_pep, no `X`, not stop_retained) / `missense` (differ, same length; false if start_lost/stop_lost/stop_gained/partial_codon) / `stop_gained` (alt gains `*`) / `stop_lost` (ref loses `*`) / **`frameshift` purely length-based `|altтИТref| mod 3 тЙа 0`** / inframe ins-del (├Ч3). Precedence stop_gained>missense, start_lost(rank 7)>coding-substitution. Oracles GAAтЖТGTA missense/MODERATE ┬╖ TTAтЖТTTG synonymous/LOW ┬╖ CAAтЖТTAA stop_gained/HIGH ┬╖ TAAтЖТCAA stop_lost/HIGH ┬╖ ATGтЖТATC start_lost/HIGH ┬╖ ACтЖТA frameshift ┬╖ AтЖТATTT inframe_insertion. Sources McLaren 2016 (PMC4893825) + Ensembl Constants.pm/VariationEffect.pm (release/110) + NCBI gc.prt + Sequence Ontology (Eilbeck 2005). Two assumptions (Standard code table 1 only; single-codon SNV peptide comparison). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[variant-call-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-CALL-001 (**variant calling** тАФ SNP/insertion/deletion detection from a referenceтЖФquery alignment + transition/transversion + Ti/Tv). The **calling / detection** member of the variant-analysis family тЖТ NEW concept [[germline-variant-calling-snp-indel]] (**upstream of** annotation [[variant-effect-annotation-vep]]; the germline referenceтЖФquery counterpart of the oncology tumor-vs-normal caller [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]]). `CallVariantsFromAlignment` runs `SequenceAligner.GlobalAlign(reference,query)` and walks aligned columns: **SNP** (both bases differ), **Insertion** (`-`/base), **Deletion** (base/`-`), 0-based `Position` + `"-"` gap sentinel (in-memory model; VCF padding + 1-based POS only in serialized `ToVcfLines`). SNPs classified case-insensitively **Transition** (AтЖФG, CтЖФT) vs **Transversion** (AтЖФC/AтЖФT/GтЖФC/GтЖФT); **Ti/Tv = #Ti/#Tv**, undefined `#Tv=0` тЖТ **0** by convention; non-SNP тЖТ `Other`. Sources VCFv4.3 (samtools/hts-specs тАФ REF/ALT/POS + padding-base grammar, ┬з1.1 `GтЖТA` SNP / `GTCтЖТG` 2-base del / `GTCтЖТGTCT` 1-base ins) + Danecek 2011 (VCF classes) + Tan 2015 (normalized тЯ║ left-aligned+parsimonious) + Collins & Jukes 1994 (transitional bias, Ti rate > Tv rate). Three assumptions (gap-sentinel internal rep; indels **not** normalized тЖТ position-only implementation-dependence in repeats; Ti/Tv zero тЖТ 0). Alignment-based (single query vs reference), **not** a read-pileup genotype caller. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
