- [[variant-indel-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-INDEL-001 (**indel detection** тАФ `FindInsertions` / `FindDeletions`, the insertion/deletion facet of the aligned-column caller). **Enriches** (does not fork) the concept [[germline-variant-calling-snp-indel]] тАФ the indel facet of the same VARIANT-CALL-001 caller, not a separate algorithm. `FindInsertions`/`FindDeletions` are **filters over `CallVariants`** returning only their class (insertion column `-`/base, deletion column base/`-`); a multi-base indel = **consecutive per-base indel columns**. Load-bearing claim = the **directional length invariant**: **insertion тЗТ ALT longer than REF** (VCF `CтЖТCA`), **deletion тЗТ REF longer than ALT** (VCF `TCтЖТT`); VCFv4.3 ┬з1.1 `GTCтЖТG,GTCT` shows both anchored at `G`. Normalization theory (Tan 2015 **normalized тЯ║ left-aligned + parsimonious**; Algorithm 1 = suffix-then-prefix trimming) documents the ASM: the caller reports the indel at the `GlobalAlign` column with **no** normalization pass, so **position** is implementation-dependent in repeats/low-complexity only (PharmCAT `AATGAтЖТA`@97740414 тЗТ `GATGAтЖТG`@97740410, same count/type), **not** counts or types. Reference oracles: `ATGCAT`тЖТ`ATGTCAT` = 1-base insertion `T`; `ATGTCAT`тЖТ`ATGCAT` = 1-base deletion `T`; minimal_representation CFTR p.F508del `(7,117199646,CTT,-)тЖТ(...,ATCT,A)` + BRCA2 `(13,32914438,T,-)тЖТ(...,GT,G)` confirm deletion тЗТ len(REF)>len(ALT) + left-anchor padding. Three assumptions (gap-sentinel internal rep; indels not normalized тЖТ position-only in repeats; 0-based in-memory Position). Sources VCFv4.3 + Tan 2015 (PMID 25701572) + minimal_representation (Minikel) + PharmCAT. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[variant-snp-001-evidence]] тАФ evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-SNP-001 (**SNP detection** тАФ `FindSnps` / `FindSnpsDirect`, the single-nucleotide-substitution facet of the aligned-column caller). **Enriches** (does not fork) the concept [[germline-variant-calling-snp-indel]] тАФ the SNP facet of the same VARIANT-CALL-001 caller, not a separate algorithm (mirrors how [[variant-indel-001-evidence]] folded in the indel facet). Two entry points, **substitution columns only** (no indels): **`FindSnps`** = alignment-based filter over the caller (keeps columns where both bases differ, `Type=SNP`); **`FindSnpsDirect`** = positional / **Hamming-style** тАФ over two **equal-length** sequences it enumerates exactly the **Hamming-mismatch positions** (Acharya 2017, PMC5410656) and the SNP count equals the **Hamming distance**. Each SNP: `Position=i` (0-based mismatched index), `ReferenceAllele=ref[i]`, `AlternateAllele=query[i]`, `ref[i]тЙаquery[i]` (**REF==ALT is not a variant**). Load-bearing scope claim = the **equal-length precondition**: `FindSnpsDirect` on unequal-length inputs compares only the **common prefix** `min(ref.Length,query.Length)` тАФ the trailing region is indel territory (VARIANT-INDEL-001), never a SNP. Identical sequences тЖТ 0 SNPs (Hamming distance 0); comparison + Ti/Tv classification **case-insensitive** (VCFv4.3 REF alphabet A,C,G,T,N). Oracles: `ATGC`тЖТ`ATTC`={2} (GтЖТT) ┬╖ `AAAA`тЖТ`TGTA`={0,1,2} ┬╖ VCFv4.3 ┬з1.1 simple SNP `GтЖТA`@14370. Two assumptions (unequal-length тЖТ common prefix; 0-based in-memory Position). Sources VCFv4.3 + Wikipedia/Futuyma Transversion + Acharya 2017 (PMC5410656, Hamming) + Collins & Jukes 1994 (transitional bias). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.

## Concepts

- [[three-front-doors]] тАФ one algorithm engine exposed through skills, the C# API, and MCP, with identical results.
- [[skill-layer]] тАФ the Agent-Skill routing + discipline layer that keeps 427 tool schemas out of the model's context.
- [[layered-architecture]] тАФ the strict up-only dependency layering (Levels 0тАУ4) enforced by architecture tests.
- [[scientific-rigor]] тАФ runtime honesty: `LimitationPolicy`, tool-only computation, provenance on every result.
- [[validation-and-testing]] тАФ 22k+ tests across ten methodologies plus the per-unit validation campaign.
- [[validation-findings-disposition]] тАФ the A/B/C/D triage governance process for validation findings, with green-washing detection and the spec-not-impl remedy.
- [[operating-envelope-and-limitation-policy]] тАФ the validated operating envelope + the `LimitationPolicy` runtime guard (Strict/Moderate/Permissive, minimum-access-mode table) and the irreducible/data-blocked/scope limitation taxonomy.
- [[property-based-testing]] тАФ P0 methodology (FsCheck): hundreds of generated inputs checked against expressible invariants (R/S/I/M/P/RT/D); 258/258.
- [[metamorphic-testing]] тАФ P0 methodology: metamorphic relations across runs (SUB/MON/INV/SYM/COMP/SHIFT) that solve the oracle problem; 258/258, ~200+ relations.
- [[fuzzing]] тАФ P2 methodology: random/malformed/boundary input for clean-failure; parsers the hot target; zeroтЖТ258/258.
- [[snapshot-testing]] тАФ P1 methodology (Verify): golden-master `.verified.txt` regression capture; the least-complete methodology at 37/255.
- [[algebraic-testing]] тАФ P1 methodology: explicit algebraic laws (identity/associativity/involution/round-tripтАж); 89 applicable + 169 not-applicable.
- [[architecture-testing]] тАФ P2 methodology (ArchUnitNET): 22 IL-level module rules enforcing the [[layered-architecture]] Dependency Rule; scales by module not algorithm.
- [[differential-testing]] тАФ P2 methodology: two independent implementations cross-checked (ALT/BRUTE/REF/DUAL); 107/255.
- [[combinatorial-testing]] тАФ P3 methodology: minimal pairwise parameter-interaction coverage; 193/255 + 65 not-applicable.
- [[characterization-testing]] тАФ P3 methodology: golden-master pinning of behaviour before refactors (invariance, not correctness); on-demand.
- [[build-quality-gate]] тАФ the build-time static-analysis gate: SonarAnalyzer ratcheted to blocking under `TreatWarningsAsErrors`, fix-or-silence, review-not-blind-fix.
- [[test-unit-registry]] тАФ the area-prefixed Test Unit ID scheme and per-unit record behind the validation effort.
- [[definition-of-done]] тАФ the six-criterion acceptance bar (TestSpec, tests, тЙе80% coverage, edge cases, CI, evidence) each unit must clear.
- [[algorithm-validation-evidence]] тАФ the templated per-unit `docs/Evidence/` artifact pattern (sources, worked-example dataset, deviations) behind the "Evidence documented" DoD criterion.
- [[global-alignment-needleman-wunsch]] тАФ the canonical DP global-alignment algorithm (`GlobalAlign`): linear-gap recurrence, O(nm), traceback, affine-as-extension.
- [[multiple-sequence-alignment]] тАФ aligning 3+ sequences (NP-complete): Seqeron's star (`MultipleAlign`), iterative-refinement (MUSCLE), and consistency (T-Coffee) aligners; sum-of-pairs + consensus.
- [[local-alignment-smith-waterman]] тАФ the canonical DP local-alignment algorithm (`LocalAlign`): zero-floor linear-gap recurrence, 0/0 border, optimum from the max cell, traceback-to-zero тЖТ best local subsequences; linear-gap only (affine/WтВЦ not implemented).
- [[semi-global-alignment-fitting]] тАФ ends-free "glocal" alignment: fitting/query-in-reference variant (Rosalind SIMS); NW recurrence with free reference end gaps, traceback from max of last row.
- [[alignment-statistics]] тАФ post-alignment metrics: percent identity/similarity/gaps (EMBOSS/BLAST convention, denominator includes gaps, positive-score тЗТ similar) and srspair three-line markup.
- [[coding-potential-hexamer-score]] тАФ CPAT hexamer usage-bias coding-potential score: mean of ln(coding/noncoding) over in-frame hexamers (wordSize 6/step 3), sign convention, ┬▒1 pseudo-scores; Fickett TESTCODE as not-implemented alternative.
- [[prokaryotic-gene-prediction-rbs]] тАФ annotation-layer prokaryotic ORF-based gene prediction + Shine-Dalgarno RBS detection (ANNOT-GENE-001, `GenomeAnnotator.PredictGenes` / `FindRibosomeBindingSitesBothStrands` / `ScanStrandForShineDalgarno`): both-strand startтЖТstop CDS finding with `protein_length` excluding the stop, and SD consensus `AGGAGG` (+ substrings) matched upstream of a start at an aligned spacing тИИ [minDistance,maxDistance] (score = motifLen/6). Core correctness = the reverse-strand SD mapping `forwardPosition = len тИТ hit.position тИТ motifLen` (scan the reverse complement, since the SD is an mRNA feature); anti-SD 3' 16S tail `YACCUCCUUA`, ~8 nt location, 5 nt literature optimum (Chen 1994). `alternative_to` the Analysis-layer six-frame [[open-reading-frame-detection]] (not contract-equivalent); the strand/spacing-aware counterpart to the bare `AGGAGG` row in [[regulatory-element-detection]]. Validation report [[annot-gene-001-report]].
- [[relative-synonymous-codon-usage]] тАФ RSCU (Sharp & Li 1986) codon-usage-bias measure: n_i┬╖x/╬гx normalization, 1.0=no bias, bounded [0,n_i], ╬г-over-family=n_i invariant; pooled counts, sense codons only; base anchor of the codon-usage family (vs CAI's max-normalization).
- [[codon-adaptation-index]] тАФ CAI (Sharp & Li 1987) whole-gene codon-bias / expression-proxy score in [0,1]: geometric mean of relative adaptiveness w=f/max_synonym_f, low-value-sensitive, stop excluded; dual include/exclude-Met/Trp mode (exclude can give L=0тЖТ0); E. coli oracles; Seqeron deviation = 1e-6 zero-freq clamp (vs Sharp & Li's 0.5 reference-table pseudocount); one level above RSCU.
- [[rare-codon-analysis]] тАФ codon-usage family's *localization/diagnostic* unit (`FindRareCodons` + cluster addendum): a codon is rare when its per-family frequency < threshold (default 0.15), reports position/AA/frequency (E. coli AGA 0.04/AGG 0.02/CGA 0.06/CUA 0.04); addendum adds two published cluster methods тАФ Clarke & Clark 2008 %MinMax (18-codon window, signed %Min/%Max тИИ[тИТ100,+100], rare clusters = negative peaks) and Chartier 2012 Sherlocc (7-codon window, тЙе4 of 7 freqтЙдthreshold "slow" positions = a rare-codon cluster); single-codon-AA contributes 0 to %MinMax (no NaN), overlapping windows merged; feeds [[codon-optimization]]'s AvoidRareCodons; oracles тИТ86.36/+100/+36.47% and 7├ЧAGAтЖТ1 cluster; deviations None.
- [[codon-usage-comparison]] тАФ codon-usage family's *raw* end (`CalculateCodonUsage` + `CompareCodonUsage`): unnormalized codon-count table (non-overlapping triplets, TтЖТU, drop partial codon, Dictionary<codon,int>, ╬гcounts=total invariant) + Total Variation Distance similarity `1тИТ╬г|fтВБтИТfтВВ|/2 тИИ [0,1]` between two codon-frequency distributions; proven identity 1.0 / symmetry / range [0,1] / disjointтЖТ0 / partial-overlap-exact properties; emptyтЖТ0, TVD-not-cosine deliberate metric choice; Kazusa-verified organism tables; shares RSCU's counting primitive, the distribution-comparison op none of the bias measures provide.
- [[codon-optimization]] тАФ codon-usage family's CDS-*rewriting* operation (`OptimizeSequence`): synonymous substitution to improve host expression; five strategies (MaximizeCAI / BalancedOptimization 40-60% GC / HarmonizeExpression=Mignon 2018 / AvoidRareCodons / MinimizeSecondaryтЖТReduceSecondaryStructure); invariants protein-preservation + Met/AUG & Trp/UGG fixed + stop preserved + CAIтИИ(0,1]; RNA notation, TтЖТU, trim-to-codon, 1e-6 CAI clamp; E. coli/yeast/human preferred-codon fixtures; actuator to RSCU/CAI/ENC's measurement.
- [[effective-number-of-codons]] тАФ ENC/Nc (Wright 1990) reference-free whole-gene codon-bias measure in [20,61]: reciprocal of codon homozygosity F╠В=(n┬╖╬гp┬▓тИТ1)/(nтИТ1) aggregated by degeneracy class (Nc=2+9/F╠ВтВВ+1/F╠ВтВГ+5/F╠ВтВД+3/F╠ВтВЖ); 20=max bias / 61=uniform, unbiasedтЖТ61, no-bias-simтЖТ40.5; Ile absentтЖТ(F╠ВтВВ+F╠ВтВД)/2 fallback, overshoot re-adjusts to 61; reference-free counterpart of CAI; one assumption = non-source-prescribed lower clamp at 20.
- [[genetic-code-translation]] тАФ the codon-family's foundational table: `GeneticCode` codonтЖТamino-acid map (64 codons тЖТ 20 AA + 3 stops), 4 of NCBI's 33 tables (Standard/1, Vertebrate-Mito/2, Yeast-Mito/3, Bacterial-Plastid/11) as static singletons; `Translate`/`IsStartCodon`/`IsStopCodon`/`GetCodonsForAminoAcid`; DNAтЖФRNA TтЖТU + case-insensitive + stopтЖТ`*` + lenтЙа3тЖТArgumentException; Met/AUG & Trp/UGG single-codon fixed points (the wтЙб1 fact behind CAI/optimization); IUPAC ambiguity codonтЖТ`'X'` (a flagged divergence from the Evidence doc's promised exception). The table [[open-reading-frame-detection|ORF detection]] and [[codon-optimization]] read. Also covers the **whole-sequence `Translator` layer** (TRANS-PROT-001 + TRANS-SIXFRAME-001): framed / six-frame translation + genetic-code-parameterized STARTтЖТSTOP ORF finding, verified against the UniProt-P01308 insulin B-chain oracle; six-frame reverse-frame numbering follows the **Biopython independent-offset** convention (тИТk = RC offset kтИТ1), the documented alternative to EMBOSS phase-locked.
- [[repetitive-element-detection]] тАФ repeats/tandem family anchor: tandem (head-to-tail, тЙе2 copies, primitive unit), inverted (W┬╖G┬╖W╠Дс┤┐ / zero-gap palindrome, IUPACpal), and RepeatMasker-class assignment; ClassifyRepeat = exact-substring containment, not Smith-Waterman homology.
- [[consensus-sequence]] тАФ assembly CONSENSUS family anchor: column-wise majority/threshold consensus (Biopython dumb_consensus rule) тАФ gaps skipped, emit iff unique max and freq тЙе threshold else ambiguous, tieтЖТambiguous, all-gapтЖТN no div-by-zero; N/0.5 parameterized defaults; shared with MSA consensus step.
- [[consensus-from-alignment]] тАФ Motif-Analysis consensus-from-a-multiple-alignment (MOTIF-CONS-001, `MotifFinder.CreateConsensusFromAlignment`): pure most-frequent (plurality) column consensus over equal-length aligned strings, deterministic alphabetical tie-break (A<C<G<T), no threshold (always emits); Rosalind CONS `ATGCAACT` oracle; `alternative_to` the threshold/tieтЖТambiguous assembly [[consensus-sequence]], motif-family sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]].
- [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] тАФ MotifFinder degenerate-consensus unit (MOTIF-GENERATE-001, `MotifFinder.GenerateConsensus`): collapses equal-length aligned columns into an IUPAC-ambiguity-coded string тАФ per column keep every base with `count > 0.25┬╖n` (strict `>`), emit the NC-IUB 1984 symbol for that base set (R/Y/S/W/K/M, B/D/H/V, N), no-pass fallback тЖТ most-frequent (alphabetical tie); DECIPHER threshold-consensus family + NC-IUB/UCSC/Wikipedia bijective setтЖТsymbol table; `A,A,G,G,C`тЖТR / strict-`>` boundary / four-wayтЖТA-fallback oracles; `alternative_to` the plurality [[consensus-from-alignment]], degenerate sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]].
- [[regulatory-element-detection]] тАФ Motif-Discovery regulatory-element unit (MOTIF-REGULATORY-001, `KnownMotifs` catalog scan): matches a **fixed, cited catalog of 12 canonical regulatory consensus elements** (TATA/тИТ10/тИТ35/CAAT/GC promoter boxes, Kozak + Shine-Dalgarno translation signals, poly(A), and E-box/AP-1/NF-╬║B/CREB TF sites) against a DNA sequence, reporting each occurrence's Name/Pattern/Sequence at its 0-based start; mixes exact and one IUPAC-degenerate (E-box `CANNTG`) match; anchors the AP-1 corrected-consensus regression (`TGAGTCA`тЖТ`TGACTCA`, `AATGAGTCAGG`тЖТ0 hits); two source-backed representative-site assumptions (NF-╬║B `GGGACTTTCC`, Kozak `GCCGCCACCATGG`); the curated-biological-catalog specialization of the generic exact [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the generation-direction [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]]; the scored тИТ10/тИТ35 alternative is [[promoter-detection]].
- [[promoter-detection]] тАФ Annotation-layer scored тИТ10/тИТ35 promoter motif detector (ANNOT-PROM-001, `GenomeAnnotator.FindPromoterMotifs`): scans DNA for the prokaryotic тИТ35 box `TTGACA` and тИТ10/Pribnow box `TATAAT` plus derived prefix-5/suffix-5/prefix-4 variants, scoring each hit `╬г matched-position p / ╬г all-6 consensus p тИИ [0,1]` from the E. coli position-specific frequencies (тИТ35 sum 373, тИТ10 sum 412); a full box scores 1.0, partial variants 0.665тАУ0.855; `position` is a **0-based string index** (not the TSS-relative negative coordinate), `type` тИИ {`-35 box`,`-10 box`}, тИТ35/тИТ10 scanned independently (no pairing). Declared scope limits: **17 bp spacing not enforced**, **exact-substring not PWM/HMM/mismatch-tolerant** тАФ motif annotation, not full promoter prediction; no null guard. The `alternative_to` the exact-hexamer catalog scan [[regulatory-element-detection]] (same two boxes, no scoring). Validation report [[annot-prom-001-report]].
- [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] тАФ Motif-Discovery de-novo unit (MOTIF-DISCOVER-001, `MotifFinder.DiscoverMotifs`): finds **unknown** over-represented motifs by enumerating every length-`k` k-mer, counting overlapping occurrences, and ranking by observed/expected enrichment `Count/((NтИТk+1)/4^k)` under a zero-order i.i.d. uniform background (Compeau & Pevzner); deterministic exact single-pass, 0-based positions; `ATGC` in `ATGCATGCATGC` k=4 тЖТ 768/9тЙИ85.333, `AAA` in `AAAAAAAAAA` k=3 тЖТ 64.0 oracles; `k>N`тЖТempty, minCount presentation-only, zero-order-only + no-p-value simplifications; the de-novo inverse of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and distinct from the [[consensus-from-alignment]] plurality consensus.
- [[shared-motifs]] тАФ Motif-Discovery cross-sequence unit (MOTIF-SHARED-001, `FindSharedMotifs`): the van Helden / RSAT oligo-analysis **"matching sequences"** quorum тАФ enumerate every fixed-`k` exact word across a *set* of sequences and report each word present in тЙе `minSequences` of them (each carrying its `SequenceIndices` set + `Prevalence`=matching/total); a within-sequence repeat counts **1** (presence/absence, not multiplicity); exact-word only (no degenerate/substitution); the cross-sequence sibling of the single-sequence O/E [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] and `alternative_to` the fixed-k-quorum-vs-single-longest LCSM framing of [[longest-common-substring]] (returns all qualifying words, not one longest present in all).
- [[approximate-pattern-matching-mismatches]] тАФ pattern-matching PAT-APPROX family anchor (PAT-APPROX-003): Hamming-distance **approximate matching** тАФ a `k`-mer appears with тЙд`d` mismatches when `HammingDistance(P,P')тЙдd` (BA1H); `Count_d`/`FindApproximateOccurrences` scan windows, `FindFrequentKmersWithMismatches` (BA1I) ranks `k`-mers by their **d-neighborhood** (Hamming-ball) tally so the winner need not occur exactly, `Neighbors` (BA1N) enumerates the ball (includes identity), `FindBestMatch` returns the leftmost min-Hamming window; oracles {GATG,ATGC,ATGT} count 5, {6,7,26,27,78}, Count_1=4, ACG/1тЖТ10; d=0 degenerates to exact so it is the mismatch-tolerant `alternative_to` [[k-mer-positions]] and the fuzzy sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] / de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]]; substitution-only (no indels тАФ that is the alignment family), deviations none.
- [[coverage-depth-calculation]] тАФ assembly COVER family anchor: per-base sequencing depth over a reference (count of placed reads spanning each position, exact); average depth = ╬гdepth/G = Lander-Waterman C=LN/G, breadth = covered/G = 1тИТe^тИТc; boundary-clip + empty-input rules; ACGTTGCAATтЖТ1.5/1.0 oracle; Poisson (e^тИТc gap) as a property check only; read placement (minOverlap best-match) out of scope.
- [[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]] тАФ assembly DBG family anchor: k-mer graph (distinct (k-1)-mers = nodes, each k-mer = one prefixтЖТsuffix edge, directed multigraph) + Eulerian-walk reconstruction (balanced/semi-balanced, Euler theorems 8.1/8.2, O(|E|) Hierholzer); spelling = path[0]+last char of each node; unique-walk oracles only (AAABBBA, a_longтАж, to_everyтАж k=4, ATGGCGTGCA); repeat/gap/error тЖТ non-Eulerian; walk-selection unspecified so exact asserts on unique-walk inputs; OLC is the alternative formulation.
- [[overlap-layout-consensus-assembly]] тАФ assembly OLC family anchor: the three-stage Overlap-Layout-Consensus paradigm (`FindAllOverlaps` + `AssembleOLC`) тАФ overlap graph (read=node, edge on longest suffix-of-A/prefix-of-B тЙе threshold), Layout = Hamiltonian path (NP-complete) + transitive reduction + non-branching contigs, Consensus = majority vote; GTACGTACGAT 12-edge / 5-overlap-tiling oracles; suffix-tree O(N+a) vs all-pairs O(N┬▓); NP-complete/repeat-split/greedy-suboptimal failure modes; identity-1.0 + empty-input assumptions; Hamiltonian/overlap-graph alternative to DBG's Eulerian/k-mer formulation.
- [[contig-merge-overlap-collapse]] тАФ assembly MERGE family anchor: suffixтАУprefix overlap collapse primitive (`MergeContigs`) behind greedy SCS and OLC layout; overlap = length-l suffix of X = prefix of Y, longest match reported, collapse keeps one copy so |merge|=|c1|+|c2|тИТl; overlap 0 / out-of-range тЖТ plain concatenation; BAA+AABтЖТBAAB, chainтЖТAAABBBA oracles; caller-trusts-length + out-of-rangeтЖТconcat API-contract assumptions; overlap-based sibling of DBG's k-mer/Eulerian formulation.
- [[scaffolding]] тАФ assembly SCAFFOLD family anchor: joining ordered contigs into a scaffold, adjacent contigs separated by `N`-runs of length = the (upstream) inter-contig distance estimate (ABySS 2.0 rule); positive gap `g` тЖТ `g`├Ч`N`, scaffold length = ╬г|contig|+╬гgap; non-positive (zero/negative) estimate тЖТ AGP unknown-size default 100 N (negative = overlap, unresolved here); each contig in тЙд1 scaffold, unlinked тЖТ singleton; parameterized fill char; ACGTNNNTTGGNNCCAA / AAAA+100N+TTTT oracles; downstream of DBG/OLC/merge, hands off to contig-merge on the negative-gap overlap case; 100-constant source-backed (INSDC), only the fall-back-not-resolve decision is assumed.
- [[assembly-statistics]] тАФ assembly STATS family anchor: contiguity/QC summary metrics over contig lengths (read-only, downstream of DBG/OLC/merge/scaffold) тАФ Nx = shortest length covering тЙеx% (largest-first, inclusive тЙе; N50/N90), Lx = the matching contig count, N90 тЙд N50 / L90 тЙе L50, auN = ╬гLс╡в┬▓/╬гLт▒╝ (area under Nx curve, more stable than N50); + totals/largest/smallest/GC and 0-based inclusive N-run gaps; Miller 2010 + Wikipedia + QUAST + Heng Li 2020; Assembly A N50 70/L50 2, auN 73.333 oracles; emptyтЖТzeros (not None) + upper-median-not-source-derived assumptions.
- [[quality-trimming-running-sum]] тАФ assembly TRIM family anchor: BWA/cutadapt running-sum quality trimming тАФ subtract cutoff from each Phred quality, take partial sums to the 3' end, cut at the minimum (= BWA argmax of accumulated thresholdтИТq, with `s<0` early break + `BWA_MIN_RDLEN=35` floor); Phred+33 decode (Cock 2010); `KI;<)(,%#$`@thr 10тЖТfirst 4 bases oracle; threshold<1 disables / all-high unchanged / all-low dropped / good-base-among-bad refinement; both-end pass + downstream minLength filter as assumptions; read-QC preprocessing upstream of correction/DBG/OLC.
- [[kmer-spectrum-error-correction]] тАФ assembly CORRECT family anchor: two-sided k-mer-spectrum read error correction (Musket/Quake) тАФ trusted (multiplicity > cut-off) vs untrusted k-mers, base trusted if covered by any trusted k-mer, unique alternative making all covering k-mers trusted, ambiguity/no-setтЖТunchanged; substitution-only (count+length preserved); kmerSize=15/minKmerFrequency=2 non-behavioral defaults.
- [[centromere-analysis]] тАФ chromosome centromere/alpha-satellite family anchor (second Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeCentromere` + 4 additive detectors тАФ Levan 1964 q/p arm-ratio classes (Metacentric тЙд1.7 / Submetacentric тЙд3.0 / Subtelocentric <7.0 / Acrocentric тЙе7.0 / Telocentric p=0); alpha-satellite-specific `DetectAlphaSatellite`/`FindCenpBBoxes` (171-bp tandem period ┬▒5, AT>0.5, 17-bp CENP-B box `YTTCGTTGGAARCGGGA`, no embedded monomer); `DetectHigherOrderRepeat` (HOR period = smallest k with monomers k apart тЙе95% identical across тЙе90%, intra-HOR 50тАУ70% vs inter-HOR 97тАУ100%); `AssignSuprachromosomalFamily` (bundled CC0 Dfam ALR/ALRa=A/ALRb=B, SF3 pentameric/SF4 monomeric/{SF1,SF2} dimeric/SF5 irregular); base AlphaSatelliteContent is density-heuristic-not-specific + SF1/SF2-unresolved (non-redistributable consensus library) limitations.
- [[base-composition]] тАФ foundational sequence-composition tally (SEQ-COMPOSITION-001): exact **nucleotide** partition of Length into A/T/G/C/U/`CountN`/`CountOther` (seven counts sum to Length), **GC content** `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C+U)` тИИ [0,1] (Biopython `gc_fraction`, empty тЗТ 0), and **amino-acid** residue counts over the 20 IUPAC letters; case-insensitive, non-canonical/degenerate codes tracked separately (not folded into A/T/G/C/U) тАФ the documented assumption vs Biopython (which counts S toward GC / W toward denominator), agreeing exactly over {A,T,G,C,U}; the magnitude/fraction view whose *asymmetry* counterpart is the sibling [[nucleotide-composition-skew]], base layer under [[cpg-island-detection]] dinucleotide O/E, [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]] window entropy, and the GC constraints in [[taqman-probe-design-rules]]/[[codon-optimization]]. Records [[seq-composition-001-evidence]].
- [[nucleotide-composition-skew]] тАФ strand compositional-skew family (Lobry 1996): **AT skew** `(AтИТT)/(A+T)` + **GC skew** `(GтИТC)/(G+C)`, both bounded [тИТ1,+1] (AT skew `тИТ1тЗФA=0`/`+1тЗФT=0`); zero-denominator тЗТ **0.0** (Biopython `GC_skew` convention), case-insensitive counting, ambiguous/non-canonical bases ignored; biological meaning = replication-strand asymmetry, cumulative-skew sign flip locates the origin/terminus (Charneski 2011: Firmicute AT skew from selection, not mutation); AT-skew member validated by [[seq-atskew-001-evidence]] (SEQ-ATSKEW-001), GC-skew member (`gc-skew`) not yet ingested; single-base cousin of the dinucleotide CpG O/E in [[cpg-island-detection]] and the GC-skew unit flagged in [[centromere-analysis]].
- [[dinucleotide-relative-abundance]] тАФ dinucleotide composition & the **Karlin genomic signature** (SEQ-DINUC-001): the 2-mer generalization of [[base-composition]] and the general case of the CpG O/E in [[cpg-island-detection]]. Two outputs over the `NтИТ1` adjacent base-steps тАФ **dinucleotide frequency** `f_XY = count/(NтИТ1)` and the **relative-abundance odds ratio** `╧Б_XY = f_XY/(f_X┬╖f_Y)` (`CalculateDinucleotideRatios`; `╧Б=1` no-bias independence baseline, Karlin & Burge over/under thresholds `╧БтЙе1.23`/`╧БтЙд0.78` documentation-only); CpG O/E is the `CG`-specialized case, differing only by the `N` vs `NтИТ1` normalization (`N/(NтИТ1)тЖТ1` long sequences, a documented modeling choice). Exact-rational oracles for `ATGCGCGT` (GC/CG ╧Б=64/21, AT ╧Б=32/7, TG/GT ╧Б=32/21); div-by-zero guard тЖТ ratio 0 when a constituent base is absent, `U` counted as a fifth base for RNA, case-insensitive. Also validates the codon-frequency metric owned by [[codon-usage-comparison]]/[[seq-codon-freq-001-evidence]]. Records [[seq-dinuc-001-evidence]].
- [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]] тАФ composite **GC-analysis** unit's distinct layer (SEQ-GC-ANALYSIS-001, `GcAnalysisResult`): bundles the whole-sequence scalars OverallGcContent `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C)├Ч100` (percentage ├Ч100, [[base-composition]] carries the `[0,1]` fraction), OverallGcSkew `(GтИТC)/(G+C)`, OverallAtSkew `(AтИТT)/(A+T)` ([[nucleotide-composition-skew]]) with a **sliding-window** GC%/GC-skew profile (only fully-contained windows; shorter-than-window тЗТ empty lists) and the **population variance** `╧Г┬▓=╬г(xс╡втИТ╬╝)┬▓/N` (├╖N, not ├╖NтИТ1) of each windowed series тАФ a compositional-heterogeneity/isochore-style variability signal, cumulative GC-skew locating the replication origin/terminus (Grigoriev 1998), same window-GC signal the [[centromere-analysis]] heuristic uses, composition sibling of the entropy/complexity [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]]. Sources GC-content Brock/Wikipedia + GC skew Lobry 1996/Biopython `GC_skew` + Cuemath population variance (6.8 anchor); `GGGCCAT`тЖТ71.428тАж/0.2/0.0, `GGCC` w2s2тЖТ`GcSkewVariance` 1.0/`GcContentVariance` 0.0; two labelling/estimator assumptions (├Ч100 vs fraction; ├╖N population variance), no contradictions. Records [[seq-gc-analysis-001-evidence]].
- [[replication-origin-cumulative-skew]] тАФ the skew family's *localisation* algorithm (SEQ-REPLICATION-001): predicts the **replication origin from the cumulative GC-skew minimum** and the **terminus from its maximum** (Grigoriev 1998; Rosalind BA1F Minimum Skew Problem). Distinct from the scalar/windowed skew тАФ uses an **integer** cumulative running sum (G:+1, C:тИТ1, A/T:0, `Skew_0=0`, `|Genome|+1` prefix values over `iтИИ[0,n]`), then argmin=`PredictedOrigin` / argmax=`PredictedTerminus`, first-occurrence tie-break (BA1F sample тЖТ 53 of {53,97}); the leading strand is G-rich so skew flips sign at origin/terminus (Lobry 1996), making the integral a valley at ori and peak at ter. `IsSignificant` redefined threshold-free as `max>min` (invented `amplitude>count├Ч0.01` constant removed); flat diagram (no/balanced G/C) тЗТ origin=terminus=0/false. Diagram oracles `CCGGGG`/`GGGCCC`/`AATT`; consumes the same G/C tally as [[base-composition]]/[[nucleotide-composition-skew]], localisation counterpart of the [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]] variability view. Records [[seq-replication-001-evidence]].
- [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] тАФ protein-property member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-HYDRO-001): the **Kyte-Doolittle (1982) GRAVY index** `╬г(kd value)/length` (Expasy/Biopython `gravy()`; positive тЗТ hydrophobic, negative тЗТ hydrophilic) + the **unweighted sliding-window hydropathy profile** (exactly `NтИТW+1` window means, Biopython `protein_scale(edge=1.0)`); the 20-residue kd table I 4.5тАжR тИТ4.5 (identical to [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]]'s `HydropathyScale`), window-size guidance W=9 surface / W=19 transmembrane peaks > 1.6; oracles `A`тЖТ1.8 / `FLIV`тЖТ3.825 / `RKDE`тЖТтИТ3.85, window-3 `FLIV`тЖТ[3.7, 4.1666666667], `W>N`тЖТempty, case-insensitive; one deviation (unknown residues **skipped** not Biopython `KeyError`), no source contradictions. The whole-sequence-scalar + raw-profile amino-acid analogue of the nucleotide [[base-composition]]; the segment-calling [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]] thresholds this same profile, and it shares the kd scale with [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]]'s `CalculateHydropathy`. Records [[seq-hydro-001-evidence]].
- [[dna-duplex-nearest-neighbor-thermodynamics]] тАФ full-tuple thermodynamics member of the SEQ-\* family (SEQ-THERMO-001): the **╬ФH┬░/╬ФS┬░/╬ФG┬░тВГтВЗ/Tm** of a Watson-Crick DNA duplex from the **nearest-neighbor model** тАФ a port of Biopython `Tm_NN` over the **DNA_NN3 / Allawi & SantaLucia 1997** table (10 WC dinucleotide ╬ФH┬░/╬ФS┬░ stacks) plus **two-terminus initiation** (`init_A/T` 2.3/4.1 and `init_G/C` 0.1/тИТ2.8 counted off the two terminal bases). Tm `= (1000┬╖╬ФH┬░)/(╬ФS┬░ + R┬╖ln k) тИТ 273.15`, `R=1.987`, `k=(dnac1тИТdnac2/2)┬╖1eтИТ9` (default 25 nM each тЗТ k=C_T/4, the F=4 non-self-complementary factor); SantaLucia-1998 salt correction `╬ФS┬░ += 0.368┬╖(lenтИТ1)┬╖ln[NaтБ║]` тЗТ Tm monotone in salt; ╬ФG┬░тВГтВЗ `= ╬ФH┬░ тИТ 310.15┬╖╬ФS┬░/1000`. Oracles `CGTTCCAAAGATGTGGGCATGAGCTTAC` (25 nM, 50 mM Na) тЖТ **Tm 60.32 ┬░C**, `GCGC` тЖТ ╬ФH тИТ30.0/╬ФS тИТ84.91/╬ФG тИТ3.67/Tm тИТ18.6, `ATCG` (one A/T + one G/C end) тЖТ ╬ФH тИТ23.6/╬ФS тИТ71.81; **length<2 тЗТ `(0,0,0,0)`**, case-insensitive, non-self-complementary (F=4) only. Distinct from the legacy Wallace/Marmur scalar Tm ([[melting-temperature]], SEQ-TM-001) and from the 2004-unified PCR-primer engine [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] (different init bookkeeping; returns the full tuple). Records [[seq-thermo-001-evidence]]; zero correctness-affecting assumptions, no source contradictions.
- [[melting-temperature]] тАФ the **legacy %GC scalar** melting-temperature member of the SEQ-\* family and the **third distinct Tm surface** (SEQ-TM-001, `CalculateMeltingTemperature`): a single ┬░C number **length-dispatched** at `ThermoConstants.WallaceMaxLength = 14` between the **Wallace rule** `Tm = 4┬╖(G+C)+2┬╖(A+T)` for short oligos (Thein & Wallace 1986) and the **Marmur-Doty GC formula** `Tm = 64.9 + 41┬╖(GCтИТ16.4)/N` (тЙб `64.9 + 0.41┬╖%GC тИТ 672.4/N`) for lenтЙе14 (Marmur & Doty 1962). A **rule of thumb carrying no ╬ФH┬░/╬ФS┬░/╬ФG┬░**, no concentration term, no salt correction тАФ the canonical home of the Wallace/Marmur formulas (previously only sketched as the legacy default on [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]) and the fast approximation that [[seq-summary-001-evidence|SummarizeNucleotideSequence]]'s `MeltingTemperature` field and the primer engine's *default* per-oligo Tm both use. Oracles `ACGTTGCAATGCCGTA`тЖТ48.0 / `ATGCATGC`тЖТ24.0 (Wallace), `GCGCGCGCGCATATATATAT`тЖТ51.78 / 16-mer `ATGCATGCATGCATGC`тЖТ43.375 (Marmur-Doty); empty/nullтЖТ0, case-insensitive; one ASSUMPTION (14-nt dispatch boundary), formula-variant note (repo 64.9/тИТ672.4 vs Biopython `Tm_GC` valueset-1 69.3/тИТ650), no source contradictions. The %GC rule-of-thumb `alternative_to` the two SantaLucia NN engines [[dna-duplex-nearest-neighbor-thermodynamics]] (SEQ-THERMO-001, whose `CalculateThermodynamics` is the NN facet of the same consolidated SEQ-TM-001 registry entry) and [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]. Records [[seq-tm-001-evidence]].
- [[molecular-weight]] тАФ mass member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-MW-001): the average-isotopic **molecular mass in Daltons** of a **protein, DNA or RNA** sequence via one shared polymerization formula `weight = ╬г (monomer mass) тИТ (lenтИТ1)┬╖water` (Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils.molecular_weight`; one water removed per bond тАФ peptide for protein, phosphodiester for nucleic acid; for protein algebraically = the Expasy `╬г residue masses + water`), with average free-amino-acid (protein G 75.0666тАжW 204.2252) and 5'-monophosphate nucleotide (DNA A 331.2218тАж; RNA A 347.2212тАж) mass tables and `water = 18.0153`; single monomer тЗТ free-monomer mass, circular тЗТ тИТone more water, double-strand adds the complement (error for protein); oracles `AGC`тЖТprotein 249.29 / DNA 949.61 / RNA 997.61, `G`тЖТ75.0666, `A`тЖТDNA 331.2218 / RNA 347.2212, empty/nullтЖТ0; case-insensitive, one deviation (unknown symbols **skipped** not Biopython-rejected), no source contradictions. The mass-weighted view of the [[base-composition]] tally and a whole-sequence-scalar sibling of the [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] GRAVY scalar (pI/charge is the separate [[isoelectric-point]] unit). Records [[seq-mw-001-evidence]].
- [[isoelectric-point]] тАФ charge/pH member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-PI-001): the **pH at which a protein's net charge is zero**, found by **bisecting the HendersonтАУHasselbalch net-charge function over [0,14]** to ┬▒0.01. Net charge `╬г_basic +1/(1+10^(pHтИТpKa)) + ╬г_acidic тИТ1/(1+10^(pKaтИТpH))` (Moore 1985, Peptides `charge_pI.cpp`; monotone-decreasing тЗТ unique root); basic/positive = {R,K,H,N-term}, acidic/negative = {D,E,C,Y,C-term}, both termini once. **EMBOSS `Epk.dat` pKa scale** (N-term 8.6/C-term 3.6/C 8.5/D 3.9/E 4.1/H 6.5/K 10.8/R 12.5/Y 10.1) тАФ the single-pKa-per-residue model, *not* position-dependent Bjellqvist. **Composition-only / order-independent** ("no electrostatic interactions" тАФ a permutation gives identical pI), the trait it shares with [[base-composition]]; the ExPASy Compute pI/Mw partner of [[molecular-weight]] and protein-property sibling of [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]]. Oracles `A`/`AG`тЖТ6.10, `D`тЖТ3.75, `K`тЖТ9.70, `DDDD`тЖТ3.23, `KKKK`тЖТ11.27, `FLPVLAGLTPSIVPKLVCLLTKKC`тЖТ9.67 (net charge 3.037398/2.914112/0.7184524 @ pH 5/7/9), `ACDEFGHIKLMNPQRSTVWY`тЖТ7.36 (EMBOSS тЙа Bjellqvist 6.78454); pIтИИ[0,14] invariant, two assumptions (empty/nullтЖТ7.0 guard; scale=EMBOSS parameter choice), small/highly-basic-protein accuracy caveat, no source contradictions. Records [[seq-pi-001-evidence]].
- [[protein-secondary-structure-chou-fasman]] тАФ conformational-propensity member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-SECSTRUCT-001): the **Chou-Fasman (1978) P╬▒/P╬▓/Pt sliding-window mean-propensity profile** тАФ for a window `W`, the arithmetic mean of each of the ╬▒-helix/╬▓-sheet/╬▓-turn propensities (observed/expected; A 1.42/0.83/0.66 тАж V 1.06/1.70/0.50) over each window. The **generic profile, not** the classic 4-of-6-helix / 3-of-5-sheet nucleation-extension state machine тЖТ default `W=7` is an API convenience not a CF constant; shares the exact SEQ-\* sliding-window mechanism with [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] (`NтИТW+1` unweighted window means, `W>N`тЖТempty, unknown residues skip-and-excluded, case-insensitive). Oracles single-residue window = that residue's (P╬▒,P╬▓,Pt) tuple, `AE`тЖТhelix 1.465/sheet 0.60/turn 0.70, `AEV`тЖТhelix 1.330, `AXE` W3 averages only A+E; one contested value resolved (**Lys P╬▒ 1.14** two-source incl. reference impl vs CSB|SJU 1.16), three assumptions (window-7 default, skip-unknown, Lys 1.14), ~50тАУ60% Q3 / 29-protein reliability caveat. A raw propensity profile that does **not** emit helix/sheet/turn segments тАФ distinct from the hydropathy segment-caller [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]], the disorder view [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]] and the SEG scan [[protein-low-complexity-seg]]. Records [[seq-secstruct-001-evidence]].
- [[karyotype-analysis]] тАФ chromosome karyotyping/ploidy-detection family anchor (third Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeKaryotype` builds a karyotype from chromosome descriptors (split sex/autosome, group by base name, count copies, compare to expected ploidy, label nullisomy..pentasomy by absolute count; TotalChromosomes/TotalGenomeSize/MeanChromosomeLength invariants) and `DetectPloidy` estimates whole-genome ploidy from read depth (true-median ratio тЖТ round(ratio├Ч2) clamped [1,8], confidence 1тИТ|ratio├Ч2тИТploidy|├Ч2, emptyтЖТ(2,0)); Down/Turner + diploid/tetraploid/haploid oracles; DD4 nullisomy-unreachable-via-GroupBy, DD5 disomy-only-aneuploid-in-polyploid; deviations None. Descriptor-count sibling of depth-log-ratio [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] тАФ shared synteny anchor (fourth Chromosome-analysis unit; comparative-genomics COMPGEN-SYNTENY will reuse it): `FindSyntenyBlocks` builds syntenic blocks from ortholog pairs (group by chr pair, sort by ref position, collinear runs merged under maxGap, emit тЙеminGenes; block carries strand '+'/'-', GeneCount, SequenceIdentity=NaN for coordinate-only input per MCScanX; I1тАУI5) + `DetectRearrangements` classifies adjacent-block signals (diff target chrтЖТTranslocation, same chr diff strandтЖТInversion, gap asymmetryтЖТDeletion, overlapping source diff targetsтЖТDuplication); forward/inverted-block + translocation(50000)/inversion(size 10000) oracles; empty/below-minGenes/maxGap-split/multi-pair edge cases; MCScanX/SyRI/MUMmer + Wikipedia; deviations None.
- [[telomere-analysis]] тАФ chromosome telomere family anchor (fifth Chromosome-analysis unit): telomere repeat detection + length estimation тАФ 3тА▓ end forward TTAGGG / 5тА▓ end reverse-complement CCCTAA (6-bp vertebrate unit, Meyne 1989), configurable 70%-per-window purity so imperfect repeats accepted (5/6 for 6-bp, 5/7 for Arabidopsis TTTAGGG; divergent TTAGGAтЖТ0.833), purityтИИ[0,1] tracked with length; length direct from run or qPCR T/S ratio (Cawthon 2002) EstimatedLength=referenceLength├Ч(tsRatio/referenceRatio); IsCriticallyShort=(hasTelomere&&length<criticalLength)OR empty; criticalLength 3000 / minTelomereLength 500 / searchLength(truncates) / referenceLength 7000 configurable defaults not biological constants; Wikipedia/Meyne/Cawthon/Blackburn-Gall sources; deviations None. Sibling of [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]] тАФ comparative-genomics common-interval / conserved-cluster unit: a conserved gene cluster = a gene-label SET contiguous in EVERY genome (order- and strand-free inside the window), the common-interval model (Uno & Yagiura 2000, Heber & Stoye 2001 k-permutation O(kn+z), Bui-Xuan/Habib/Paul 2013 unifying view, Didier et al. 2013 sequences-with-duplicates/paralogs); interval size тЙе2 (singletons excluded), whole set (1..n) trivially common, meaningful only for KтЙе2; Seqeron does the strict O(n┬▓┬╖K) check with minClusterSize filter; strict gap-free model тАФ maxGap retained for API/MCP back-compat only and does NOT relax it, gene-teams gapped extension (Bergeron 2002) not implemented; golden vector IdтВЗ vs (7 2 1 3 6 4 5) тЖТ {1,2}/{1,2,3}/{3,4,5,6}/{4,5}/{4,5,6}/{1..6} + trivial {1..7}, split-negative {2,3}, duplicates T/S тЖТ {1,2,3,4}; order-free sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] and [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; deviations None.
- [[average-nucleotide-identity]] тАФ comparative-genomics ANI family anchor (first COMPGEN unit): the ANIb genome-similarity metric (Goris 2007) that operationalizes the prokaryotic species boundary (ANIтЙИ95%тЖФ70% DDH) тАФ fragment query into 1020 nt pieces, best-match place each against the reference (`CalculateAni`), keep fragments >30% identity over тЙе70% alignable (both recalculated over the query-fragment length), average the qualifying per-fragment identities; gapped Smith-Waterman placement recovers indels (`gapped:true`), reciprocal/symmetric ANI = mean of both directions (`CalculateReciprocalAni`, order-independent); null/emptyтЖТ0, non-positive fragmentLength throws; engine decision = SequenceAligner.LocalAlign (full DP, BLAST DNA scoring) not NCBI-BLASTN, indel handling correct; sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] in the COMPGEN family; deviations None.
- [[dot-plot-word-match]] тАФ comparative-genomics visual pairwise-comparison unit (`COMPGEN-DOTPLOT-001`): the word-match / k-tuple dot matrix (Gibbs & McIntyre 1970 тЖТ EMBOSS `dottup`) тАФ dot at (x,y) iff the length-`wordSize` word at x in seq1 exactly matches the word at y in seq2 (case-insensitive, x=seq1/y=seq2, all overlapping occurrences via suffix tree), diagonals = similarity / main diagonal = self-comparison / repeats = extra diagonals / indels break the diagonal; `wordSize` (EMBOSS default 10) noise-vs-sensitivity trade-off (longer=less noise/less sensitive), `stepSize` x-subsampling; exact-match `dottup` not scored `dotmatcher`; AGCGT/AT k=1тЖТ{(0,0),(4,1)}, ACGTACGT self wordSize4тЖТ{(0,0),(0,4),(1,1),(2,2),(3,3),(4,0),(4,4)}, ACGT self main-diagonal oracles; word>seq/null/empty/disjointтЖТno dots, non-positive wordSize/stepSize throws; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters; orientation + case-insensitivity assumptions, deviations None.
- [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] тАФ comparative-genomics ortholog & in-paralog detection unit (`COMPGEN-ORTHO-001`): orthologs by Reciprocal Best Hits (RBH тАФ each gene the other's best hit across two genomes, Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008 / Tatusov 1997 / Fitch 1970 speciation-vs-duplication), recent (in-)paralogs by within-genome mutual best hits (Remm 2001); best hit=max-similarity with deterministic tie-break, reciprocity mandatory (one-directional best hit is NOT an ortholog = the guarded defect), тЙе50% coverage + min-similarity gates, partial-matching output, emptyтЖТno orthologs / single-geneтЖТno paralogs; reciprocity/non-reciprocity(RBH count 1)/in-paralog oracles; one assumption = alignment-free 5-mer Jaccard replaces BLAST bit-score ranking (reciprocity/coverage/threshold source-backed); shared anchor for COMPGEN-RBH-001, the core/shared-gene sub-unit of [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]]; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
- [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]] тАФ comparative-genomics signed-permutation / breakpoint rearrangement-detection unit (`COMPGEN-REARR-001` + `COMPGEN-REVERSAL-001`): the HannenhalliтАУPevzner/BafnaтАУPevzner theory тАФ signed permutation (strand=sign), extended `(0,тАж,n+1)` (endpoints=telomeres), breakpoint = consecutive pair where neither `(x,y)` nor `(тИТy,тИТx)` survives in ╬▓, `b(╬▒)` count = `d_BP=nтИТsim(common adjacencies)`, reversal-distance lower bound `dтЙеb/2`; `ClassifyRearrangement` тЖТ Inversion (reversal = sign-flip + local reverse) vs Transposition (block move preserving orientation), Translocation/Deletion/Insertion/Duplication "Not implemented" (single permutation can't express them); Hunter `(тИТ2,тИТ3,+1,+6,тИТ5,тИТ4)`тЖТb=6/dтЙе3, identityтЖТ0, single-inversion `(+1,тИТ4,тИТ3,тИТ2,+5)`тЖТb=2 oracles; `bтИИ[0,n+1]` invariant; the signed-permutation `alternative_to` the block-signal [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]], sibling of ANI/ortholog/clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
- [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]] тАФ comparative-genomics end-to-end pipeline (`CompareGenomes`): partitions each genome's genes into core (conserved = RBH ortholog pairs, Tettelin 2005 pan-genome) vs dispensable (genome-specific = the rest), reports Conserved/Specific1/Specific2 + OverallSynteny=(genes in MCScanX syntenic blocks)/min(|g1|,|g2|) clamped тЙд1; symmetric partition, emptyтЖТall-0; orchestrates RBH ortholog detection (COMPGEN-RBH-001) + synteny (COMPGEN-SYNTENY-001); sibling of [[average-nucleotide-identity]] & [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]]; two source-backed assumptions (alignment-free RBH gate, MCScanX тЙе5-anchor block threshold тЖТ OverallSynteny can be 0 with conserved orthologs); deviations None.
- [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] тАФ protein-disorder family MoRF unit (DISORDER-MORF-001, second DISORDER-* unit): Molecular Recognition Feature prediction by the "dip within disorder" heuristic (Oldfield 2005 / Cheng-Oldfield PMC2570644 / Mohan 2006) тАФ a short ordered run (per-residue TOP-IDP disorder score <0.5) of total length 10тАУ70 flanked on both sides by disorder (score тЙе0.5) = one MoRF; 0.5 order/disorder threshold, ╬▒/╬▓/╬╣ bound-state sub-types (Mohan 2006), MoRF scoreтИИ[0,1] rising with dip depth; terminal dip / fully-ordered / fully-disordered / out-of-band тЖТ none; TOP-IDP normalized `(raw+0.884)/1.871` per-residue score from `PredictDisorder`; one assumption = exact flank-length params paywalled тЖТ qualitative criterion (threshold/band/shape source-traceable); distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]]; deviations None.
- [[protein-low-complexity-seg]] тАФ protein disorder / features family anchor (first DISORDER-* unit, DISORDER-LC-001): the SEG algorithm (Wootton & Federhen 1993/1996) partitioning a protein into low-/high-complexity segments; complexity = Shannon entropy `H=тИТ╬гpс╡вlogтВВpс╡в` bits/residue (max logтВВ20тЙИ4.322), two-stage scan with W=12 trigger window / K1=2.2 trigger cutoff / K2=2.5 extension cutoff (NCBI `blast_seg.c` defaults); homopolymer H=0 triggers, 12-distinct HтЙИ3.585>K2 no segment; X-rich/X-Y-rich label + greedy single-residue extension are flagged repository extensions not moving boundaries; distinct from [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp|intrinsic-disorder prediction]] (TOP-IDP) and the genomic-DNA [[repetitive-element-detection]] low-complexity counterpart.
- [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]] тАФ protein-disorder family shared anchor (DISORDER-PRED-001 + DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001 + DISORDER-REGION-001): the TOP-IDP `PredictDisorder` sliding-window intrinsic-disorder predictor (Campen 2008) that [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] + disordered-region detection sit on; also hosts the region-detection layer (contiguous runs тЙе minRegionLength, default RegionType classification proline-rich/acidic/basic/Ser-Thr-rich > 0.25 + Long/Standard IDR, opt-in MobiDB-lite flavor scheme); per-residue Sс╡в=mean over window of min-max-normalized TOP-IDP `(pтИТ(тИТ0.884))/1.871 тИИ [0,1]`, disordered when Sс╡втЙе0.542 (max-likelihood cutoff), default window 21 (edge-clipped) / minRegionLength 5; Dunker 2001 disorder{A,R,G,Q,S,P,E,K}/order{W,C,F,I,Y,V,L,N}/ambiguous{D,H,M,T} sets + Kyte-Doolittle `CalculateHydropathy`; W30тЖТ0.0/P30тЖТ1.0/E30тЖТ0.866 oracles, null/emptyтЖТempty, non-canonical skipped (all-unknown windowтЖТ0.0), case-insensitive, O(n┬╖w); also anchors the raw per-residue propensity primitives (DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001: `GetDisorderPropensity` returns the RAW un-normalized Table-2 value, unknownтЖТ0.0, + the two public Dunker sets); assumptions None (params source-traced), impl = simplified single-feature heuristic not competitive with IUPred2A/MobiDB-lite; distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]].
- [[coiled-coil-prediction]] тАФ ProteinMotif family anchor (first ingested unit, PROTMOTIF-CC-001): the heptad a/d hydrophobic-core occupancy coiled-coil predictor `ProteinMotifFinder.PredictCoiledCoils` тАФ for each window `score = (#a/d positions with residue тИИ {I,L,V})/(#a/d positions)` maximised over the 7 heptad registers (`p(k,r)=(kтИТr) mod 7`, core a=0/d=3), contiguous windows with score тЙе threshold mapped to residue regions тЙе21 residues (3 heptads) with peak `ScoreтИИ[0,1]`; defaults window 28 (4 heptads, Lupas 1991) / threshold 0.5 / min-region 21 (Mason & Arndt тЙе3-heptad); INV-01..05 (scoreтИИ[0,1]; regionтЙе21; len<windowтЖТempty; off-frame found via 7-register max); (LAALAAA)├Ч5тЖТ(0,34,1.0) / no-{I,L,V}тЖТnone / (LAAAAAA)тЖТ0.5 boundary oracles; COILS 21├Ч20 PSSM deliberately omitted (weights not retrievable, use COILS/Paircoil2 for P-scores) + {I,L,V}-only core-set assumption (source-verbatim); sequence-only heuristic, distinct from the ProteinPred disorder/features family ([[protein-low-complexity-seg]], [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]], [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]]).
- [[common-protein-motifs]] тАФ ProteinMotif family second unit (PROTMOTIF-COMMON-001, `ProteinMotifFinder.FindCommonMotifs`): scans an amino-acid sequence against a fixed built-in `CommonMotifs` dictionary of canonical PROSITE patterns and aggregates every hit carrying its accession/name тАФ PS00001 `ASN_GLYCOSYLATION` `N-{P}-[ST]-{P}`, PS00005 `PKC_PHOSPHO_SITE` `[ST]-x-[RK]`, PS00006 `CK2_PHOSPHO_SITE` `[ST]-x(2)-[DE]`, PS00016 `RGD` `R-G-D`, PS00017 `ATP_GTP_A` `[AG]-x(4)-G-K-[ST]`; PROSITE syntax (`x` wildcard, `[ ]` allowed set, `{ }` excluded set, `x(n)`/`x(m,n)` repetition); 0-based-inclusive `MotifMatch.Start`/`End` (PROSITE reports 1-based) + substring invariant + overlaps-all-reported (ScanProsite "overlaps, no includes"); `NFTA`/Pro-exclusion-no-match/`SAR`/`SAAE`+`SDED`/`GXXXXGKS`/`RGD`+`RGD`-overlap oracles; one API-shape assumption (0- vs 1-based origin, no correctness effect); the **protein** fixed-catalog analogue of the DNA [[regulatory-element-detection]], sibling of the windowed [[coiled-coil-prediction]], distinct from the caller-supplied-set DNA exact [[known-motif-search]].
- [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] тАФ ProteinMotif family third unit (PROTMOTIF-DOMAIN-001): protein **domain** prediction + **signal-peptide** prediction. `ProteinMotifFinder.FindDomains` scans PROSITE **domain patterns** (PS00028 C2H2 zinc finger/PF00096, PS00017 P-loop/PF00069, PS00678 WD40 15-residue/PF00400; ScanPrositeтЖТregex), 0-based inclusive hits, tandem repeats all detected тАФ SH3/PDZ excluded (PROSITE **PROFILEs**, no deterministic pattern). Opt-in `FindDomainsByHmm`/`Plan7ProfileHmm` reproduces the **HMMER3** engine over 3 bundled CC0 Pfam HMMs (SH3/PDZ/WD40): Viterbi/Forward log-odds (exact 1e-9 hand-HMM), local-multihit `pre_score` vs Swiss-Prot `bg->f` (~1e-5-bit hmmsearch parity), null2 bias (omega 1/256), Gumbel/exponential E-values (`E=P┬╖Z`), `p7_domaindef` multi-domain envelope decomposition (GBB1/PF00400тЖТ7 blades exact) + stochastic-traceback clustering for overlapping tandems (fixed-seed Easel LCG 42), verified vs pyhmmer 0.12.1. `PredictSignalPeptide` = von Heijne tripartite n(K/R+)/h(hydrophobic ╬▒-helix)/c(polar) + тИТ1,тИТ3 rule {A,G,S}, score (n+2h+c)/4 with evidence-based constraints (nScore>0, hScoreтЙе0.5) and Probability=Score. Six resolved design decisions; MSV/bias prefilters + exact-RNG-bit parity + full-Pfam coverage out of scope (research-grade). Sibling of [[coiled-coil-prediction]] & [[common-protein-motifs]].
- [[protein-motif-pattern-search]] тАФ ProteinMotif family general engine (PROTMOTIF-FIND-001, `ProteinMotifFinder.FindMotifByPattern`): the **general, arbitrary caller-supplied** PROSITE-pattern protein motif finder underneath the fixed-dictionary [[common-protein-motifs]]. Three primitives тАФ `ConvertPrositeToRegex` (PROSITEтЖТregex: `x`тЖТ`.`, `[ABC]`тЖТ`[ABC]`, `{ABC}`тЖТ`[^ABC]`, `x(n)`тЖТ`.{n}`, `x(n,m)`тЖТ`.{n,m}`, `<`тЖТ`^`, `>`тЖТ`$`); `FindMotifByPattern` (all matches incl. overlaps via zero-width lookahead `(?=(pattern))` per ScanProsite, 0-based `MotifMatch.Start`/`End`, case-insensitive, empty/nullтЖТempty, invalid regex handled gracefully); and information-content scoring `CalculateMotifScore` IC=╬гlogтВВ(20/allowed_count) over constrained positions (`x`=0 bits, fixedтЙИ4.32 bits) + `CalculateEValue` E=(NтИТL+1)┬╖2^(тИТIC), Schneider & Stephens 1990 (NOT BLAST statistics тАФ that citation was removed). Pins the PROSITE-pattern catalog (PS00001/00004тАУ00009/00016тАУ00018/00028 C2H2/00029 leucine-zipper) and fixed two impl bugs (PS00007 exact repeat counts; PS00018 EF-hand `{W}`+trailing `[LIVMFYW]`); five non-PROSITE linear motifs literature-verified (NLS1/NES1/SIM1/WW1/SH3_1); SKIP-FLAG=TRUE common sites noted. Sibling of the fixed-catalog [[common-protein-motifs]], windowed [[coiled-coil-prediction]], and longer-signature [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]]; all assumptions eliminated (0-vs-1-based coordinate convention only). Revalidated by PROTMOTIF-PATTERN-001 ([[protmotif-pattern-001-evidence]]), which adds the end-to-end `FindMotifByProsite` path and the `*`-rejection / range-only-on-`x` PA-line grammar contracts.
- [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]] тАФ ProteinMotif family transmembrane-helix unit (PROTMOTIF-TM-001): the classic **Kyte-Doolittle (1982) hydropathy sliding window** for membrane-spanning ╬▒-helices тАФ slide a window `W=19`, score each window as the **arithmetic mean** of per-residue Kyte-Doolittle hydropathy (`HydropathyScale` I 4.5тАжR тИТ4.5), emit contiguous runs with window mean **тЙе threshold 1.6** as segments (`[iтВА, iтВБ+WтИТ1]`, peak `Score`); profile length `nтИТW+1`, non-standard residues excluded from the mean, `<W`/null/emptyтЖТempty; window 19 & min-span=W justified by ~18тАУ21 residues / ~3тАУ4 nm bilayer. Oracles `D├Ч10+L├Ч20+D├Ч10`тЖТ(5,34) peak 3.8 / `D├Ч40`тЖТnone / `L├Ч19`тЖТ(0,18,3.8). One assumption (`End=lastPassingProfileIndex+WтИТ1` clamped, 2026-06-16 off-by-one fix), no deviations; sequence-only hydrophobicity heuristic тАФ no in-out topology / positive-inside rule / TMHMM-Phobius HMM. Shares the Kyte-Doolittle scale with [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]]'s `CalculateHydropathy`; distinct sibling of [[coiled-coil-prediction]] (heptad a/d, not window-mean), [[common-protein-motifs]], [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] (cleaved signal peptide, not membrane span) & [[protein-motif-pattern-search]].
- [[aneuploidy-detection]] тАФ chromosome copy-number/ploidy family anchor (first Chromosome-analysis unit): abnormal chromosome count from read depth тАФ per-bin CN=round(2^log2(depth/median)├Ч2) clamped [0,10], whole-chromosome call needs dominant CN across тЙе80% of bins (mosaicism tolerance), confidence=1тИТmin(1,|CN/2тИТ2^logRatio|)=1.0 at integer-CN ratios; nullisomy..pentasomy terminology; Down/Edwards/Patau/Turner/Klinefelter oracles; sex-chromosomes-not-special-cased + partial-aneuploidy-needs-80%-bins limitations.
- [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] тАФ epigenetics family bisulfite-sequencing unit (second EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-BISULF-001): base-level DNA-methylation calling from sodium-bisulfite reads тАФ distinct from the age clock (it *produces* the ╬▓-values a clock consumes). Three deterministic ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: (1) `SimulateBisulfiteConversion` тАФ single-strand per-base Frommer 1992 rule (unprotected CтЖТT, protected 5mC stays C, non-C unchanged, case preserved, ACGTCGAA{1}тЖТACGTTGAA); (2) `CalculateMethylationFromBisulfite` тАФ reuses `FindCpGSites`, Bismark C=methylated/T=unmethylated tally, level = meth/(meth+unmeth)тИИ[0,1], zero-coverage sites excluded (ACGTACGT readsтЖТ0.5&0.0); (3) `GenerateMethylationProfile` тАФ Schultz 2012 per-context weighted level ╬г(level┬╖coverage)/╬гcoverage (0.25тЙаunweighted 0.5), zero-total-coverage falls back to unweighted mean; CpG needs C+G, neither-C-nor-T call ignored, past-reference ignored; research-grade, no CHG/CHH calling / no complement merge / no non-conversion-rate correction; sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]; deviations None.
- [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] тАФ epigenetics family anchor (first EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-AGE-001): DNAm ("epigenetic") age from methylation ╬▓-values via the Horvath 2013 multi-tissue clock тАФ two-stage model, linear predictor `Y = intercept + ╬г coef_i┬╖╬▓_i` over 353 elastic-net-selected clock CpGs (transformed-age units), then the two-branch inverse calibration `anti.trafo` (adult.age=20): `21┬╖exp(Y)тИТ1` for Y<0 (exponential), `21┬╖Y+20` for YтЙе0 (linear), continuous at (0,20)=age 20; embedded intercept 0.695507258 + 353 `CoefficientTraining` weights cross-verified byte-identical; invariants Y=0тЖТ20 / CpGs-absent-ignored / empty-mapтЖТFтБ╗┬╣(intercept); nullтЖТArgumentNullException, empty coefficientsтЖТArgumentException; anti.trafo oracles (0тЖТ20, 1тЖТ41, тИТ1тЖТ6.7254682646, тИТ2.5тЖТ0.7237849711) + Y=0.684247258тЖТ34.369192418; scope = multi-tissue only (algorithm doc later extends to Horvath-2018 skin&blood 391-CpG + Levine-2018 PhenoAge 513-CpG no-transform); no BMIQ input normalisation (research-grade); sibling [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] (produces the ╬▓-values); third Epigenetics sibling [[chromatin-state-prediction]] (histone-mark axis).
- [[cpg-island-detection]] тАФ epigenetics family CpG site & island unit (fourth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CPG-001): sequence-only CpG dinucleotide detection (no methylation state тАФ distinct from all siblings). Three ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: `FindCpGSites` (linear scan, 0-based C position, `CGCG`тЖТ2 sites, reused by [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]); `CalculateCpGObservedExpected` (Gardiner-Garden O/E=CpG/((C┬╖G)/L), div-by-zero guardтЖТ0, oracles CGCG├Ч 2.0/ACGTCGACG 3.0/ACGT 4.0/AT-only 0); `FindCpGIslands` (sliding-window merge, default тЙе200bp/GCтЙе0.5/O-EтЙе0.6 inclusive, 0-based inclusive-Start/exclusive-End tuple, 400bp CGCGтЖТ1 island, O(n┬╖w)); GpCтЙаCpG, case-insensitive; Takai-Jones 2002 stricter (тЙе500/55%/0.65) + Saxonov 2006 alt-expected not preset (custom args); Gardiner-Garden & Frommer 1987 + Takai-Jones + Saxonov + Wikipedia; assumptions None. Siblings [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]/[[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]].
- [[chromatin-state-prediction]] тАФ epigenetics family chromatin-state / histone-mark unit (third EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CHROM-001): ChromHMM-style (Ernst & Kellis 2012) annotation of a locus from the *combination of present histone marks* тАФ distinct from the methylation siblings (operates on histone ChIP-seq signals, not DNA methylation). Binary present/absent mark model (ChromHMM binarizes then learns; state = function of the SET of present marks, magnitude beyond the call irrelevant = binary invariance); `PredictChromatinState` takes the six Roadmap 18-state marks {H3K4me3, H3K4me1, H3K27ac, H3K36me3, H3K27me3, H3K9me3} as [0,1] signals, calls present > threshold (default 0.5), maps pattern тЖТ ActivePromoter(TssA, H3K4me3┬▒H3K27ac)/ActiveEnhancer(H3K4me1+H3K27ac)/WeakEnhancer(H3K4me1 no H3K27ac)/Transcribed(Tx, H3K36me3)/Repressed(ReprPC, H3K27me3)/Heterochromatin(Het, H3K9me3)/BivalentPromoter(TssBiv, H3K4me3+H3K27me3)/BivalentEnhancer(EnhBiv, H3K4me1+H3K27me3)/LowSignal(Quies, none); two combinatorial rules тАФ bivalency is a state not a contradiction, promoter(H3K4me3) dominates enhancer(H3K4me1); companions `AnnotateHistoneModifications` (per-mark region label) + `FindAccessibleRegions` (ATAC-like contiguous-merge + minWidth); research-grade тАФ state-assignment logic source-backed, NOT a trained HMM (no LearnModel/Poisson binarization/spatial context); two assumptions (0.5 threshold, single-locus precedence); sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] & [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]; no contradictions.
- [[differentially-methylated-regions]] тАФ epigenetics family DMR-detection unit (fifth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-DMR-001): methylKit (Akalin 2012) two-sample tiling-window + Fisher's-exact-test model тАФ *compares* methylation between two samples (distinct from the single-sample siblings), consuming the per-CpG C/(C+T) ╬▓-values [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] produces over the CpGs [[cpg-island-detection]] locates. Fixed tiles (`win.size=1000/step.size=1000/cov.bases=0`, `tileMethylCounts`), meth.diff=group2%тИТgroup1% (percentage points), per-window pooled 2├Ч2 methylated/unmethylated counts тЖТ Fisher's exact (one sample per group; replicatesтЖТlogistic regression out of scope), hypergeometric single-table p `(a+b)!(c+d)!(a+c)!(b+d)!/(a!b!c!d!n!)` + two-sided тЙд-observed sum; report q<0.01 AND |meth.diff|>25 strict (`getMethylDiff`): hyper meth.diff>+25 / hypo <тИТ25; emptyтЖТno DMRs, zero-coverage group / zero marginalтЖТp=1.0, |meth.diff|=25тЖТexcluded; oracles Fisher a=1/b=9/c=11/d=3тЖТтЙИ0.001346076, hyper window g1=0.0/g2=1.0тЖТ+100/pтЙИ0; two evidence-backed assumptions (per-window pooling, numC/numT=round(level├Чcoverage)); research-grade (no logistic path/SLIM/overlapping tiles); siblings [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]]; no contradictions.
- [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] тАФ Analysis alignment-free pairwise-similarity unit (`GENOMIC-SIMILARITY-001`, `GenomicAnalyzer.CalculateSimilarity`): Jaccard index of the two sequences' distinct k-mer sets (Jaccard 1901 `|AтИйB|/|AтИкB|` over HashSet k-mer sets, Ondov 2016 *Mash* fraction-of-shared-k-mers), exact (no MinHash sketch) J├Ч100 in `[0,100]`, O(n+m); INV symmetry / identicalтЖТ100 / disjointтЖТ0 / distinct-set (repeats once); default k=5, empty-unionтЖТ0 (ASM-1 convention), ├Ч100 scaling; k=3 oracles 80/(100/3)/100/0; `alternative_to` positional [[alignment-statistics]], the 5-mer-Jaccard metric behind [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] and the exact-set basis Mash sketches for [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; limitations = exact-match/composition-only; deviations None.
- [[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] тАФ K-mer family alignment-free word-frequency **distance** unit (`KMER-DIST-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.KmerDistance`): Euclidean (L2) distance between two sequences' normalized k-mer **frequency** vectors `f_s(w)=count/(LтИТk+1)` over the union of observed k-mers (absent wordтЖТ0 component), exact/O(n+m); Zielezinski 2017 word-vector model + Lau 2022 frequency normalization + Vinga-Almeida 2003 4^k-vector + Boden 2014 relative-frequency Euclidean; INV d(x,x)=0 / symmetric / тЙе0 / disjoint-single-kmerтЖТтИЪ2; тИЪ0.11тЙИ0.3316624790 (ATGTGTG/CATGTG k=3) + тИЪ0.125 (AAAA/AAAT k=1) oracles; case-insensitive (ASM-01) + empty/L<kтЖТzero-vector (ASM-02); count-based/Manhattan/Canberra/Chebyshev/cosine/D2/spaced-word not implemented, deviations None; `alternative_to` the presence/absence [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] (this captures abundance), shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-dist-001-evidence]].
- [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]] тАФ K-mer family async count unit (`KMER-ASYNC-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersAsync`): the cooperatively cancelable, progress-reporting thread-pool wrapper over synchronous `CountKmers` тАФ numeric result identical to the sync reference (counts fixed by the k-mer formula `L тИТ k + 1`, nс╡П possible), so the distinctive validated content is *execution* not arithmetic: the .NET cancellation contract (`ThrowIfCancellationRequested`тЖТOperationCanceledException + Canceled state, pre-start `Task.Run(func,token)` cancellation, awaiting a canceled task throws) + `IProgress<double>` 0тЖТ1.0; INV ╬гcounts=LтИТk+1 / empty┬╖k>LтЖТempty dict / kтЙд0тЖТArgumentOutOfRangeException via awaited task; uppercased (case-insensitive) + alphabet-agnostic (IUPAC N counted literally); ATGGтЖТ{ATG:1,TGG:1} + GTAGAGCTGT oracles; one assumption = numeric contract identical to sync (non-correctness-affecting); single-thread offload (not parallelized), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; wraps sync KMER-COUNT-001 (not yet ingested); record [[kmer-async-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-generation]] тАФ K-mer family *space-enumeration* unit (`KMER-GENERATE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.GenerateAllKmers`): exhaustive enumeration of ALL possible k-mers of length `k` over an alphabet тАФ the complete k-mer universe `╬г^k` of size `n^k` (4^k for DNA), depends only on `k`+alphabet not on any sequence; DISTINCT from counting (produces the full n^k word set / address space, siblings extract observed substrings + counts); k-fold Cartesian product `itertools.product(╬г,repeat=k)`, lazy recursive prefix-extension, odometer emission тЖТ lexicographic for a sorted alphabet; INV n^k count / all-distinct-set / length-k / sortedтЖТlexicographic; k=1тЖТ{A,C,G,T}, k=2тЖТ16 (AA..TT), k=3тЖТ64, protein 20^2=400, single-letter 1^4=1 oracles; kтЙд0тЖТArgumentOutOfRangeException, empty alphabetтЖТArgumentException, unsortedтЖТpositional order, verbatim/no-dedup; O(k┬╖n^k) time/O(k) lazy space, suffix-tree N/A (generates not searches); shares the "ACGT"-default + kтЙд0-throws API contract with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] but NOT the `CountKmers` primitive; supplies the index space for [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]]/[[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]]; deviations None; record [[kmer-generate-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-positions]] тАФ K-mer family *occurrence-index* unit (`KMER-POSITIONS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindKmerPositions`): the ascending 0-based positions where a given k-mer occurs in a sequence тАФ *where*, not *how many* (the inverse index to the counting units) тАФ solving the exact Pattern Matching Problem `Occ(P,T)={iтИИ[0,LтИТk]:T[i..i+k)=P}` with all overlapping starts reported; INV-01..04 (match predicate / ascending / count=overlap-occurrences / range `[0,LтИТk]`, empty when k>L); case-insensitive upper-casing (sibling `CountKmers`), unrestricted-text alphabet, null/empty & k>L & absent тЖТ empty (no throw), whole-seqтЖТ`[0]`; `ATAT`/`GATATATGCATATACTT`тЖТ`[1,3,9]` + `AA`/`AAAA`тЖТ`[0,1,2]` oracles; O(L┬╖k) naive span scan, suffix-tree evaluated-not-used (unordered leaves, single-query no amortization); three API-shape assumptions (0-based, case-fold, empty-not-throw), deviations None; the single-pattern K-mer sibling of multi-pattern [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the counting siblings [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-positions-001-evidence]].
- [[both-strand-kmer-counting]] тАФ K-mer family strand-aware count unit (`KMER-BOTH-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersBothStrands`): the ADDITIVE / kPAL-"balance" both-strand profile `count[w] = forward[w] + forward[RC(w)]` (count k-mers of S and of RC(S), sum per key), grounded in inversion symmetry (Shporer 2016) + kPAL balance (Anvar 2014); distinct from тАФ and does NOT implement тАФ the canonical-collapsing convention (lexicographically-smaller of {w,RC(w)} as one key, Jellyfish `-C` / Mash); INV ╬гcount=2┬╖(LтИТk+1) / count[w]=count[RC(w)] strand-symmetric / palindrome RC(w)=wтЖТcount doubled on one key; two linear passes O(n┬╖k), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; case-insensitive/IUPAC-complemented, empty┬╖k>LтЖТempty dict, kтЙд0тЖТArgumentOutOfRangeException (inherited from `CountKmers`); ATGGC k=2тЖТ{AT:2,TG:1,GG:1,GC:2,CC:1,CA:1} + ACGTтЖТ{AC:2,CG:2,GT:2} + AAAтЖТ{AA:2,TT:2} oracles; built on the same sync `CountKmers` primitive as [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; two API-shape assumptions, deviations None; record [[kmer-both-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-statistics]] тАФ K-mer family *summary-statistics* unit (`KMER-STATS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.AnalyzeKmers`): a companion summary layer over the shared `CountKmers` multiset that reduces the count profile to `KmerStatistics` {TotalKmers=LтИТk+1=╬гcounts, UniqueKmers=**distinct** count, MaxCount, MinCount, AverageCount=total/distinct (rounded 2dp), Entropy=Shannon **k-entropy** `тИТ╬г p(╬▒)logтВВp(╬▒)`, `p=mult/(LтИТk+1)`, bits}; the one distinct piece of content is the k-entropy (Manca 2021 + EntropyтАУRank Ratio, corroborated by Wikipedia/BioInfoLogics count tables); GOTCHA `UniqueKmers` = distinct count NOT the count==1 singletons (that is KMER-UNIQUE-001); INV Total=╬гcounts / Unique=distinct(CountKmers) / homopolymerтЖТH0,max=min=total / all-distinctтЖТH logтВВD,max=min=1 / k>L┬╖emptyтЖТall-zero; GTAGAGCTGT k=1 (10/4/4/1/2.5/1.8464) + k=3 (8/8/1/1/logтВВ8=3.0) + ATCGATCAC k=3 (7/6/2/1/2.5216) + AAAA k=2 (3/1/3/3/0) oracles; case-insensitive, kтЙд0тЖТArgumentOutOfRangeException; two presentation-only assumptions (AverageCount 2dp, Entropy unrounded); shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]], distinct from generation/positions/distance siblings; deviations None; record [[kmer-stats-001-evidence]]. Also the home of the **second entry point** for the same k-entropy: `SequenceComplexity.CalculateKmerEntropy` (SEQ-COMPLEX-KMER-001, record [[seq-complex-kmer-001-evidence]]) тАФ the entropy member of the `SEQ-COMPLEX-*` complexity family (siblings [[sequence-complexity-compression-lempel-ziv]]/[[dust-low-complexity-score]]), identical formula from a different class.
- [[unique-and-mincount-kmers]] тАФ K-mer family *frequency-filtering* unit (`KMER-UNIQUE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindUniqueKmers` + `FindKmersWithMinCount`): selects k-mers by their per-k-mer **Count** (overlapping occurrences, Compeau & Pevzner `Count(Text,Pattern)`) at opposite ends of the frequency distribution тАФ `FindUniqueKmers` = the `Count==1` **singletons**, `FindKmersWithMinCount` = the `CountтЙеminCount` **recurrent** k-mers ordered by count desc; total/distinct/unique terminology (BioInfoLogics: unique = "appear only once"; Wikipedia LтИТk+1 total); GOTCHA "unique"=singleton set here тЙа [[k-mer-statistics]]'s `UniqueKmers`=distinct count (ATCGATCAC k=3 тЖТ 5 unique vs 6 distinct, ATC=2 excluded); oracles ATCGATCAC k=3тЖТ{TCG,CGA,GAT,TCA,CAC}, AGAT k=2тЖТ{AG,GA,AT}, ACGTACGT k=4 FindKmersWithMinCount(тАж,2)тЖТ{(ACGT,2)}/(тАж,1)тЖТall-4-count-desc/FindUniqueKmersтЖТ{CGTA,GTAC,TACG}, AAAAA k=3тЖТтИЕ; case-insensitive, kтЙд0тЖТArgumentOutOfRangeException, empty┬╖k>LтЖТempty; two assumptions (minCountтЙд1тЖТall distinct count-desc; upper-casing), deviations None; filters the shared `CountKmers` multiset like [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-unique-001-evidence]].
- [[longest-common-substring]] тАФ Sequence-Comparison longest-common-substring / common-region-detection unit (`GENOMIC-COMMON-001`): the maximal *contiguous* substring shared by two strings (distinct from the gapped longest common *subsequence*) via a generalized suffix tree (LCS = deepest internal node whose subtree holds leaves from both strings, ╬Ш(n+m) build + DFS, Gusfield 1997); `FindLongestCommonRegion` (0-based positions in both) + `FindCommonRegions(minLength)` (all distinct shared runs тЙе minLength), None=empty/len 0/pos тИТ1, identicalтЖТwhole seq at 0/0; documented deterministic first-found-in-`other` tie-break (CACAGAG/TACATAGAT ties ACA vs AGA тЖТ ACA); Wikipedia + GeeksforGeeks sources, shares the suffix-tree exact-match engine with [[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[longest-repeated-substring]] тАФ Repeat-Analysis LRS + repeat-enumeration unit (`GENOMIC-REPEAT-001`): the longest substring recurring within *one* DNA sequence (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindLongestRepeat`) + all distinct substrings occurring тЙе2├Ч with length тЙе minLength (`FindRepeats`), both via the *single-string* suffix tree's deepest internal node with тЙе2 leaves (string depth = repeat length; CMU ┬з2.1 / Wikipedia / GeeksforGeeks App-3 / Gusfield 5.4); overlaps counted, no-repeat/emptyтЖТ`RepeatInfo.None`, `minLengthтЙд0`тЖТ`max(1,minLength)`, ACGT-only, no reverse-complement/maximal-repeat classification; FindRepeats via sorted-suffix adjacent-LCP *every-prefix* enumeration (O(n┬▓), FINDINGS_REGISTER short-prefix fix); ATCGATCGAтЖТATCGA{0,4}, AAAAAAAAAAтЖТAAAAAAAAA{0,1}, ATATATAтЖТATATA{0,2}, ACGTACGTTTTTACGT@3тЖТ8-substring oracles; the *single-string* sibling of [[longest-common-substring]], distinct from the tandem/inverted [[repetitive-element-detection]] anchor; tie-break + ascending-positions assumptions, deviations None.
- [[open-reading-frame-detection]] тАФ Analysis ORF-detection unit (`GENOMIC-ORF-001`): six-frame ATGтЖТfirst-in-frame-stop enumeration (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindOpenReadingFrames`), standard code (start ATG / stops TAA-TAG-TGA), reported span **includes** the stop (Length%3==0) while the translated protein **excludes** it; THE correctness rule = every in-frame ATG reaching a stop reported, so **nested ORFs sharing a stop** both returned (Rosalind `MGMTPRLGLESLLE`/`MTPRLGLESLLE`), ATG-with-no-stopтЖТnone; `minLength` in **nucleotides** inclusive (default 100), 0-based Position, Frame 1тАУ3 + IsReverseComplement, INV-01..05 (starts ATG / ends stop / len%3==0 / тЙеminLength / six-frame), O(n┬▓) worst / O(n) typical; Rosalind_99тЖТ4 distinct proteins + ATGAAAAAATAAтЖТMKK oracles; Rosalind + Wikipedia + NCBI ORFfinder + transl_table=1 sources; deviations None (one fixed greedy bug); deliberately **not** contract-equivalent to annotation `GenomeAnnotator.FindOrfs` (ANNOT-ORF-001: ATG/GTG/TTG, aa-length, strand/start flags) or `Translator.FindOrfs` (genetic-code-parameterized); coding potential is a separate step ([[coding-potential-hexamer-score]]).
- [[known-motif-search]] тАФ Motif-Analysis known-motif-search anchor (`GENOMIC-MOTIFS-001`): multi-pattern **exact** substring matching of a caller-supplied set of known query motifs (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindMotif`) тАФ the "you know what you're looking for" exact-equality baseline, distinct from motif *discovery* and *degenerate* (IUPAC/PROSITE/PWM) matching; THE correctness rule = all **overlapping** occurrences reported (AAA in AAAAAтЖТ{0,1,2}, per Gusfield/Biopython `count_overlap` 3-not-2); 0-based sorted positions, per-motif position lists with absent motifs omitted, upper-cased result keys, empty/whitespace motifтЖТno entry (`Array.Empty<int>()`); EcoRI GAATTCтЖТ{0,9} + `{ACGT,AA,TTT}` in ACGTACGTAA oracles; Tufts/Gusfield + Biopython `Seq.search` + Wikipedia "Restriction site" sources; shares exact-all-occurrences semantics with [[longest-common-substring]]/[[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[alpha-diversity]] тАФ Metagenomics diversity family anchor (first META-* unit, META-ALPHA-001): within-sample diversity indices from one taxonтЖТabundance map (`MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateAlphaDiversity` тЖТ `AlphaDiversity` record) тАФ observed richness S_obs, Shannon H=тИТ╬гpс╡вln(pс╡в) in nats, Simpson concentration ╬╗=╬гpс╡в┬▓, inverse Simpson 1/╬╗ (Hill order-2 effective species), Pielou evenness J=H/ln(S) for S>1 else 0, Chao1 S_obs+fтВБ┬▓/(2fтВВ) (fтВВ=0тЖТbias-corrected S_obs+fтВБ(fтВБтИТ1)/2, non-integer/proportionalтЖТS_obs); Whittaker 1960 ╬▒/╬▓/╬│ framework, Shannon 1948/Simpson 1949/Hill 1973/Chao 1984/Pielou 1966; counts-or-proportions internally normalized, non-positive filtered, O(n); empty/nullтЖТall-0, single speciesтЖТH0/╬╗1/J0; one accepted deviation = Chao1 count-vs-proportion gate; between-sample [[beta-diversity]] its sibling; deviations else None.
- [[metagenomic-binning]] тАФ Metagenomics family binning unit (third META-* unit, META-BIN-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.BinContigs`): groups mixed-community contigs back to their genome of origin (MAGs) by k-means over a composite distance `|╬ФGC|+|╬Фcoverage|+TNF-Pearson-distance` (GC-sorted deterministic centroid init, тЙд50 iters, minBinSize 500 kb filter) тЖТ `GenomeBin` records; completeness=`min(L/expectedGenomeSize├Ч100,100)` (default 4 Mbp) + contamination=`min(gcStdDev/0.5├Ч100,100)` are LENGTH-RATIO/GC-VARIANCE **proxies** (CheckM marker-gene QC now built as a SEPARATE opt-in path тАФ CheckM Eqs. 1тАУ2 over CC0 Pfam marker sets, `EstimateBinQualityFromMarkerCounts`/`DetectMarkers`, NOT wired into `BinContigs`; see [[meta-bin-001-markerqc-evidence]]); INV unique BinId / metrics [0,100] / GC [0,1] / TotalLength=╬г / disjoint partition / Coverage=mean; M5 50.0 / M6 0-100 / M7 1.0-0.0 / M12 25 oracles; opt-in TETRA z-score signature (`CalculateTetranucleotideZScores`/`TetranucleotideZScoreCorrelation`) тАФ RC-extended strand, 256-word Markov expectation `E=N(n1n2n3)┬╖N(n2n3n4)/N(n2n3)`, Schbath variance, Pearson correlation of z-vectors (scale-invariant), z(ACGT)=тИЪ5 for ACGTACGTGGCC, N(n2n3)=0/non-positive-varтЖТz=0; Maguire 2020 limits (plasmids 1-29%/GIs 38-44% poorly recovered), similar-GC+coverageтЖТco-bin; three prior assumptions resolved, deviations None; record [[meta-bin-001-evidence]]; Metagenomics-family sibling of [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]].
- [[taxonomic-classification]] тАФ Metagenomics family taxonomic-classification unit (fourth META-* unit, META-CLASS-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.ClassifyReads` + `BuildKmerDatabase` + `TaxonomyTree.Lca`): faithful Kraken (Wood & Salzberg 2014) per-read/contig assignment тАФ canonical-k-mer (`min(kmer,revcomp)`, default k=31) database mapping each k-mer to the **LCA of all owning reference taxa**, per-read **classification tree** (hit taxa + ancestors weighted by k-mer count) scored over **root-to-leaf (RTL)** paths тЖТ assigned taxon = max-scoring path's leaf, equal-max тЖТ LCA of leaves, no k-mer hits тЖТ **Unclassified** (taxonomy root, C=0); Confidence = **C/Q** (Kraken 2: C = clade k-mers under assigned label, Q = non-ambiguous k-mers queried); ambiguous (non-ACGT) k-mers skipped/not in Q, upper-cased, semicolon/pipe taxonomy strings; invariants |out|=|in| / 0тЙдC/QтЙд1 / CтЙдQ / Q=lenтИТk+1 (all-ACGT) / canonical uniqueness / DB-build LCA / LCA siblingsтЖТparent, ancestor/descendantтЖТancestor, selfтЖТself, disjointтЖТroot; empty/short-<k/no-match тЖТ Unclassified, empty DB тЖТ all Unclassified; scoped to **per-read classification** (abundance *profiling* Taxonomic_Profile is a separate later unit); research-grade, no deviations / no open questions; siblings [[metagenomic-binning]] (per-contig MAGs) & [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]] (consume the abundance profile); record [[meta-class-001-evidence]].
- [[beta-diversity]] тАФ Metagenomics diversity family between-sample unit (second META-* unit, META-BETA-001): between-sample dissimilarity from two taxonтЖТabundance maps (`MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateBetaDiversity` тЖТ `BetaDiversity` record) тАФ Bray-Curtis BC=1тИТ2┬╖╬гmin(N_ij,N_ik)/╬г(N_ij+N_ik) (abundance-sensitive, range [0,1], NOT a true metric) + Jaccard distance J=1тИТ|AтИйB|/|AтИкB| (presence/absence via abundance>0, true distance metric); Whittaker 1960 ╬▒/╬▓/╬│ (beta=turnover), Bray & Curtis 1957, Jaccard 1901; single union-pass O(u), no BC normalization (caller-scaled), +SharedSpecies/UniqueToSample1/2 counts; identicalтЖТ0/0, disjointтЖТ1/1, both-emptyтЖТ0/0 & one-emptyтЖТ1 guards; fish-tank BC 13/33 & J 1/3, symmetry BC 3/5 & J 2/3 oracles; one accepted deviation = UniFracDistance placeholder 0 (no phylo tree); within-sample sibling [[alpha-diversity]]; ecological-Jaccard shares the index math but not domain with sequence [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]].
