- [[functional-prediction]] тАФ Metagenomics family functional-prediction unit (fifth META-* unit, META-FUNC-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.PredictFunctions` + `FindPathwayEnrichment`): predicts a community's *functional* capability (PICRUSt / KO-pathway style) in two exact-numeric pieces тАФ (A) homology-based annotation transfer: exact-signature `string.Contains` hit scored by BLOSUM62 self-score S, bit `S'=(╬╗SтИТlnK)/ln2` and E-value `E=K┬╖m┬╖n┬╖e^(тИТ╬╗S)=m┬╖n┬╖2^(тИТS')` (ungapped BLOSUM62 ╬╗=0.3176/K=0.134, Altschul/`blast_stat.c`), best hit = lowest E-value / highest bit (INV-01..03,06); (B) hypergeometric pathway ORA `P(XтЙеx)=1тИТ╬г C(M,i)C(NтИТM,nтИТi)/C(N,n)` in log-Gamma space, background=union-of-pathways default + query unioned in, sorted ascending, pтИИ[0,1], x/M/n=0тЖТp=1 (INV-04,05); oracles WWWтЖТS'18.0202932787533/E 3.3852730346546eтИТ5 + N8000/M400/n100/x20тЖТ7.88eтИТ8; *Simplified* тАФ exact substring not gapped alignment (ASM-01, divergent homologs missed), no gapped ╬╗/K / composition stats / HMM / FDR; asks "what can they do" vs the "who is there" of [[taxonomic-classification]]/[[metagenomic-binning]] and the diversity of [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]]; BLAST significance distinct from percent-id [[alignment-statistics]]; ORA half owned by [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] (the dedicated META-PATHWAY-001 unit); record [[meta-func-001-evidence]].
- [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] тАФ Metagenomics family pathway-enrichment unit (META-PATHWAY-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindPathwayEnrichment` / `HypergeometricUpperTail`): the GO::TermFinder / clusterProfiler over-representation statistic тАФ score each pathway by the hypergeometric **right-tail** `P(XтЙеx)=1тИТ╬г_{i=0}^{xтИТ1}C(M,i)C(NтИТM,nтИТi)/C(N,n)` (N=background, M=pathway size, n=query, x=overlap; sampling without replacement, upper tail only), `phyper(xтИТ1,M,NтИТM,n,lower.tail=FALSE)` reference (the q=xтИТ1 shift gives P(XтЙеx)); log-Gamma summation to N=8000, pтИИ[0,1], pathways sorted ascending; p=1 when x/M/n=0, **MтЖФn symmetry**, without-replacement feasibility drops C(┬╖,┬╖)=0 terms; background = explicit `backgroundGenes` else union-of-pathway-members default (query always unioned in), members intersected with background; **no BH/Bonferroni FDR** correction; Boyle 2004 + PNNL ORA ┬з8.2 sources, oracles 7.88eтИТ8 + 1/252 + 5/6 + 251/252; one caller-overridable background-defaulting assumption; **owns** the ORA machinery that [[functional-prediction]] uses as component B; generic statistic (GO/proteomics), research-grade, no contradictions; record [[meta-pathway-001-evidence]].
- [[taxonomic-profile]] тАФ Metagenomics family community-abundance profiling unit (sixth META-* unit, META-PROF-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.GenerateTaxonomicProfile`): the **aggregation/estimation** step downstream of per-read [[taxonomic-classification]] тАФ takes an `IEnumerable<TaxonomicClassification>` and returns a `TaxonomicProfile` with **relative-abundance maps at four ranks** (kingdom/phylum/genus/species, abundance = count(taxon)/╬гcount(classified)), **inline species-level diversity** (Shannon H=тИТ╬гpс╡вln(pс╡в) in nats + Simpson concentration ╬╗=╬гpс╡в┬▓), and **read counts** (TotalReads/ClassifiedReads); Unclassified excluded from denominators, empty rank strings filtered, per-rank ╬гтЙИ1.0; invariants ClassifiedReadsтЙдTotalReads / ClassifiedReads=╬г(counts any rank) / ShannonтЙе0 / 0тЙдSimpsonтЙд1; oracles Shannon=ln(3) (3 uniform), Simpson=0.375 ([2,1,1]); emptyтЖТ0/0/empty & single taxonтЖТ1.0/H0/╬╗1 (vs emptyтЖТ╬╗0); count-based tally (NOT MetaPhlAn marker-coverage, no genome-size correction), inherits upstream classifier accuracy; the profiling unit [[taxonomic-classification]] deliberately deferred, sibling of [[alpha-diversity]] (richer six-index within-sample summary) / [[beta-diversity]]; MetaPhlAn/Segata 2012, research-grade, no contradictions; record [[meta-prof-001-evidence]].
- [[antibiotic-resistance-gene-detection]] тАФ Metagenomics family AMR gene-detection unit (seventh META-* unit, META-RESIST-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindAntibioticResistanceGenes`): ResFinder-style screen of assembled contigs against a **caller-supplied** resistance-gene reference DB, reporting the single **best-matching gene per contig** тАФ `BestUngappedMatch` slides each reference across the contig (offsets тИТ(mтИТ1)..nтИТ1, overhanging both ends), keeps the max-match window (tieтЖТshorter/higher-identity), then identity=matches/w (BLAST gapless, Heng Li 2018) & coverage=w/m (fraction of **reference** length, so contig-edge/split genes still scored), reported iff identityтЙеidThreshold AND coverageтЙеcovThreshold; best match = max identity, tieтЖТmax coverage (Zankari 2012 "best-matching gene", CARD RGI best-hit); INV-01..05, defaults 0.90 ID / 0.60 cov (named constants), Perfect=1.0/1.0 (CARD); oracles CGTACGT@AAACGTACGTтЖТ1.0/1.0, CGTTCGT vs CGTACGTтЖТ6/7тЙИ0.857/1.0, edge CGTAтЖТ1.0 / 4тБД7тЙИ0.571; *Simplified* тАФ gapless ungapped (ASM-01, indel matches under-scored vs gapped BLAST; substitution + edge-truncation exact), no SNP/protein-homology (CARD variant/homolog models out of scope), nucleotide-only case-sensitive, legacy `FindResistanceGenes` motif stub separate; asks "**which known resistance genes are present**" vs the who/what/how-diverse of [[taxonomic-classification]]/[[functional-prediction]]/[[alpha-diversity]]; BLAST-style homology screen sharing machinery with [[functional-prediction]] but scoring nucleotide identity/coverage not BLOSUM62 bit-score (identity denominator = [[alignment-statistics]] rule); provenance note flagged (evidence 0.80/0.98 vs impl 0.90 default); record [[meta-resist-001-evidence]].
- [[significant-taxa-detection]] тАФ Metagenomics family differential-abundance unit (eighth META-* unit, META-TAXA-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.MannWhitneyU` / `FindSignificantTaxa`): per-taxon **two-group MannтАУWhitney U (Wilcoxon rank-sum)** test asking "which taxa differ in abundance between two groups?" тАФ non-parametric, rank-based, suits compositional/zero-inflated data (Xia & Sun 2017). PoolтЖТmidranks (tied values averaged, accumulate ╬г(t┬│тИТt))тЖТ`U1=R1тИТn1(n1+1)/2`, `U2=n1┬╖n2тИТU1`; `m_U=n1┬╖n2/2`, tie-corrected `╧Г_U=sqrt(n1┬╖n2┬╖(n1+n2+1)/12 тИТ n1┬╖n2┬╖╬г(t┬│тИТt)/(12n(nтИТ1)))`; `z=(|UтИТm_U|тИТcc)/╧Г_U` on `max(U1,U2)`, ccтИИ{0,0.5} (0.5 on by default = SciPy `use_continuity`); two-tailed `p=2┬╖(1тИТ╬ж(z))` clamped [0,1], ╬ж via `StatisticsHelper.NormalCDF` (A&S 7.1.26, тЙИ1eтИТ6 accuracy). `FindSignificantTaxa` runs it per taxon over label-defined ({1,2}) groups тЖТ `SignificantTaxon` ascending by p. INV-01..06 (U1+U2=n1┬╖n2, 0тЙдUтЙдn1┬╖n2, pтИИ[0,1], SignificantтЗФp<threshold, all-tiedтЖТ╧Г0тЖТz0тЖТp1, group-swap symmetric); oracles SciPy x[19,22,16,29,24]/y[20,11,17,12]тЖТU1=17/U2=3/╧Г=4.0825/z_cc=1.5922тЖТpтЙИ0.11135 (z_nocc=1.7146тЖТpтЙИ0.08641) + tortoise/hare U_T=11/U_H=25/sum=36; empty groupтЖТArgumentException, absent taxonтЖТabundance 0 (ASM-03); asymptotic-not-exact, no FDR (caller applies BH), ignores compositionality; **consumes** [[taxonomic-profile]] abundance vectors; distinct-by-**test** from the hypergeometric [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] and Fisher's-exact [[differentially-methylated-regions]]; siblings [[alpha-diversity]] / [[beta-diversity]]; record [[meta-taxa-001-evidence]].
- [[methylation-context-classification]] тАФ epigenetics family CpG/CHG/CHH context-classification unit (sixth/final EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-METHYL-001): sequence-only trinucleotide classifier partitioning cytosines into CpG/CHG/CHH from the downstream base(s) тАФ distinct because it handles the *non-CpG* CHG/CHH contexts [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] does not call from reads. Rule (Cornish-Bowden 1985 IUPAC H={A,C,T}="not G"): CpGтЯ║bтВБ=G, CHGтЯ║bтВБтИИH & bтВВ=G, CHHтЯ║bтВБтИИH & bтВВтИИH; CpG/CHG symmetric, CHH asymmetric (Krueger-Andrews 2011). Three ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: `GetMethylationContext` (O(1), null when not a classifiable C), `FindMethylationSites` (O(n) scan тЖТ one site/classifiable C, 0-based, sequence-only level=0/coverage=0 placeholder), `GenerateMethylationProfile` (shared with [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]], Schultz 2012 weighted ╬г(level┬╖cov)/╬гcov, zero-coverageтЖТunweighted-mean fallback); CGACAGCAAтЖТCpG@0/CHG@3/CHH@6 + weighted (8+2)/(10+10)=0.5 oracles; G-never-H (CGGтЖТCpG), terminal-CG-still-CpG, incomplete-trailing / non-ACGT unclassified; Lister 2009 realism (IMR90 99.98% CG vs H1 ES ~25% non-CG); single-strand only, no symmetric-strand pairing; two assumptions (level=0 placeholder, 0.5 MethylatedCpG count cutoff); no contradictions.
- [[rna-base-pairing]] тАФ MiRNA family anchor + shared RNA base-pairing primitive (first MiRNA unit, MIRNA-PAIR-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): deciding **whether two RNA bases can pair** and building the antiparallel miRNA-mRNA duplex from that rule. `CanPair`тЯ║{A-U,U-A,G-C,C-G,G-U,U-G} = Watson-Crick {A-U,G-C} (Agarwal 2015) + the single standard **G-U wobble** (Crick 1966); `IsWobblePair`тЯ║{G-U,U-G}, wobbleтКЖpairable, wobble counted **separately** from matches (PMC4870184). `GetReverseComplement` = antiparallel RNA reverse complement for seedтЖТtarget motif (Lewis 2005; let-7a `GAGGUAG`тЖТ`CUACCUC`). `AlignMiRnaToTarget` pairs miRNA[i]тЖФtarget[lenтИТ1тИТi] over the shorter overlap, ungapped, emitting `|`(WC)/`:`(wobble)/space(mismatch); counts sum to min(len), Gaps=0; ╬ФG = **simplified** Turner-2004 stacking sum over consecutive paired runs (sign reliable тАФ fully-WC тЙд0, all-mismatch тЙе0 тАФ magnitude not). Oracles AAAA/UUUUтЖТ4 matches, GGGG/UUUUтЖТ4 wobbles, AAAA/AAAAтЖТ4 mismatches; DNA TтЖТU normalised, unknown baseтЖТN never pairs, emptyтЖТempty duplex. The **shared** pairing rule RNA secondary-structure classification also uses; **not** target-site efficacy prediction (that is `FindTargetSites`/MIRNA-TARGET-001), and the A-opposite-position-1 preference is Argonaute recognition, not base pairing; record [[mirna-pair-001-evidence]].
- [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] тАФ MiRNA family precursor-hairpin unit (second MiRNA unit, MIRNA-PRECURSOR-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): finding stem-loop pre-miRNA precursors (~60-120 nt) from which Dicer excises the ~22 nt mature duplex. **Default heuristic** `FindPreMiRnaHairpins` counts uninterrupted complementary pairs ({A-U,G-C}+G-U wobble, [[rna-base-pairing]] primitive) from both ends inward тЖТ accept iff stem тЙе18 bp (Krol 2004) + loop 3-25 nt (Bartel 2004); extracts mature(5' arm)/star(3' arm), balanced dot-bracket, Turner-2004 ╬ФG; **documented limitation** тАФ consecutive-pairing is stricter than real structure, rejects natural miRBase precursors (hsa-mir-21 16 end-pairs, let-7a-1 5, tests M18/M19). **Opt-in** `AssessHairpinByMfe`/`FindPreMiRnaHairpinsByMfe` fold with the RNA-STRUCT-001 ZukerтАУStiegler engine and read the hairpin from the real MFE structure (single dominant hairpin/no multibranch + stem тЙе16 (Ambros 2003) + loop 3-25 + MFEI тЙе0.85 (Zhang 2006, AMFE=100┬╖|╬ФG┬░|/n, MFEI=AMFE/GC%)) тЖТ detects hsa-mir-21 (╬ФG┬░ тИТ35.13/MFEI 1.0037) & let-7a-1; rejects a stronger-╬ФG┬░ multibranch 5S-rRNA-like on **structure**. **Opt-in** `PredictDroshaDicerCleavage` = published ruler (Drosha +11 bp basal junction/Han 2006, Dicer 22-nt 5'-count/Park 2011, RNase III 2-nt overhang/Lee 2003, CNNC 16-18 nt confidence flag/Auyeung 2013; hsa-miR-21-5p cross-check). **Opt-in** `ClassifyPreMiRna` = logistic regression over [╬ФG,AMFE,MFEI,GC,%paired], 13 public-domain miRBase positives vs Altschul-Erickson di-shuffle negatives (Bonnet 2004 convention), held-out AUC 1.0, no GPL miRDeep2 code; read-stacking miRDeep2 signal out of scope (needs reads); record [[mirna-precursor-001-evidence]].
- [[seed-sequence-analysis]] тАФ MiRNA family seed-extraction unit (third MiRNA unit, MIRNA-SEED-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): **string-level** extraction and comparison of the mature-miRNA 5' seed тАФ the primary determinant of animal target recognition тАФ not binding prediction. `GetSeedSequence` returns positions **2-8** (7 nt, extended seed) via `Substring(1,7)` uppercase (casing only, **no** TтЖТU); `<8 nt`/null/empty тЖТ `""`. `CreateMiRna(name, sequence)` normalises `ToUpperInvariant()`+`TтЖТU`, extracts the seed from the normalised sequence, stores `SeedSequence` + fixed **zero-based** `SeedStart=1`/`SeedEnd=7`. `CompareSeedRegions` = Hamming over the 7-nt seed (`Matches`+`Mismatches`=7, mismatches also count any length diff), `IsSameFamily` тЯ║ **exact seed-string equality**; empty seed тЖТ zeroed result. **miRNA family = identical 2-8 seed** (let-7a/-7b/-7c-5p all `GAGGUAG` тЖТ same family; miR-21-5p `AGCUUAU` differs); selfтЖТ0 mismatches. Domain context: TargetScan site ladder 8mer/7mer-m8/7mer-A1/6mer over the 2-7-vs-2-8 distinction, but matching-to-target + site-class assignment is deferred to target-site prediction (MIRNA-TARGET-001, future); seedтЖТtarget motif reverse complement is owned by [[rna-base-pairing]] (`GetReverseComplement`). **Intentionally simplified** тАФ exact-7-mer family equality (no isomiR/offset/noncanonical seeds, not a curated taxonomy); 2-7-vs-2-8 terminology collapse flagged, no source contradictions; record [[mirna-seed-001-evidence]].
- [[mirna-target-site-prediction]] тАФ MiRNA family target-site-prediction unit (fourth & **final** MiRNA unit, MIRNA-TARGET-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`, **completes** the family): finding mRNA target sites for a miRNA and classifying the **Bartel/TargetScan hierarchy**. `FindTargetSites(mRna, miRna, minScore=0.5)` = two-pass, `TтЖТU`, 0-based-inclusive antiparallel scan for the seed reverse complement (`seedRC=revcomp(mтВВтАжmтВИ)`, 6mer core `seedRC[2..7]`): pass-1 upgrades 6mer-core hits to **8mer** (pos 2-8 + A opposite pos 1) / **7mer-m8** (2-8) / **7mer-A1** (2-7 + A1) / **6mer** (2-7); pass-2 finds **offset-6mer** (3-8) only where not overlapping a retained higher-priority site (INV-04). Heuristic `ScoreтИИ[0,1]` (base 1.0/0.52/0.32/0.15/0.10, +0.05 >10 matches, тИТ0.01/mismatch) + heuristic `FreeEnergy` (sign-reliable) тАФ ranking aid, **not** calibrated repression. **Depends on** [[seed-sequence-analysis]] (the 2-8 seed determines targeting) + [[rna-base-pairing]] (`GetReverseComplement` motif + `AlignMiRnaToTarget` `|`/`:`/space duplex). **Opt-in `ScoreTargetSiteContextPlusPlus`** = source-fitted TargetScan **context++** (Agarwal 2015): per-site-type MLR, sum of `coeff├ЧscaledScore`, continuous features min-max scaled + indicators raw; realises Intercept/Local_AU/sRNA1/sRNA8/Site8/3P_score/Min_dist/Len_3UTR/Off6m, **computes** TA_3UTR=log10 N (`ComputeTa3Utr`, Garcia 2011) + SA (Turner-2004 McCaskill partition unpaired-prob) + PCT (Friedman BlsтЖТpublished sigmoid); SPS/Len_ORF/ORF8m/PCT-`b0..b3` caller-supplied (compiled TargetScan tables, not bundled) тЖТ honest **partial** `ContextScorePartial` + `OmittedFeatures` (8mer let-7a all-G-flank partial CS = тИТ0.7561913315126536). `Centered`/`Supplementary` enum members not emitted (accepted); bulged/centered/supplementary/noncanonical + isoforms out of scope; no contradictions; record [[mirna-target-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] тАФ RNA secondary-structure family **notation layer** (RNA-DOTBRACKET-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): parse an extended-**WUSS** structure string into base pairs `(i,j)` and validate well-formedness. `ParseDotBracket` uses **one stack per bracket family** тАФ `()`/`<>`/`{}`/`[]` + uppercase(5' open)/lowercase(3' close) letter pairs тАФ each an **independent pairing system** (ViennaRNA / Infernal `vrna_db_from_WUSS()`: any matched pair = a base pair, symbol has no meaning); a shared stack would mis-pair `([)]`. `ValidateDotBracket` тЯ║ every family's stack empty at end & never underflows; a closer must match a **same-family** opener. **Pseudoknots** (crossing families) are valid; `(]` (mismatched families) is not. Non-bracket WUSS symbols `-`/`,`/`:`/`.` are single-stranded (Rfam). Oracles `((((....))))`тЖТ4 pairs, `([)]`тЖТ(0,2)+(1,3), `<<<<[[[[....>>>>]]]]`тЙб`((((AAAA....))))aaaa`тЖТtwo crossing 4-bp helices; valid `(((...)))`/`(([[]]))`/`([)]`, invalid `(((...)` / `...)` / `)(` / `(]`. Notation-only (does not fold/score); distinct from the base-pairing chemistry [[rna-base-pairing]]; the structure the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] unit emits and the MFE folder reads. Two API-contract assumptions (malformedтЖТbest-effort parse; empty/nullтЖТvalid). Record [[rna-dotbracket-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] тАФ RNA secondary-structure family **energy layer** (RNA-ENERGY-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the individual **Turner 2004 nearest-neighbor free-energy terms** summed into a fold's ╬ФG┬░ at 37 ┬░C (`CalculateStackingEnergy`/`CalculateStemEnergy`/`CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy`/`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy`), all verified exact against **NNDB Turner04**. Model `╬ФG┬░total = init + ╬гstacking + ╬гloops`. **WC stacking all negative**, GC-rich most stable (`GC/CG` тИТ3.42, `GG/CC` тИТ3.26; `AA/UU` тИТ0.93); **G-U wobble variable** тАФ mostly negative but **two positive** (`UG/GU` +0.30, `GU/UG` +1.29), note-a `GG/UU`=тИТ0.5, **note-b special 3-stack** `5'GGUC/3'CUGG`=тИТ4.12 (vs тИТ1.77). **Hairpin-loop initiation positive and NOT monotonic** (3тЖТ5.4, 4тЖТ5.6, 6тЖТ5.4, 8тЖТ5.5, 9тЖТ6.4; Jacobson-Stockmayer `╬ФG(n)=╬ФG(9)+1.75RT┬╖ln(n/9)` beyond 9). **Special UNCG/GNRA tri/tetra/hexaloops** use NNDB total energies keyed by closing pair+loop (replace the model; GNRA>random). **All-C loop** penalty (3-nt +1.5, >3-nt 0.3n+1.6), terminal mismatch (96 entries), **+0.45 per-AU/GU-end**. A single base pair contributes **0** stacking (needs тЙе2 adjacent); empty/poly-AтЖТ0. Oracles GC 3-bp stem тИТ5.78, NNDB hairpin example-1 `GGGAUAAAUCCC` тИТ3.42, GGUC/CUGG тИТ4.12. The **energy** the folding units consume (pre-miRNA `FreeEnergy`, RNA-STRUCT-001 MFE), assigned to [[rna-base-pairing]] pairs, distinct from the [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] notation. No contradictions; three defined conditions (37 ┬░C, 2-dp, unknown stacksтЖТ0), not assumptions. Record [[rna-energy-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] тАФ RNA secondary-structure family **folding/search layer** (RNA-MFE-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the **ZukerтАУStiegler dynamic-programming MFE folder** that searches structure space for the fold of lowest total free energy (`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy` / `PredictStructure`). Loop decomposition (hairpin / stacking / bulge-interior / multibranch); DP matrices **C(i,j)=min(hairpin, interior/bulge over an inner pair, multiloop)** + multiloop **M** (тЙе1 component)/**M1** (exactly one) + exterior **F** (Ward 2017); **standard affine multiloop model тЖТ O(n┬│) time / O(n┬▓) space** ("simplest model is best"; logarithmic model would be O(nтБ┤)). The unit that **consumes** the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] Turner-2004 terms (summing them over candidate structures) and **produces** a [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] structure; builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. Oracles `CACAAAAAAAUGUG`тЖТ`((((......))))` тИТ1.41 (NNDB Example 1), `CACAGAAAGUGUG` тИТ1.91 (Example 2). Invariants MFE тЙд 0 (INV-01, empty structure always available), suffix-monotone `MFE(s) тЙд MFE(prefix)` (INV-02), optimized DP == classic O(n┬│) baseline (INV-03); empty/null / unfoldable homopolymer / sequence `< minLoopSize+2` тЖТ 0 (hairpin loop тЙе 3 nt); intramolecular тЗТ no helix-init constant. The folder the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] opt-in `AssessHairpinByMfe` path uses (once generically called *RNA-STRUCT-001* before that artifact was ingested тАФ RNA-STRUCT-001 is now the **distinct sibling** Nussinov predictor [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]], sharing this unit's Zuker MFE machinery). Two documented simplifications (multiloop per-unpaired `c=0`; 2-dp rounding), no source contradictions; sources Zuker & Stiegler 1981 + Lorenz 2011 (ViennaRNA) + Ward 2017 + NNDB Turner 2004 + Mathews 2004. Record [[rna-mfe-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]] тАФ RNA secondary-structure family **probabilistic/ensemble layer** (RNA-PARTITION-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the **McCaskill 1990** partition function тАФ the Boltzmann-weighted counterpart of MFE folding that computes the equilibrium `Z = ╬г_P exp(тИТE(P)/RT)` over all pseudoknot-free structures plus per-base-pair binding probabilities and the Boltzmann probability of a given structure, in **O(n┬│) time / O(n┬▓) space**. Inside recursion `Q_ij = Q_{i,j-1} + ╬г_{iтЙдk<j-m} Q_{i,k-1}┬╖Q^b_{kj}` (base `Q_ij=1` for iтЙеjтИТm), total **`Z = Q_{1n}`** (disjoint/unambiguous decomposition); pair probability needs the **outside** recursion `p_kl = Q^b_kl┬╖O_kl/Z` тАФ the external-only term is **wrong for nestable pairs** (`GGGAAACCC` P(2,6)=6/20 not 1/20; outside matches Boltzmann brute force to 3.3e-16). Oracles (E_bp=0 тЗТ Z counts structures) `AAAA`тЖТ1, `GC`тЖТ1, `GGGGCCCC`тЖТ16, `GGGAAACCC`тЖТ20; invariants Z тЙе 1 (empty structure weight 1), P(i,j) тИИ [0,1] + symmetric, per-base pairing sum тЙд 1, monotone in E_bp; WC + GU pairing only, min-loop forbids jтИТk тЙд m. The **`alternative_to` / ensemble counterpart** of the single-optimum [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] MFE folder; Boltzmann-weights the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] energies (ViennaRNA default 37 ┬░C = Turner standard); builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. One simplification (fixed-per-pair `E_bp` energy model vs full Turner NN тАФ energy model only, invariants conformant with McCaskill 1990), no source contradictions. Record [[rna-partition-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] тАФ RNA secondary-structure family **crossing-helix layer** (RNA-PKPREDICT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain a single **canonical H-type pseudoknot** тАФ two helices whose pairs **cross** (`i<k<j<l`), the one feature the nested [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] and [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill|McCaskill ensemble]] cannot represent. **pknotsRG class** (Reeder & Giegerich 2004): "two crossing helices with three intervening loops", H-type 5'тЖТ3' stem1-5'тЖТloop1тЖТstem2-5'тЖТloop2тЖТstem1-3'тЖТloop3тЖТstem2-3', two-layer dot-bracket `((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]`; full grammar **O(nтБ┤)/O(n┬▓)**. Canonization rules (equal-length bulge-free helices / maximal extent / fixed overlap boundary) bound the search. Energy = Turner NN stacking on **both** helices (same model as nested, `Energy.lhs`) + penalties **initiation 9.0** (anti-spurious-knot gate тАФ a knot is reported only when it beats both the penalty and the best nested alternative) / **unpaired loop nt 0.3** / **base pair inside knot 0.0** kcal/mol. **Depends on** [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] (helix scoring) and [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] (MFE fallback baseline `FreeEnergy тЙд CalculateMfeStructure().FreeEnergy` + folds internal loops); emits two-layer [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]]; builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. Oracles designed H-type `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`тЖТknot with two crossing 4-bp helices; plain `GGGGAAAACCCC`тЖТno knot = MFE; BWYV `GGCGCGGCACCGUCCGCGGAACAAACGG` (PDB 437D) **not** recovered (tertiary-stabilized, outside NN model тАФ documented limit of all NN-only pseudoknot predictors). Two boundaries: PARTIAL pknotsRG coverage (single H-type only; recursive/over-arching/multiple knots not implemented) + tertiary-stabilized knots not recovered. No contradictions. Record [[rna-pkpredict-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] тАФ RNA secondary-structure family **crossing detection layer** (RNA-PSEUDOKNOT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure.DetectPseudoknots`): given a **set of base pairs** describing a known structure, a pure **O(n┬▓) combinatorial scan** finds every **crossing** pair-of-pairs `i<k<j<l` (Antczak 2018) тАФ one pair's opener inside the other while its closer lies outside. Two exhaustive negatives: **nested** `i<k<l<j` (one pair fully inside) and **disjoint** `j<k` (side-by-side). Each crossing pair-of-pairs = one pseudoknot (binary relation); тЙе2 pairs required, endpoints normalized min-max to open<close, deterministic. Oracles `([)]`=(0,2)+(1,3)тЖТone, nested (0,5)+(1,4)тЖТnone, disjoint (0,2)+(3,5)тЖТnone. The **detection/analysis facet** тАФ genuinely distinct from the energy-driven [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] predictor (input = pair set vs sequence, machinery = combinatorial scan vs Turner-NN energy DP, cost = O(n┬▓) vs O(nтБ┤)) тАФ and the crossing primitive that predictor's validity invariant leans on. Operates on the pairs the [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] parser emits; complements the nested-only [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] / [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]]. One scope note: pseudoknot-**order** assignment (Antczak DBL layering / Smit 2008 removal) Not Implemented. Sources Antczak 2018 + Smit & Knight 2008 + biotite + Wikipedia, no contradictions. Record [[rna-pseudoknot-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-stem-loop-enumeration]] тАФ RNA secondary-structure family **enumeration layer** (RNA-STEMLOOP-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): **scan a sequence for every stem-loop (hairpin)** it can form under size constraints тАФ `FindStemLoops(sequence, minStem, minLoop, maxLoop, allowWobble)` / `FindHairpins`, extending an antiparallel WC/wobble stem outward around each candidate loop, **O(n┬▓┬╖L)**. The general, sequence-agnostic hairpin *finder* тАФ distinct from the single-optimal-fold [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] (O(n┬│) DP), the hairpin *energy* unit [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]], and the miRNA-specific [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] precursor detector. Loop **тЙе3 nt** (steric floor, shared with the MFE/Turner units), optimal **4-8 nt**. **Tetraloops** тАФ GNRA / UNCG / CUUG, UUCG the most stable, UUCG+GNRA ~70% of 16S-rRNA tetraloops, ~3.0 kcal/mol bonus via [[rna-free-energy-turner-model|Turner 2004]]. `FindPseudoknots` shares the `i<k<j<l` crossing primitive with [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]. Builds on [[rna-base-pairing]], emits [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]]. Invariants non-overlap / тЙд1 pair per base / contiguous loop / antiparallel stem; limitations no PK-from-sequence, simplified energy, hairpin loops only, single structure. Record [[rna-stemloop-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]] тАФ RNA secondary-structure family **top-level prediction umbrella** (RNA-STRUCT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict a structure from a sequence by a **Nussinov base-pair-maximizing** DP тАФ `Predict` / `PredictWithConstraints` (forced pairs, Mathews 2004) / `ToDotBracket` / `FromDotBracket`. Nussinov & Jacobson 1980 O(n┬│)/O(n┬▓) maximizes the **(weighted) base-pair count** (WC тИТ2.0 / wobble тИТ1.0), signalling **relative stability, not physical energy units** тАФ the **`alternative_to`** the physical Turner-kcal/mol [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] (RNA-MFE-001), same problem / different objective. A **distinct sibling** test unit, **not an alias** of RNA-MFE-001: both share the `RnaSecondaryStructure` Zuker MFE machinery (this unit's D5 added `CalculateMfeStructure`/`PredictStructureMfe`). Builds on [[rna-base-pairing]], converts to/from [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]], consumes [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] stem-loop terms, shares the `i<k<j<l` crossing test with [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] (detects, never predicts, pseudoknots). Oracles `GGGGAAAACCCC`тЖТ`((((....))))`, poly-AтЖТMFE 0; min loop 3 nt (steric), single-sequence only, int21/int22 lookup tables blocked. Record [[rna-struct-001-evidence]].
- [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]] тАФ Oncology family anchor (first ONCO-* unit, ONCO-ACTION-001): **clinical actionability assessment** by the OncoKB Therapeutic Levels of Evidence (Chakravarty 2017). A **pure ranking** тАФ given a variant's caller-supplied leveled drug associations, return the **maximum** level under the fixed combined order `R1 > 1 > 2 > 3A > 3B > 4 > R2` (sensitivity axis `1 > 2 > 3A > 3B > 4`, resistance axis `R1 > R2`), the two axes reported separately (a variant may carry both); no leveled association тЖТ **NotActionable**. Seven tiers: 1 (FDA in-indication) / 2 (NCCN in-indication) / 3A (clinical evidence in-indication) / 3B (another indication) / 4 (biological evidence) / R1 (standard resistance) / R2 (investigational resistance); 1/2/R1 = standard vs 3A/3B/4/R2 = investigational (SOP v3, consistent with AMP/ASCO/CAP Li 2017). **Knowledgebase is a caller input** тАФ the library ranks, it does not embed/annotate the OncoKB DB; NotActionable-name is the library's; not for clinical use; record [[onco-action-001-evidence]].
- [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] тАФ Oncology family, second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ANNOT-001): **cancer variant tier classification** by the **AMP/ASCO/CAP 2017 four-tier** consensus (Li MM et al. 2017). A **pure decision rule** over caller-supplied evidence level (AтАУD) + population MAF + cancer-association flag тЖТ **Tier I** (strong, Level A/B) / **II** (potential, Level C/D) / **III** (unknown, no level + rare + cancer assoc) / **IV** (benign, no level + MAF тЙе 1% **or** no assoc). Population frequency is the **IIIтЖФIV discriminator**; **evidence level dominates frequency** (a significant biomarker stays Tier I at high MAF). 1% (0.01) is the guideline **primary benign cutoff**, inclusive (MAF 0.01 тЖТ Tier IV). `AnnotateCancerVariants` = one annotation per variant in input order; `GetCOSMICAnnotation` = null-on-miss lookup against a **caller-supplied** COSMIC catalog (external DB, not embedded). Distinct from but **consistent with** the sibling OncoKB level-ranking [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; not for clinical use; record [[onco-annot-001-evidence]].
- [[sequencing-artifact-detection]] тАФ Oncology family, third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ARTIFACT-001): **sequencing artifact detection** (`FilterArtifacts`) тАФ the **QC** sibling that removes false-positive somatic calls from DNA damage / mapping bias **before** clinical interpretation (distinct from the two clinical-significance ONCO units). Three disjoint signals: **substitution class** (OxoG oxidation G>T/C>A per Chen 2017 vs FFPE cytosine-deamination C>T/G>A per Do & Dobrovic 2015; else not-an-artifact), the **GIV** read-pair imbalance ratio (`GIV_G_T = count(G>T in R1)/count(G>T in R2)`, neutral 1 / damaged > 1.5, Chen 2017 + Damage-estimator), and **FisherStrand** FS = тИТ10┬╖log10(two-sided Fisher-exact p) on the `[ref_fwd,ref_rev,alt_fwd,alt_rev]` 2├Ч2 table (GATK, FS тЙИ 0 no bias / high = artifact). Result тКЖ input; **no BAM parser** (per-strand/read-mate evidence supplied on the variant record); GIV thresholds from the Nature Methods summary; not for clinical use; record [[onco-artifact-001-evidence]].
- [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] тАФ Oncology family, fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ASCAT-001): the **upstream tumor copy-number layer** тАФ allele-specific integer copy number (nA/nB) from per-locus **logR/BAF** by a joint **purity ╧Б / ploidy ╧И** grid fit (**ASCAT**, Van Loo 2010: `nA/nB` inversion, minimise length-weighted squared minor-allele distance to non-negative integers, BAF=0.5 down-weighted ├Ч0.05, GoF = (1тИТd/maxdist)┬╖100, **╬│=1 for sequencing**). Four disjoint stages: (1) ASCAT core (╧Б,╧И) fit; (2) **ASPCF** penalised-least-squares joint segmentation `L=╬г(yтИТ╚│)┬▓+╬│|S|` via O(n┬▓) DP (Nilsen 2012) with common change points + BAF mirroring (Ross 2021); (3) **subclonal** two-state mixture `n_obs=f┬╖nтВБ+(1тИТf)┬╖nтВВ` over bracketing integers (Battenberg / Nik-Zainal 2012); (4) **multiplicity/CCF** VAF inversion `VAF=(m┬╖CCF┬╖p)/(c┬╖p+2(1тИТp))`, clamp m to [1,major-CN] (McGranahan 2016 / PICTograph / DeCiFering). Planted-truth tests invert the forward model (╧БтВА=0.80, ╧ИтВАтИИ{2,3}). The allele-specific/clonal counterpart to the total-CN [[aneuploidy-detection]]; substrate beneath the clinical-interpretation ONCO siblings; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ascat-001-evidence]].
- [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] тАФ Oncology family, fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CCF-001): the **downstream clonal-structure layer** тАФ estimate each mutation's **cancer cell fraction** `CCF = f┬╖(╧Б┬╖N_T+2(1тИТ╧Б))/(╧Б┬╖m)` (`EstimateCCF`; McGranahan 2016 / PICTograph / Tarabichi 2021, corroborated three ways; m тИИ [1,tumor CN], ╧Б тИИ (0,1]) with a reported-value **[0,1] cap** that exposes the uncapped raw (the raw formula can exceed 1 тАФ CNAqc 1.06 noise case), then **`ClusterCCFValues`** deconvolutes the CCF vector into clones/subclones by a **deterministic 1D Lloyd k-means** (Lloyd 1982, quantile seeding, no RNG) with **highest-centroid = clonal** (Tarabichi 2021). Consumes the purity ╧Б / copy number N_T / multiplicity m from the upstream [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (whose ┬з4 carries the same CCF closed form); two source-consistent assumptions ([0,1] cap; Lloyd k-means as the concrete 1D method); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ccf-001-evidence]].
- [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] тАФ Oncology family, sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CHIP-001): the **pre-interpretation biological-origin filter** for liquid biopsy тАФ removes **clonal-hematopoiesis (CHIP)** false positives, the dominant cfDNA confounder (Razavi 2019: 81.6% controls / 53.2% cancer). `IdentifyCHIPVariants` flags a driver-gene variant ({DNMT3A,TET2,ASXL1,TP53,JAK2,SF3B1,SRSF2,PPM1D}, top-3 DNMT3A/TET2/ASXL1) at **VAF тЙе 0.02** (Steensma 2015 / Genovese 2014); `FilterCHIP` removes CH calls by **matched-WBC subtraction** (present in matched WBC тЗТ blood-derived, the definitive origin test, Razavi 2019) plus a **conservative labelled gene+VAF heuristic fallback** (over-removes; strict mode = empty gene panel); `CallVariantOrigin` = the strict **Bolton 2020** rule (WBC VAF тЙе 2% AND тЙе 10 reads AND тЙе ╧Ж├Ч tumour VAF, ╧Ж=2.0 / 1.5 lymph node). The **biological-origin sibling** of the technical-artifact QC filter [[sequencing-artifact-detection]], upstream of the clinical-interpretation and clonal-structure ONCO units; two source-consistent assumptions (canonical default gene set, тЙе1-alt-read WBC presence test); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-chip-001-evidence]].
- [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]] тАФ Oncology family, seventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CLONAL-001): the **probabilistic clonal-structure classifier** тАФ per-mutation **Bayesian CCF posterior** `P(c) тИЭ Binom(a|N,f(c))` (uniform prior, 100-point grid `cтИИ[0.01,1]`) with expected allele fraction `f(c) = ╬▒Mc/(2(1тИТ╬▒)+╬▒q)` (Landau 2013 ABSOLUTE-style; multiplicity M generalisation, Satas 2021 DeCiFering Eq. 1), classified **clonal iff `P(CCF>0.95) > 0.5`** (two distinct thresholds: 0.95 CCF cut, 0.5 posterior-mass cut) via `ClassifyClonality(variants, purity)`, plus the point-estimate `IdentifyClonalMutations` (strict CCF > 0.95, boundary excluded тЖТ indices {0,2,4}). The **`alternative_to`** the point-estimate + Lloyd-k-means [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] тАФ same clonal/subclonal question, but classifies each mutation on its own read-count uncertainty without clustering; consumes purity ╬▒ / local copy number q / multiplicity M from the upstream [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]]; one API-shape assumption (per-variant local copy number q over a genome-wide ploidy scalar); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-clonal-001-evidence]].
- [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] тАФ Oncology family, eighth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-001): the **total-copy-number classification layer** тАФ a single **log2 copy ratio** тЖТ absolute integer CN `n = 2┬╖2^log2` (CNVkit `_log2_ratio_to_absolute_pure`, diploid ref_copies=2) тЖТ discrete **CNA state** via CNVkit's `absolute_threshold` hard-threshold caller (default `тИТ1.1/тИТ0.25/0.2/0.7` тЖТ DeepDeletion/Loss/Neutral/Gain/Amplification; CN = index of the **first** threshold with `log2 <= thresh`, **boundary-inclusive тЖТ lower bin**; above the last тЖТ `ceil(2┬╖2^log2)` open-ended Amplification; NaN тЖТ neutral CN 2), corroborated by **GISTIC2** (Mermel 2011: ┬▒0.1 noise band subsumed by the neutral bin + +0.848/тИТ0.737 high-amplitude cutoffs). The **total-CN** counterpart to the allele-specific [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] and the per-segment oncology-state sibling of the whole-chromosome [[aneuploidy-detection]] (both share the `n = 2┬╖2^log2` conversion); distinct from SV-CNV-001's `round`-based integer CN (no state classification). One diploid-ploidy=2 assumption; threshold-variant note (docs germline `тИТ0.4/0.3` vs code tumor `тИТ0.25/0.2`); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-001-evidence]].
- [[focal-amplification-detection]] тАФ Oncology family, ninth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-002): the **focal-amplification layer** тАФ a two-part predicate `DetectFocalAmplifications` keeps segments both **amplified** (log2 gain > GISTIC2 `t_amp` 0.1) **and** **focal** (SegLen / ArmLength < `broad_len_cutoff` 0.98 тАФ Mermel 2011's length-based, not amplitude-based, focal-vs-arm-level split; strict `< 0.98`, exactly 0.98 тЖТ arm-level), then `IdentifyAmplifiedOncogenes` maps each focal amplification's arm prefix to a built-in oncogene panel (17qтЖТERBB2 ┬╖ 8qтЖТMYC ┬╖ 7pтЖТEGFR ┬╖ 11qтЖТCCND1 ┬╖ 12qтЖТMDM2 **and** CDK4, NCBI Gene cytobands). Orthogonal to the log2тЖТ5-state [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) тАФ a **length** question, not an amplitude bin тАФ sharing only the GISTIC2 `t_amp`=0.1 amplitude gate. Sources GISTIC2 Mermel 2011 + GISTIC2 docs (`broad_len_cutoff`/`t_amp`) + CNVkit (single-copy gain log2 0.585 > 0.1) + NCBI Gene. Worked oracles A 17q 0.50тЖТERBB2 / B 8q 0.99 arm-level / C 7p log2 0.05 not-amplified / D 11q 0.98 boundary. Two assumptions (amplitude+length fusion; caller-supplied arm label + length, no cytoband table); deletions out of scope (ONCO-CNA-003); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-002-evidence]].
- [[homozygous-deletion-detection]] тАФ Oncology family, tenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-003): the **deep-deletion layer**, the **deletion mirror of ONCO-CNA-002** тАФ filter segments whose classified integer copy number is **exactly 0** (a homozygous / deep deletion: cBioPortal `тИТ2` "Deep Deletion", Cheng et al. 2017 "zero copies of both alleles" / two hits; **reuses** [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]'s CN-0 = `DeepDeletion` call, **no new threshold**), then `IdentifyDeletedTumorSuppressors` maps each arm prefix to a built-in tumour-suppressor panel (17pтЖТTP53 ┬╖ 13qтЖТRB1 **and** BRCA2 ┬╖ 9pтЖТCDKN2A ┬╖ 10qтЖТPTEN ┬╖ 17qтЖТBRCA1, NCBI Gene cytobands). A single-copy loss (`тИТ1`, heterozygous, CN тЙе 1) is NOT a homozygous deletion. The loss-side counterpart of the amplification unit [[focal-amplification-detection]] (`IdentifyDeletedTumorSuppressors` mirrors `IdentifyAmplifiedOncogenes`) and a consumer of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]'s CN-0 state. Two assumptions (CN-0 reuse, caller-fixed panel); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-003-evidence]].
- [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] тАФ Oncology family, eleventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CTDNA-001): the liquid-biopsy **quantification / limit-of-detection** layer for **circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA)** тАФ the Poisson detection probability `DetectionProbability` **p = 1 тИТ e^(тИТn┬╖d┬╖k)** (n genome equivalents, d mutant allele fraction, k reporters; Patent US 11,085,084 restating Avanzini 2020, corroborated by Pessoa 2023's ╬╗ = n┬╖d = 15) with a detectability test (caller threshold default 0.95 **and** ╬╗ = n┬╖d┬╖k тЙе 1; only p is non-assumption), **`CalculateTumorFraction` = 2 ├Ч mean clonal-heterozygous VAF** (copy-neutral diploid, CNAqc/Antonello 2024 v = ╧А/2), `CalculateMeanVaf` = mean altReads/totalReads across reporters (Newman 2014 CAPP-Seq across-reporter fraction, detection 0.025%тАУ10%), and a genome-equivalents helper (3.3 pg/haploid, Devonshire 2014 тЗТ тЙИ303 GE/ng, Alcaide 2020). The **quantification counterpart** on the same cfDNA input as the biological-origin filter [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] (measures signal vs filters it), sharing the diploid-heterozygous VAF inversion with [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] / [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]; underpins MRD monitoring; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ctdna-001-evidence]].
- [[driver-gene-classification-20-20-rule]] тАФ Oncology family, twelfth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-DRIVER-001): the **gene-level** driver classifier тАФ the Vogelstein 2013 **20/20 rule** classifying a cancer gene **Oncogene** (> 20% missense at **recurrent** positions, тЙе 2├Ч = activating), **TumorSuppressor** (> 20% **truncating / inactivating** тАФ nonsense / frameshift / splice donor-acceptor / stop gain-loss = loss of function), or **Ambiguous** (neither criterion, or exact dual-pass tie), via `IdentifyDriverMutations` (driver тКЖ somatic) + `MatchCancerHotspots` (caller-supplied (gene, position) hotspot set) + `ScoreDriverPotential` (= max of the two criterion fractions in [0,1]; CADD/SIFT/PolyPhen are caller-supplied, not implemented). Oracles: IDH1 10 missense@codon 132 тЖТ recurrent-missense 1.00 тЖТ Oncogene; dispersed 8/10 truncating тЖТ 0.80 тЖТ TumorSuppressor; truncating exactly 0.20 тЖТ NOT TSG (strict `>`). A **heuristic, not a statistical test** (passenger truncations / low-recurrence drivers mislead it; 20/20+ / MutSigCV successors out of scope), **orthogonal** to the variant-level clinical classifiers [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] and [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]. Three assumptions (strict `> 0.20`, dual-pass tie-break by larger fraction with Ambiguous on tie, ScoreDriverPotential proxy); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-driver-001-evidence]].
- [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]] тАФ Oncology family, thirteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-EXPR-001), and the wiki's **first expression/transcriptome method**: the per-gene **outlier z-score** `z = (r тИТ ╬╝)/╧Г` against a caller-supplied **reference (base) population** (cBioPortal's diploid or all-samples convention) with **╧Г = sample SD, divisor (n тИТ 1)** (settled by `NormalizeExpressionLevels.java`), classified over/under-expressed under the **strict ┬▒2** default threshold (exactly ┬▒2 is NOT an outlier), plus the **combined-z signature/pathway activity** `a = (╬гс╡в zс╡в)/тИЪk` (Lee et al. 2008, the GSVA `zscore` method). Zero-SD reference **throws** (reference-code `fatalError`, a behavioural deviation from the prose "z тЖР NA" spec тАФ the two cBioPortal sources disagree); reference `{2,2,4,6,6}` тЖТ ╧Г=2 so x=10тЖТ3.0 over / x=8тЖТ2.0 boundary-not-outlier / x=4тЖТ0.0 / x=тИТ1тЖТтИТ2.5 under, signature `{3,1,тИТ1,1}`тЖТ2.0 & single-gene `{2.5}`тЖТ2.5 oracles. **Orthogonal** to the copy-number / clonal-structure ONCO units ([[copy-number-alteration-classification]], [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]) тАФ the diploid reference option touches copy number only as an input filter. Two scope assumptions (caller-supplied cohort + signature; inputs pre-normalized) + one behavioural deviation (throw not NA); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-expr-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] тАФ Oncology family, fourteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-001), and the wiki's **first gene-fusion / read-evidence structural-rearrangement method**: the STAR-Fusion / Arriba **split-read + discordant-pair + minimum-support** candidate-fusion caller (BCR-ABL1 / EML4-ALK / TMPRSS2-ERG). **DETECTED** iff (junction тЙе `MIN_JUNCTION_READS`=1 AND total тЙе `MIN_SUM_FRAGS`=2) OR (zero junction AND discordant тЙе `MIN_SPANNING_FRAGS_ONLY`=5), where **total support = split_reads1 + split_reads2 + discordant_mates** (Arriba) and the **gene5p тЙа gene3p** distinct-gene invariant rejects self-fusions; results ordered by descending support (STAR-Fusion scores by "abundance of fusion-supporting reads"). Plus a standalone **exon-phase in-frame** check `(5' coding bases тИТ 3' start phase) mod 3 == 0` (Genomics England / Wikipedia Reading-frame). Oracles: EML4-ALK(3,2,4)/TMPRSS2-ERG(1,0,1)/CD74-ROS1(0,0,5) DETECTED, NCOA4-RET(0,0,4) span<5 / KIF5B-RET(1,0,0) sum<2 / ALK-ALK same-gene REJECTED, frame 300/0тЖТin 301/0тЖТout 301/1тЖТin. Consumes **already-grouped candidate breakpoint counts** (Arriba schema, not raw BAM тАФ chimeric-read extraction is a separate `FindChimericReads`) and does **not** scan for a premature stop before the junction (Arriba `stop-codon` value, ONCO-FUSION-003 scope). **Orthogonal** to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units, distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]. Two scope assumptions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-fusion-nomenclature-known-fusion-lookup]] тАФ Oncology family, fifteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-002), the wiki's fusion **annotation/naming** method: the **HGNC gene-fusion designation** `GetFusionAnnotation(5p,3p) = "5p::3p"` (Bruford et al. 2021 тАФ `::` double-colon separator, **5тА▓-partner-first** directional order irrespective of chromosomal location, HGNC approved symbols, read-throughs keep the hyphen `INS-IGF2`) plus the **directional known-fusion match** `MatchKnownFusions` against a **caller-supplied** set keyed by `5тА▓::3тА▓`, case-insensitive. A **Framework** algorithm тАФ format/keying source-backed (Bruford 2021 + consortium extension letter), set contents caller-supplied (no bundled Mitelman/COSMIC/ChimerDB). `BCR::ABL1` worked example; `A::B тЙа B::A` reciprocal-direction and hyphen тЙа `::` corner cases; null/empty rejected. The **naming layer downstream** of the read-evidence caller [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] (annotation round-trips through a `DetectFusions` `FusionCall`), distinct from the ONCO-FUSION-003 premature-stop scope; orthogonal to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units. Two assumptions (caller-supplied set, case-insensitivity); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-002-evidence]].
- [[fusion-breakpoint-frame-and-protein-prediction]] тАФ Oncology family, sixteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-003), the **protein-consequence** third member of the fusion trio: given a fusion breakpoint it computes the **four-state** `BreakpointFrameStatus` (`InFrame`/`OutOfFrame`/`StopCodon`/`NotPredicted`) and reconstructs the **fusion protein**. Follows **Arriba's two-way** native-frame model (Uhrig 2021 `reading_frame`/`site` columns) тАФ the in/out call is whether the 3тА▓ gene is read in its NATIVE frame via the exon-phase rule `(5' coding bases тИТ 3' start phase) mod 3 == 0` (reused from [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] ONCO-FUSION-001) тАФ deliberately **not** AGFusion's three-way class (`in-frame (with mutation)`, contiguous ORF multiple-of-3 but 3тА▓ frameshifted, maps to **`OutOfFrame`**). Gated by breakpoint-site classification: a breakpoint in UTR/intron/non-coding-exon/intergenic тЖТ `NotPredicted`. `PredictFusionProtein` follows AGFusion `model.py` exactly: 5тА▓ CDS prefix + 3тА▓ CDS suffix тЖТ concatenate тЖТ translate (transl_table=1) тЖТ **truncate at first stop** (out-of-frame trims to whole codons first). Oracles `ATGAAA|GATGGT`тЖТ`MKDG`, `ATGAAA|GATTAAGGT`тЖТ`MKD` (in-frame premature stop), `ATGA|AAGGT` phase-0тЖТ`OutOfFrame` yet clean `MKG` (the Arriba-vs-AGFusion divergence point) / phase-1тЖТin-frame, `ATGAA|GATGGT`тЖТtrim-to-9 `MKM`. Downstream of ONCO-FUSION-001 (elaborates its binary in-frame check into a full consequence + transcript/peptide reconstruction, the premature-stop scope both siblings deferred here), orthogonal to the naming unit [[gene-fusion-nomenclature-known-fusion-lookup]] and to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units. One API-shape assumption (caller supplies CDS strings + junction offsets, no bundled GTF); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-003-evidence]].
- [[intratumor-heterogeneity-metrics]] тАФ Oncology family, seventeenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HETERO-001): the **scalar-summary ITH-metric layer** that reduces the reconstructed clonal structure to comparable numbers тАФ the **MATH score** `100┬╖1.4826┬╖median(|VAFтИТmedian VAF|)/median(VAF)` (Mroz & Rocco 2013 / Mroz 2015 / maftools `mathScore.R`, three-way identical; the ratio of the width to the centre of the mutant-allele-fraction distribution, no clustering needed), the **Shannon clonal diversity** `H = тИТ╬г pс╡в ln pс╡в` (natural log, Liu 2017 / Shannon 1948), the **subclone count** (Liu richness = number of occupied CCF clusters), and the **subclonal fraction** `#(CCF<0.95)/n` (Landau 2013 threshold). MATH oracles 49.42 (odd) / 59.304 (even); Shannon 0 / ln2 / ln4; zero-median-VAFтЖТthrow, MAD=0тЖТMATH=0. **Depends on** [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] (subclone count + Shannon pс╡в consume its CCF clusters) and reuses the 0.95 clonal threshold of [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]]; a summary layer, NOT per-mutation reconstruction; shares the Shannon-index math but not the domain with [[alpha-diversity]]. Two source-consistent assumptions (Shannon pс╡в = per-cluster mutation proportions; R even-count median); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hetero-001-evidence]].
- [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] тАФ Oncology family, eighteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HLA-001), the wiki's **first HLA / immuno-oncology antigen-presentation method**: two disjoint pieces sharing the HLA locus тАФ (1) **HLA allele nomenclature parsing/validation** of the WHO IPD-IMGT/HLA name `HLA-[Gene]*[F1]:[F2][:F3][:F4][suffix]` (Marsh 2010 colon-delimited convention; Field1 type/allele-group / Field2 specific protein / Field3 synonymous / Field4 non-coding; **two-field "four-digit" minimum**, four-field maximum, `HLA-` prefix required, numeric fields, `N/L/S/C/A/Q` expression-suffix set тАФ `HLA-A*24:02:01:02L` valid, `HLA-A*02`/`A*02:01`/five-fields/`тАжX` rejected), and (2) **allele-specific HLA LOH** by the **LOHHLA** rule (McGranahan 2017 *Cell* / `mskcc/lohhla`): per-allele copy number from tumor-vs-germline logR + BAF, call HLA LOH iff min copy number **< 0.5** AND allelic-imbalance paired Student's t-test **p < 0.01** тАФ both strict `<`, the p-test the explicit "avoid over-calling LOH" guard; oracles (1.8, 0.30, 0.001)тЖТLOH allele 2 / (1.60, 0.40, 0.05)тЖТno (pтЙе0.01) / (1.50, 0.50, 0.001)тЖТno (0.5 not <0.5) / (1.70, 0.40, 0.01)тЖТno (0.01 not <0.01); the **HLA-locus specialization** of the genome-wide allele-specific copy-number / LOH derivation [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (same logR + BAF allelic-contrast idea restricted to the HLA genes), a mechanism of immune escape via lost neoantigen presentation; one assumption (both alleles <0.5 тЖТ distinct `HomozygousLoss` label, thresholds unchanged); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hla-001-evidence]].
- [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] тАФ Oncology family, nineteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HRD-001): the **HRD composite genomic-scar score** `HRD = LOH + TAI + LST`, an **unweighted sum** of three large-scale copy-number scar counts with the **HRD-high cutoff тЙе 42** inclusive (Telli 2016 + Stewart 2022, independently corroborated). All three components **derived per segment** from the [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] major/minor CN substrate in `DetectHRD(segments)`: **HRD-LOH** = LOH regions > 15 Mb & < whole chromosome, excluding whole-chr-LOH chromosomes (Abkevich 2012 / oncoscanR / scarHRD `calc.hrd.R`, no centromere table needed); **TAI** = imbalanced (major тЙа minor CN) segments reaching a sub-telomere but not crossing the centromere (Birkbak 2012 / scarHRD `calc.ai_new.R`, sub-1 Mb dropped, single-segment whole-chr imbalance excluded); **LST** = adjacent тЙе 10 Mb same-arm regions separated by < 3 Mb after iterative 3 Mb smoothing (Popova 2012 / scarHRD `calc.lst.R`, autosomes only). TAI + LST need the per-chromosome centromere `[start,end]` **acen** table embedded for GRCh38/GRCh37 (UCSC cytoBand cross-verified vs NCBI GRC тАФ resolving the prior "centromere table unretrievable" blocker). Oracles (14,14,14)тЖТ42 HRD-high / (14,13,14)тЖТ41 negative / (0,0,0)тЖТ0. The genomic-scar aggregation layer above [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]], distinct from the total-CN [[aneuploidy-detection]]; one even-ploidy AI-path assumption; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hrd-001-evidence]].
- [[immune-infiltration-deconvolution]] тАФ Oncology family, twentieth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-IMMUNE-001), the wiki's **second expression/transcriptome method**: **immune infiltration estimation** тАФ quantifies the tumor immune microenvironment two ways. (1) **Cell-type deconvolution** of the linear mixture `m = S┬╖f` (╬гf=1, fтЙе0): CIBERSORT **╬╜-SVR** `DeconvoluteImmuneCellsNuSvr` (Newman 2015 / Sch├╢lkopf 2000 linear-kernel ╬╜-SVR тАФ z-standardize m + signature columns, sweep ╬╜тИИ{0.25,0.5,0.75} by **lowest RMSE**, zero-clip negatives + normalize to ╬г=1; cross-validated by planted-truth `m=S┬╖f` recovery + scikit-learn `NuSVR`/libsvm match) with the NNLS/LLSR baseline `DeconvoluteImmuneCells` (Abbas 2009) retained. (2) **ESTIMATE** ssGSEA immune/stromal enrichment `EstimateInfiltration` (**simplified** = rank-weighted mean of signature genes, not full KS running-sum) + opt-in **tumor purity** `EstimateTumorPurity` = `cos(0.6049872018 + 0.0001467884┬╖ESTIMATE)` (verbatim, confirmed 3 sources + tidyestimate R; **Affymetrix-only** calibration, negative cosine тЖТ **NaN**, monotone-decreasing). MCP-counter geometric-mean marker abundance noted. Signature matrices: **LM22** (547 genes ├Ч 22 cell types) **caller-supplied** тАФ Stanford licence forbids redistribution/modification/commercial use, no exact-CIBERSORT parity claim, `LoadSignatureMatrix` LM22-format loader only; **ABIS-Seq** (Monaco 2019, CC BY 4.0, 1296 genes ├Ч 17 types) **bundled** as embedded resource via `LoadBundledAbisSignatureMatrix` so deconvolution works out-of-the-box (not an LM22 substitute); synthetic 5-marker `DefaultSignatureMatrix` for tests. Oracles: planted {CD8 0.60,B_naive 0.30,Mono 0.10}тЖТ{0.5971,0.2989,0.1040} corr 0.99997; sklearn cross-check ╬╜=0.75 {A 0.5085,B 0.1795,C 0.3120}; ABIS {NK 0.60,MonoC 0.40}тЖТ{тЙИ0.650,тЙИ0.350} corr 0.996 (tol 0.06) & pure MonoC 1.0 exactly; ABIS ref `CD8A`/T CD8 Mem=1060.1507652944399. Corner cases: collinear cell types (resting/activated NK) recover support but looser proportions; missing/non-overlapping genes тЖТ unreliable/zero; non-hematopoietic content in residual; ESTIMATE solid-tumors-only. Antigen-agnostic quantitative sibling of the immuno-oncology [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]], shares the ssGSEA signature-scoring layer with [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]]; two scope assumptions (LM22 caller-supplied, simplified ssGSEA) + Affymetrix purity domain, no contradictions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-immune-001-evidence]].
- [[loss-of-heterozygosity-detection]] тАФ Oncology family, twenty-first ONCO-* unit (ONCO-LOH-001): the standalone genome-wide **LOH caller** тАФ `DetectLOH` counts **HRD-LOH** regions (minor CN 0 **and** major CN тЙа 0 = allelic loss not homozygous deletion; length **strictly > 15 Mb**, length = end тИТ start; excluding any **whole-chromosome** global-LOH chromosome via `chrDel`) and `CalculateLOHFraction` returns the length-weighted per-chromosome LOH fraction тИИ [0,1]. Abkevich 2012 (intermediate-size LOH тЖФ BRCA1/2 deficiency) + scarHRD `calc.hrd.R`/`scar_score.R` (exact R criterion + 15 Mb cut-off + `chrDel`; major CN capped to 1 so LOH state, not absolute CN, drives merging) + oncoscanR `score_loh` (independent corroboration; adjacent/overlapping LOH merged тЙд 1 bp first). Synthetic 7-segment dataset тЖТ score **1** (only the 20 Mb chr1 segment; exactly-15 Mb / het-retained / homozygous-deletion / whole-chr-LOH all excluded); LOH-fraction 0.333/0.0/1.0. This **is** the LOH term the composite [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] sums with TAI + LST (centromere-free, unlike its siblings), reads its segments off [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]], and is the genome-wide counterpart of the HLA-locus [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (LOHHLA). Two assumptions (segment input shape; length-weighted LOH-fraction is a definitional/API choice); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-loh-001-evidence]].
- [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] тАФ Oncology family, twenty-second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MHC-001): the wiki's first **MHC / peptide-presentation prediction** method тАФ the affinity gate of neoantigen candidate scoring, three layers over one `Strong`/`Weak`/`NonBinder` output. (1) **Classification**: IC50 tiers `< 50` Strong / `< 500` Weak / `тЙе 500` NonBinder (Sette 1994 тЙИ 500 nM CTL threshold + IEDB) and NetMHCpan-4.1 %Rank tiers (class I SB `< 0.5` / WB `< 2`, class II `< 2` / `< 10`, all strict `<`; Reynisson 2020), + peptide-length validity (class I **8тАУ14**, class II 13тАУ25). (2) **Matrix prediction**: BIMAS **product rule** (T┬╜ = const ┬╖ тИП coeffs, 180 coeffs + const, unlisted = 1.0; Parker 1994) and SMM **additive** rule `IC50 = 50000^(1тИТscore)` (Peters & Sette 2005 / IEDB log50k; 0тЖТ50000, 0.5тЖТ223.6068, 1тЖТ1 nM). (3) Ported **MHCflurry 2.0** pan-allele class-I NN (BLOSUM62 `left_pad_centered_right_pad` 45├Ч21 peptide + 37-residue allele pseudosequence 37├Ч21, `tanh` Dense `feedforward`/`with-skip-connections`, `to_ic50 = 50000^(1тИТx)`, geometric-mean ensemble; matches `mhcflurry` 2.1.5 to < 0.03 %). **Framework/packaging** тАФ trained matrices caller-supplied (BIMAS CGI defunct / Parker paywalled / IEDB non-commercial) and 80 MB ensemble not embedded (one member for CI + `LoadWeightPack`), explicitly analogized in-file to CIBERSORT LM22 of [[immune-infiltration-deconvolution]]. Downstream of neoantigen generation [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]] (ONCO-NEO-001), presentation-machinery sibling of [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (HLA LOH removes the platform); class I 8тАУ14 resolved vs NetMHCpan-4.1; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-mhc-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-informed-mrd-detection]] тАФ Oncology family, twenty-third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MRD-001): the liquid-biopsy **MRD calling / statistical-detection** layer that `depends_on` and reuses the Poisson quantification primitive [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] (ONCO-CTDNA-001). Two engines. (1) **Signatera positivity** (`DetectMRD`): tumor-informed workflow тАФ up to 16 WES-selected clonal somatic SNVs tracked in plasma cfDNA тАФ **MRD-positive iff тЙе 2 of the 16 tracked variants are detected** (Reinert 2019 / PMC9265001 Table 1; 0/1тЖТnegative, 2/3тЖТpositive), panel Poisson `p = 1 тИТ e^(тИТnfm)`, sensitivity scales with panel size (>8 markers at тЙд0.1% VAF, LoD 0.01% / specificity >99.5%; post-op ctDNA+ тЖТ HR 7.2 relapse), longitudinal `TrackVariantsOverTime` (per-timepoint + first-positive). (2) **INVAR GLRT** (Wan 2020 + INVAR2 verbatim): per-locus mixture `q = p┬╖g + e(1тИТp)`, EM ctDNA-fraction, `LR = logL(p╠В) тИТ logL(0)` (pure background тЖТ p╠ВтЙИ0/LRтЙИ0; AF/SNR-weighted, monotone), `IntegratedMutantAlleleFractionV2` background-subtracted depth-weighted, fragment-size-weighted GLRT (`EstimateInvarSignalWithSize`/`FragmentSizeProfile`/`InvarMolecule`; discrete `COUNT/TOTAL` default + opt-in Gaussian-KDE `FromKernelDensity`; flat P1==P0 тЖТ reduces to no-size), outlier suppression `SuppressOutlierLoci` (repolish binomial + Bonferroni), control-derived background `EstimateLocusBackground`/`PassesBothStrandsFilter`. Distinct from ONCO-CTDNA-001 (multi-variant verdict vs single-reporter probability); one flagged per-variant "detected"=тЙе1 alt read assumption (tunable); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-mrd-001-evidence]].
- [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] тАФ Oncology family, twenty-fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MSI-001): the **microsatellite-instability biomarker** тАФ MSI from unstable-loci fraction + status classification. Two inputs, two classifiers. (1) **Continuous MSI score** = `unstable loci / valid loci` (as %) with **MSI-High cutoff тЙе 20%** inclusive (MSIsensor2 niu-lab README verbatim; per-site **chi-square** tumor-vs-normal repeat-length test at **FDR 0.05**, score = "% sites with a somatic indel", Niu 2014; tumor-only mode unchanged; the original cohort's **3.5%** separation is dataset-specific, not the production cutoff) тЖТ classified **binary** MSI-H (тЙе20%) vs not-High only. (2) **Categorical Bethesda** marker-count over the validated 5-marker panel (BAT-25/BAT-26/D2S123/D5S346/D17S250): **0/5тЖТMSS ┬╖ 1/5тЖТMSI-L ┬╖ тЙе2/5тЖТMSI-H** (Boland 1998, cross-checked vs the 2004 revised-Bethesda тЙе40% / тЙе20%&<40% fraction form BJC 2014). Key modelling choice: **no MSI-L band is fabricated for the continuous score** тАФ the three-way MSS/MSI-L/MSI-H scheme applies only to the discrete marker count. Oracles 5/25тЖТ20%тЖТMSI-H(boundary) ┬╖ 4/25тЖТ16%тЖТnot-High ┬╖ 0/25тЖТ0%тЖТMSS-range; corner cases zero-valid-lociтЖТundefined(throws) ┬╖ unstable>valid/negativeтЖТthrows ┬╖ MSS-vs-MSI-L 1-marker low-confidence. An independent immunotherapy/mismatch-repair biomarker orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]], consumed by [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-msi-001-evidence]].
- [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]] тАФ Oncology family, twenty-fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-NEO-001): the **upstream partner** of the affinity gate [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] тАФ **neoantigen candidate peptide window generation** (`GenerateNeoantigenPeptides`). Given a somatic **missense SNV** at 1-based position `p` in a protein of length `L`, enumerate **every length-`k` window of the mutant protein that spans the mutated residue** (valid 0-based start `s тИИ [max(0, pтИТ1тИТk+1), min(pтИТ1, LтИТk)]`, count `= last тИТ first + 1`; an interior mutation gives exactly `k` windows per length), each paired with its matched **wild-type (germline)** peptide at the same coordinates + the mutation offset тАФ the mutant/WT **agretope** on which the differential agretopic index (DAI, Wells 2020 TESLA) is computed. Class I search lengths **8тАУ11** (pVACtools Hundal 2020; a 21-mer with the substitution centred = ProGeo-neo Li 2020's ┬▒10-flank construction contains exactly every overlapping 8тАУ11-mer; NetMHCpan 8тАУ14 / 9-mer-dominant Jurtz 2017 motivates enumerating 8тАУ11 not 9 alone). Oracles: interior **Y5C** on `MKTAYIAKQRSTVWLNDEFGH` тЖТ 5 windows per k = 8/9/10/11 тЖТ **20** candidates (each WT = mutant with `C`тЖТ`Y` at the offset); **terminal M1V** k = 9 тЖТ exactly 1 truncated window `VKTAYIAKQ`/`MKTAYIAKQ` offset 0; corner cases non-coding/synonymous тЖТ no peptide, length outside 8тАУ11 not enumerated, short-protein skips that `k`. **Missense-only** (frameshift/indel/fusion neopeptides out of scope, separate translation) and **binding affinity out of scope** (IC50/%Rank scoring caller-supplied via the downstream [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] ONCO-MHC-001 gate, whose resolved class I 8тАУ14 window propagates to this generator's default); presentation-platform sibling [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (HLA LOH removes the restricted allele). Two source-backed scoping assumptions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-neo-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] тАФ Oncology family, twenty-sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PHYLO-001): the **clonal-tree reconstruction** layer тАФ assemble per-cluster **cancer cell fractions (CCF)** into a rooted **clonal-evolution tree**, deciding parentтЖТchild descent via two per-sample CCF-ordering constraints from **LICHeE** (Popic 2015) and **PICTograph** (Zheng 2022): **lineage precedence** (ancestor CCF тЙе descendant CCF тИТ ╬╡ per sample, + presence pattern `u.CCF=0 тЗТ v.CCF=0`; LICHeE Eq. 2) and the **sum rule** (children CCF sum тЙд parent CCF + ╬╡ per node тАФ the cell-fraction **pigeonhole generalization**; LICHeE Eq. 5 / PICTograph sum condition тАФ what forces **branching vs nesting**), plus **trunk** (CCF-тЙИ1 root-path clusters = clonal) vs **branch** (subclones) identification. A **constraint-satisfaction / perfect-phylogeny** builder, **not** distance-based Neighbor-Joining / UPGMA. Oracles: linear NormalтЖТAтЖТBтЖТC (1.0/1.0/0.6/0.3, Trunk {A}); two-sample branching AтЖТ{B,C} (B 0.6/0.0, C 0.0/0.7 тАФ each private, absent in the other's sample, so mutually non-ancestral; sum under A per sample 0.6 & 0.7 тЙд 1.0); equal 0.6/0.6 siblings forced into a chain NormalтЖТAтЖТBтЖТC by the sum rule (0.6+0.6=1.2 > 1.0). Two reconstructed-tree **invariants** as oracles (ancestor CCF тЙе descendant per edge; per-node sum rule); emptyтЖТroot-only, single clusterтЖТtrunk. **Downstream of** the CCF clustering [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] (ONCO-CCF-001, which produces the clusters it orders), the structural counterpart of the per-mutation trunkтЖФclonal / branchтЖФsubclonal [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]], and the structure the heterogeneity metrics [[intratumor-heterogeneity-metrics]] summarize. Two source-consistent assumptions (deepest-valid-ancestor deterministic tie-break; default ╬╡=0 strict inequalities); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-phylo-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-ploidy-estimation-and-whole-genome-doubling]] тАФ Oncology family, twenty-seventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PLOIDY-001): two **post-hoc genome-state summaries** over already-called allele-specific segments (shared `AlleleSpecificSegment` = Major+Minor CN, not raw logR/BAF): (1) **average ploidy** `EstimatePloidy` = length-weighted mean total CN **╧И = ╬г(CN_i┬╖L_i)/╬г(L_i)** (Patchwork PMC4053982; n-scale Van Loo 2010, pure diploid тЖТ 2.0, >2.7n aneuploidy; CN 2/4/3 at 100/100/50 Mb тЖТ 3.0, genuinely length-weighted not plain segment mean); (2) **whole-genome doubling** `DetectWholeGenomeDoubling` = facets-suite `is_genome_doubled` / Bielski 2018 rule тАФ WGD iff **autosome-restricted fraction at major CN тЙе 2 strictly > 0.5** (`mcn = tcn тИТ lcn`; major not total CN, so all-1:1 тЖТ not doubled), denominator = **reference chromosome-size table** (`ReferenceGenome {GRCh38,GRCh37}`, UCSC hg38/hg19 Ensembl-verified, ╬гchr1тАУ22 = 2,875,001,522 / 2,881,033,286 bp) NOT supplied segments, autosomes only (sex chromosomes excluded); half+1тЖТtrue / exactly-halfтЖТfalse (strict) / 100 Mb ampтЖТ0.035 false / chrX-onlyтЖТfalse oracles, legacy `DetectWholeGenomeDoublingFromSuppliedLength` keeps the supplied-length denominator (60%тЖТtrue/50%тЖТfalse). **Distinct from** the joint grid fit [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (ONCO-ASCAT-001 *fits* ╧Б/╧И from raw logR/BAF; this *summarizes* ╧И post-segmentation), reads the same segment substrate as [[loss-of-heterozygosity-detection]] / [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]]. Two assumptions (input shape; resolved reference-genome WGD denominator); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ploidy-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] тАФ Oncology family, twenty-eighth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PURITY-001): a **standalone closed-form tumor-purity estimator** that inverts the **CNAqc expected-VAF generative model** `v = m┬╖╧А┬╖c/[2(1тИТ╧А)+╧А(n_A+n_B)]` (Antonello 2024) to recover purity ╧А from a somatic-SNV VAF + local allele-specific copy number: `EstimatePurityFromVAF` = the copy-neutral diploid heterozygous special case **╧А = 2┬╖VAF** (clonal c=1, het m=1, n_tot=2; VAF 0.30тЖТ0.60, band 0.55тАУ0.65тЖФVAF 0.275тАУ0.325, invariant 0тЙд╧АтЙд1) and `EstimatePurity` = the general inversion `╧А = 2v/(m┬╖c + 2v тИТ v┬╖n_tot)` recovering ╧А=1 on a 2:1 (n_tot=3) segment for both m=1 (v=1/3) and m=2 (v=2/3). The `2(1тИТ╧А)+╧А┬╖n_tot` denominator (normal diploid weighted 1тИТ╧А + tumour) is confirmed by **FACETS** (Shen & Seshan 2016) and inverted the other way by **ABSOLUTE** (Carter 2012). Corner cases: multiplicity ambiguity on amplified segments (two VAF peaks 1/3, 2/3 тАФ need CN state + m), subclonal c<1 depresses VAF (use **clonal** mutations or underestimate purity), purity <0.1 below detection, no informative variants тЖТ undefined. **`alternative_to`** the joint logR/BAF grid fit [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (ONCO-ASCAT-001 тАФ same purity scalar, different substrate + method), mutation-VAF counterpart to the ploidy-side [[tumor-ploidy-estimation-and-whole-genome-doubling]], shares the diploid `╧А=2┬╖VAF` inversion with [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]]. Two modelling-scope assumptions (copy-neutral-diploid default, median cross-variant aggregation); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-purity-001-evidence]].
- [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] тАФ Oncology family, twenty-ninth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-001): the wiki's first **mutational-signature** method тАФ the **SBS-96 trinucleotide context catalog**, the classification step that builds the 96-channel single-base-substitution spectrum downstream signature fitting decomposes. A **channel** = a substitution + its centred trinucleotide context: **6** subtypes named by the **pyrimidine** of the mutated WatsonтАУCrick pair (`C>A/C>G/C>T/T>A/T>C/T>G`) **├Ч 4** 5тА▓ bases **├Ч 4** 3тА▓ bases = **96**, labelled `5'[REF>ALT]3'` (COSMIC SBS96 + SigProfilerMatrixGenerator Bergstrom 2019 + Alexandrov 2013, identical 6├Ч4├Ч4 definition). The defining rule is **pyrimidine-strand folding**: a **purine (A/G) reference** base is reverse-complemented (context via AтЖФT/CтЖФG then reverse, plus the substitution) onto the pyrimidine strand before counting; a C/T reference classifies to itself, centre unchanged. Worked fold TGA/GтЖТT тЖТ revcomp TCA + G>TтЖТC>A тЖТ `T[C>A]A`; oracles A,C,A,AтЖТA[C>A]A ┬╖ G,T,C,AтЖТG[T>C]A ┬╖ A,A,T,AтЖТT[T>A]T. Catalog **partition** invariants: exactly 96 canonical keys, ╬г per-channel counts = number of classifiable SBS variants. Corner cases: purine-ref must fold (never counted directly), non-SBS variants (indels/DBS) excluded, non-ACGT context unclassifiable, ref==alt out of scope. **Catalog/classification only** тАФ the NMF/NNLS signature-exposure fitting against COSMIC reference signatures is a separate downstream concern. A somatic-mutation-spectrum biomarker orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] and the mismatch-repair [[microsatellite-instability-detection]]; one cosmetic label-rendering assumption; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-001-evidence]].
- [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] тАФ Oncology family, thirtieth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-002): the **downstream signature-deconvolution** partner of the catalog [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] (which it `depends_on`) тАФ decompose the 96-channel SBS spectrum into **signatures ├Ч exposures** two ways. **Supervised refit** by **non-negative least squares** `min_x тАЦS┬╖xтИТdтАЦтВВ┬▓, xтЙе0` (MutationalPatterns/deconstructSigs; Lawson-Hanson active-set тАФ clamp any would-be-negative coefficient to 0 and refit, S=[[1,1],[0,1]], d=[0,1]тЖТx=[0,0.5]; reconstruction `S┬╖x`, **cosine тЙе 0.95** quality gate, raw counts + proportion `x/╬гx` exposures). **Unsupervised de-novo extraction** by **NMF** `V тЙИ WH` (Lee & Seung multiplicative updates, **Frobenius** default + **KL/Poisson** enhancement, both **monotonically non-increasing**; Alexandrov blind-source-separation W=signatures/H=exposures; COSMIC **L1-normalize** each W column to 1). Shared **cosine similarity** `A┬╖B/(тАЦAтАЦтАЦBтАЦ)тИИ[0,1]` (identicalтЖТ1, orthogonalтЖТ0, [1,1]/[1,0]тЖТ1/тИЪ2, scale-invariant, **zero-normтЖТ0.0** by convention). **Rank selection** = Brunet-2004 **cophenetic correlation** (consensus of argmax-over-H connectivity matrices; rank-1 trivially 1.0) + SigProfiler **silhouette stability**; **reference matching** = greedy best-cosine to COSMIC. Sharp edges: NMF **non-convex тЖТ local minimum** (planted-truth + fixed-seed recovery only), **permutation/scale ambiguity**, ╬╡-guarded denominators. The NNLS refit and NMF extraction are `alternative_to` each other over the same `V тЙИ WH` model; the fitted exposure profile feeds the clinical-interpretation ONCO units, orthogonal to [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] / [[microsatellite-instability-detection]]; five modelling assumptions (Frobenius, seeded init, proportions, zero-cosine, consensus/silhouette/greedy matching); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-002-evidence]].
- [[signature-exposure-bootstrap-confidence-intervals]] тАФ Oncology family, thirty-first ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-003): the **signature-exposure uncertainty** layer over the NNLS refit [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] (which it `depends_on`) тАФ a **resample тЖТ refit тЖТ percentile** loop that turns the point-estimate exposure vector into a **per-signature confidence interval**. Resample the 96-channel catalog `R` times (default 1000; sigminer тЙе100), re-run the ONCO-SIG-002 **NNLS** `FitSignatures` per replicate, and report the **[2.5%, 97.5%] percentiles** (Efron 1979 percentile CI) read off the finite bootstrap sample by the **type-7** quantile (Hyndman & Fan 1996, `h=p┬╖(nтИТ1)`, R/NumPy default). **Two resampling schemes** differing only by whether total burden N is fixed: **multinomial** (sigminer `sample(...,prob=catalog/╬г)` = fixed-N multinomial(N,p), the byte-for-byte **default**) vs **Poisson** (Senkin 2021 MSA variant, each channel `Poisson(observedтВЦ)`, N unfixed, justified by the PoissonтЖФmultinomial conditional equivalence). The **discriminating** corner case is a single non-zero channel: multinomial **collapses deterministically** (width 0, point=mean=lower=upper) while **Poisson(╬╗>0) fluctuates** (variance=mean тЖТ positive width тАФ the reason the Poisson variant was added); plus N=0тЖТ[0,0] and R=1тЖТlower=upper=mean. Invariants LowerтЙдMeanтЙдUpper, exposures тЙе0 (NNLS), fixed-seed determinism; type-7 oracles [0,1,2,3,4]тЖТ0.1/2.0/3.9 and [2,4,6,8]тЖТ2.15/5.0/7.85. The uncertainty layer two steps above the [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] spectrum; two source-aligned assumptions (type-7 interpolation, fixed seed 42); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-003-evidence]].
- [[mutational-process-classification]] тАФ Oncology family, thirty-second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-004): the **aetiology-annotation** layer over the fit [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] (which it `depends_on`) тАФ turn per-signature **exposures** into a set of **active mutational processes** via **normalize тЖТ cutoff тЖТ map тЖТ aggregate**. Normalize to relative contributions `Wс╡в = exposureс╡в/╬гexposure` (deconstructSigs "weights between 0 and 1"); drop any `Wс╡в < 0.06` (the deconstructSigs `signature.cutoff = 0.06` / `weights[weights < signature.cutoff] <- 0`, **strict `<`** so exactly 0.06 is retained, empirically 1.4% false-negative rate); map each surviving COSMIC label to its **proposed aetiology** (SBS1/5тЖТ**Aging** clock-like, SBS2/13тЖТ**APOBEC**, SBS4тЖТ**Tobacco**, SBS7aтАУdтЖТ**UV**, SBS6/15/20/26тЖТ**MMR deficiency**; COSMIC + Alexandrov 2020); **sum** member contributions per process тЖТ **active-process set** + `argmax` **dominant process**. Worked oracle SBS2/13/1/4 = 50/30/15/5 (╬г=100) тЖТ APOBEC 0.80 (dominant) / Aging 0.15 / Tobacco 0 (SBS4 0.05 below cutoff). Corner cases: surviving mass can sum < 1 (rest "unknown"), several processes reported simultaneously, an unmapped or "Unknown"-aetiology label contributes to no process (SBS5's aetiology is literally "Unknown (clock-like)" yet grouped as Aging), ╬г=0 тЖТ no active/dominant process, custom `signature.cutoff` overridable. The interpretation layer answering "**which processes are active?**" one step above ONCO-SIG-002's "how much of each signature?" and ONCO-SIG-003's "how confident?"; orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] and mismatch-repair [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] (whose MMR signal SBS6/15/20/26 echo here as a signature-based read), feeds [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; two source-aligned assumptions (per-process summation, per-signature-cutoff-then-group); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-004-evidence]].
- [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] тАФ Oncology family, thirty-third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SOMATIC-001): the **foundational somatic SNV caller** at the head of the pipeline тАФ classify each candidate variant **Somatic / Germline / NotDetected** by comparing **tumor allele frequency `f_t`** against **matched-normal `f_n`** (`VAF = altReads/totalReads`). Strelka's somatic state `S = {(f_t,f_n): f_tтЙаf_n}` restricted to a **ref/ref normal genotype** (Saunders 2012; the raw somatic probability over-calls in LOH/CN regions) / Strelka2 continuous-VAF somatic-LOD+VAF comparison (Kim 2018). **Three configurable thresholds**: tumor **LoD f_t тЙе 0.05** (Yan 2021 WES 5% LoD, тЙд5% frequently sequencing errors тЖТ NotDetected), normal **"absent" ceiling f_n тЙд 0.01** (`normalVafThreshold`), f_n above ceiling with substantial f_t тЖТ **Germline** (Mutect2 germline filter, Benjamin 2019). Bounded monotone **somatic score `max(0, f_t тИТ f_n)` тИИ [0,1]** (a documented simplification, not a caller LOD). **Tumor-only mode**: no matched normal тЖТ Mutect2 `тДУ_n = 1`, tumor-only call; `FilterGermlineVariants` returns the somatic **subset** of input. Oracles A 0.25/0.00тЖТSomatic(0.25) ┬╖ B 0.48/0.50тЖТGermline(0) ┬╖ C 0.02тЖТNotDetected ┬╖ D CHIP-like 0.30/0.03тЖТGermline ┬╖ E tumor-only 0.20/(0/0)тЖТSomatic ┬╖ boundaries f_t=0.05 present / f_n=0.01 absent. The **upstream caller** whose raw call set the two pre-interpretation QC filters clean тАФ technical-artifact [[sequencing-artifact-detection]] + biological-origin [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] тАФ before the clinical-significance units; two flagged source-consistent assumptions (1% normal ceiling parameterized not invented; score a documented simplification); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-somatic-001-evidence]].
- [[chromothripsis-inference]] тАФ Oncology family, thirty-fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SV-001), and the wiki's **first complex-rearrangement / chromothripsis** method: a **region-level pattern classifier** that consumes a per-segment integer copy-number profile (+ breakpoints / a clustered-SV count) and classifies **Chromothripsis** vs **NotComplex** by the **Korbel & Campbell 2013** six hallmark criteria, computing two directly тАФ criterion B **oscillating copy-number states** (an oscillation = an adjacent-segment CN-state reversal; profile must alternate between тЙд3, canonically **two**, states) gated by the Magrangeas-2011 **тЙе10 first-pass oscillation screen**, the Cort├йs-Ciriano-2020 confidence tiers (**тЙе7** adjacent oscillating segments high / **4тАУ6** low / **<4** not-called), the **>60%** two-state fraction, and the **тЙе6 clustered intrachromosomal SV** burden floor; and criterion A **breakpoint clustering** via the exponential-null coefficient-of-variation flag (**CV>1**, exponential CV=1). Oracles `2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2`тЖТ10 two-stateтЖТChromothripsis ┬╖ `2,1,2,1,2,1`тЖТ5<10тЖТNotComplex ┬╖ `2,3,4,5,6,7` monotoneтЖТ0 oscillations/>2 statesтЖТNotComplex (progressive amplification/BFB тАФ the "clustering necessary but not sufficient" failure mode). **Consumes** the per-segment CN states of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) тАФ a pattern classifier over that profile, not a per-segment caller тАФ orthogonal to the single-junction [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] and the length-based [[focal-amplification-detection]], distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]].
